2a1(phal chen): / sems dpa'i tshogs chen po dri'i nang nas/ byang chub
2a2(phal chen): sems dpa' kha cig 'di snyam du sems te/ sangs rgyas bcom
2a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rna mas kyi sangs rgyas kyi nang de ji tsam zhigatu bsam
2a4(phal chen): gyis mi khyad/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi smon lam dang / 
3a1(phal chen): gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i
3a2(phal chen): gsung ni ji tsa zhig tu bsar gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes
3a3(phal chen): ni ji tsam zhig tu bsagyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs
3a4(phal chen): pa'i rnam par 'phrub pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgya sa bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
3a5(phal chen): chags pa mi mnga' ba'i rnam par spyod pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
3b1(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa ni ji tsam zhig tu bsam gyis mi khyab snyam pa dang / de nas bcom ldan 'das
3b2(phal chen): kyis byang chub sems dpa' de dag gi sems thugs kyis thugs su chud nas/ byang chub sems dpa' ud pi la'i snying
3b3(phal chen): po/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyis byin tu brlang so// sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi byin dang ldan par
3b4(phal chen): mdzad do// de bzhin no/ shegs pa'i 'od kyis snang bar mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi gzi brjid kyis
3b5(phal chen): yongasu rgyas par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi mi 'jig pa la rab tu bzhag go/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa
3b6(phal chen): khong du chud par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba nyid dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi yul rab tu rtogs par mdzad do// chags
4a1(phal chen): pa med pa'i rgyud 'byam klas pa la rab tu bzhag go// sangs rgyas thams cad gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa'i rigs rab tu rtogs
4a2(phal chen): par mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyi gnas brjod du med pa la rab tu bzhag pa mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' ut+pa la'i snying pos chos kyi dbyings
4a3(phal chen): la 'jug pa rig cing khong du chud pas/ chags pa med pa'i dbyings su bsgrubs pa'i yid dang / chos thams cad la bsgribs pa med par gnas pa'i byang chub samra
4a4(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa dang / kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang ldan pa'i yang dag par 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas thams ca da kyi rjes su song ba'i sangs rgyas
4a5(phal chen): blta ba dang / snying rje chen pos lta ba'i sems can thams cad yongs su sbyongs pa'i go cha chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yi dam dang / 
4a6(phal chen): spyod pa'i dkyil 'khor rgyun chad pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi ye shes mngon par sgrub pa skad cig gi cha shas la rnam por spyod pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid
4a7(phal chen): kyi sgo mthong ba mi zad pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa'i rnam pa/ gzungs thams cad kyis snang bar byas pa dang ldan pas sangs rgyas kyi mthus byang chub
4a8(phal chen): sems dpa' pad+mo'i snying po la 'di skad ces smraso// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni tshad med pa la rnam par spyod pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
4b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par 'phrul pa chen po la rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa thams cad la sku'i mtshan nyid thams cad
4b2(phal chen): rab tu brnyas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba ni ting 'dzin dang dgos pas sbyar ba'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa
4b3(phal chen): bzhi ni brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu ston pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la bsam gyis mi khyab par rnam par spyod pa'o// sangs rgyas bcoM
4b4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang dbyangs ni tshad med pa'o// // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings thug su chud pa ni brjod du med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
4b5(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba ni/ thams cad ma ngon par mkhyen pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis chos kyi dbyings thug su chud cing
4b6(phal chen): bstan pa ni bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos rnam pa bcu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
4b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gzugs kyi sku rnam par dag pa ni rnyog pa med par rgyud thad du byung bas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa'i spyan ni// chos thad mnyam pa nyid
4b8(phal chen): kyi spyan mngon par sangs rgyas pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chags pa med pa'i snyan ni/ 'gro ba thaMd kyi sgra bsgribs pa med par thugasu chud pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas
5a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shangs kyi skye mched ni/ sangs rgyas kyi mnga' thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sang+yas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ljags shin tu yangs pa
5a2(phal chen): ni chos kyi dbyings thams cad du gsung gi dbyangs rjesu 'gro bas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sang+yas bac+doMs rnams kyi sku'i chos nyid ni/ san thams cad ma lus pa'i sems kyi rnam pa de bzhin gsher pa mthong ba rnam par dmigs pas
5a3(phal chen): mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs rgyas bac+doMs rnams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni/ chos kyi sku dang mdad cing / dus gsum chags pa med par thug su chud cing rnam par dag pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sangs bcom ldan 'das rnam
5a4(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa bsgribs pa mi mnga' ba la rnam par spyod pa ni sang+yas kyi go 'phang dang / nor 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul mi zad pa yang dag par ston pas mtha' dang dpung med pa'o// sang+yas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
5a5(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thaMd rnam par dag pa ni/ brjod med pa'i rgyan byin gyis brlabs pas// sang+yas kyi zhing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa yang da/ ga par bstan te/ bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du nar dmigs par mdzad pas/ 
5a6(phal chen): mtha dang dpung med pa'o// sang+yas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thaMdade yong su rdzogs pa ni/ nor rol pa'i ye shes kyi chos yongasu rdzor te/ chos thaMd rdzogs par byang chub par bya ba la mtha' dang dpung
5a7(phal chen): med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gsher pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzon pa'i sang+yas rnams kyi chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dpung med pa'i sang+yas kyi chos rnam so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sang+yas bac+doMs rnams
5a8(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi skad cig gcig la ye kyis mdo bsgrubs pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/ skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thad du dga' ldan gyi gnas nas 'pho ba yongasasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la
5b1(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thad du byang chub sems dpa'i tshe longasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thad du mngon par 'byung ba yongasasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad byang / 
5b2(phal chen): chub kyi shing drang du bzhugs shing mngon par 'chang brgya pa yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig gyi khams thams cad du chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khaH
5b3(phal chen): thad du 'dul ba'i sems can yongasu smin pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du dus la bab par shes pas/ sang+yas bsnyen bskur ba yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad seMn ji ltar 'dul ba'i tshul
5b4(phal chen): bzhin du de bzhin gsher pa brjod med pa dang / sangs kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs pa yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten khams thad du rgyan sna tshogs dang / rgyan brjod du med pas de bzhin gshegs
5b5(phal chen): pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / thad mkhyen pa'i mdzod yongasu bstan pa dang / skad cig gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thang du rnam par dag pa gcig ma yin pa thaMd yong su bstan pa dang / skad cis
5b6(phal chen): gcig la 'jig rten gyi khams thang du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sang+yas skye ba thang du dbang po dang / brtson 'grus rnam pa tha dang byung ba dang / mos pa dang / spyod pa rnam pa tha dad pa byung ba la dus gsum gyi sangs kyi rgyud
5b7(phal chen): du mngon par 'tshang rgya ba yong su bstan pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bac+doMs nam gyis ng+yas kyi skad cig la les mngon par sgrub pa yang dag par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ 
5b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'bar ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mngon par 'tshang rgya ba ni de'i dus las mi
6a1(phal chen): 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi dge ba rnam par smin pa dang / rnam par ma smin pa mnyam pa nyid ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus
6a2(phal chen): la bab pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis yongasu smin pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams lung bstan pa ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
6a3(phal chen): 'das rnams kyis sems can gyi bsam pa'i rgyud du cho 'phrul yongs su bstan pa ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sems can mos pa ji lta bu dang ldan
6a4(phal chen): pa'i tshul bzhin du sku yongs su bstan pa ni dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams btang snyoms su bzhugs pa ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus
6a5(phal chen): la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams yul dang / grong dang grong rdal du gshegs pa ni/ de'i dus la mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
6a6(phal chen): 'das rnams dad pa ji lta bu dang ldan pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can yongs su 'dzin pa ni/ de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can kun nas nyon mongs pa
6a7(phal chen): dang ldan zhing gdul dka' ba la gzhan la ltos pa mi mnga' bar 'dul ba ni de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnaMs kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi
6a8(phal chen): khyab pas rnam par 'phrul pa bstan pa de'i dus las mi 'da' bas dus la bab pa yin/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi dus las mi 'da' ba'o// 
6b1(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'jig rten gyis khams thams cad ma lus par dkyil
6b2(phal chen): mo dkrung gcig gis rgyas par dgang ba dang / dus gcig tu sangs rgyas thams cad yongs su bstan pa dang / 'od zer gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar bya ba dang / sku gzugs gcig
6b3(phal chen): gi lus dang / gzugs thams cad yongasu bstan pa dang / gnas gcig na bzhugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par byon pa'i skur 'gyur ba dang / ye shes gcig rtogs pas chos thams cad la
6b4(phal chen): bsgribs pa med par 'gyur ba dang / thugs gcig bskyed pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus par rgyas par 'gengs pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi che ba nyid tshad med pa dang ldan pa'i gshegs stabs
6b5(phal chen): gcig gis de kho na nyid yang dag par bstan pa dang / dus gsum thams cad sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang gis rgyas par 'ged sa pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang ma 'dres par bzhugs shing
6b6(phal chen): 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sang+yas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang mi dmigs pa'i tshul gyis rgyud kyi tshul gyi gcig pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
6b7(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi yul dpe med cing bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ 
6b8(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ 'jug pa med pa'i chos thams cad la 'jug pas/ smon lam mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / lus med pa la lus mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad mi gnyis pa
7a1(phal chen): la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / sems can gyi mthar zhugs par bdag med pa la sems can 'dul ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams
7a2(phal chen): cad mtshan ma med pa la/ mtshan ma sna tshogs mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul ma skyes pa la 'jig rten gyi khams 'du ba dang / 'jig pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / yul thams
7a3(phal chen): cad mngon par 'du bya ba med pa la las kyi rnam par smin pa mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad brjod du med pa la chos kyi dbyings su gsung mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad kun nas
7a4(phal chen): nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang bas 'jug pa med pa la kun nas/ nyon mongs pa dang / rnam par byang ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes dang / chos thams cad ma skyes pa la skye ba dang / 'jig pa'i mtshan/ 
7a5(phal chen): nyid rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mngon par sgrub pa'i ye shes so//

7a8(phal chen): rab tu dbye ba thams cad la mkhas pa ni// sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi gzungs thams cad kyi khongasu chud pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi 'khor lo thams cad ni/ de bzhin gshegs

8a1(phal chen): / cad 'dul ba'i dbang gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gshegs pa ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// chos kyi dbyangs thugs

8a4(phal chen): ba dang / gdul bar bya ba don yod par tha dad pa yang dag par ma khyen pa thogs pa med pas bstan pa'i tshul du tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa bzhi 'byung ba ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam

8a6(phal chen): steng/ bsam gyis mi khyab cing thogs pa med pa'i tshul du 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin phra ba snyed kyi thabs kyis 'byung zhing / de bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku'i ba spu'i bu ga thams cad nas 'byung ba ni/

8a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed yongasu ston cing / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang / rang bzhin gyi lha lhub dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad cing / sems can rnam par 'dug ba
8b1(phal chen): thogs pa med la 'jig rten gyi khams de dag tu gtogs pa rnams la'ang mi bde ba dang // gnod pa med kyang rdul shin tu phra ba de yang yangs par ma byas// 'jig rten gyi khams de dag kyang chung bar ma byas par ji ltar gnas
8b2(phal chen): pa'i chos kyi dbyings kyang thugs su chud pa'i ye shes mnga' ba ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos bzod par dka' ba'o// mun pa med pa'i khams de bzhin gshegs pas mngon par sangs
8b3(phal chen): rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mun pa med cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la// sems can pha rol gyi bsgribs pa sna tshogs kyi gnas par sel na/ de la bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang
8b4(phal chen): ldan pa ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i chos la bzod par dka' ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rgya che ba'i
8b5(phal chen): chos bzod par dka' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'dir ga ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba rnam pa thams cad du/ kha na ma tho ba med cing / shin tu dag pa ste/ 
8b6(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi yang dag par bsgrubs pa bdag nyid che ba ni/ sngon gyi mtha' nas rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
8b7(phal chen): rnams kyi 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud du rigs dang ldan par 'byung ba'i bdag nyid che ba ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs par dag pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba
8b8(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rnam par shes pa la mi gnas pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ni/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thugs par gnas
9a1(phal chen): pas/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na mtho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan rnams ni dus gsum la mi gnas par rnam par spyod cing chos thams cad la rten pa
9a2(phal chen): yang dag par bcom pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dngos po rnam
9a3(phal chen): pa tha dad pa la rnam par gzhag pa gcig gis len pa med pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas btso
9a4(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mthar chos kyi dbyings la gnas pas mnyam pa'i bsod nams mi zad pa dang ldan pas/ mi zad pa'i bsod nams mnga' ba ste/ sangs rgyas bcom
9a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha nam tho ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gzugs dang / kha dog mtha'
9a6(phal chen): yas pas// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na/ sems cad 'dul ba'i dus dang dbang gis chags pa med par bzhugs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad kha na
9a7(phal chen): ma na pa sa so// sa rgya tsha ma nan 'a na mangs pa sa pas ba shAn yang rgyas dang sa / 
9b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongasu mya ngan las 'das nas bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa zhig lon yang mtshan gyi tshig zos pa tsam gyis bzhugs pa dang 'dra bar sems can rnams kyi
9b2(phal chen): yon shin tu sbyong zhing / mya ngan las 'das nas de srid kyi yun ring po 'das kyang / sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i yon zad par mi 'gyur bas/ sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid che ba ni// rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma tho ba
9b3(phal chen): med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyis khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa dag na bzhugs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams rgyang ring po na bzhugs kyang // 'jig
9b4(phal chen): rten gyi khams 'di na gnas pa'i sems can rnams kyis rje su dran par byas na/ sku mngon par ston pa mdzad pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad du kha na ma
9b5(phal chen): ba med cing shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bdag nyid che ba ni/ rnam pa thams cad kha na ma tho meng cing shin tu rnam par
9b6(phal chen): dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i skyes bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas parna ma ldan 'das rnams kyi shin tu rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi tshangs
9b7(phal chen): pa'i spyod pa rnam par dag po la/ sngon gyi smon lam gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i tshul khrims kyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs
9b8(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na/ sems can thams cad kyi nyon mongs pa sel bas/ shin tu rnam par dag pa ni yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gis shin tu rnam par dag
10a1(phal chen): pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'khor gyis shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sang+yas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni rigs rnam par dag pas/ shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ 
10a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan rnams ni gzugs kyi sku'i mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po rnam par dag pas// shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi sku rnyog pa med pas// shin tu rnam par
10a3(phal chen): dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi phung po bsgrubs pa med pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par
10a4(phal chen): thar pa thams cad la mthu chen po brnyes shing / pha rol tu phyin pa dam pa brnyes pas shin tu rnam par dag pa yin te/ kye rgyal ba 'i sras bcu po de dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi shin
10a5(phal chen): tu rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing dus thams cad du gnas pa ste/ 
10a6(phal chen): bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas rje su dran pa'i thob pa'i sems can rnams la dus thams cad du/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / sems can sems cad shes dang ldan pa rnams la/ dus thams cad du chos bstan pa dang / 
10a7(phal chen): sems can sangs rgyas la dad pa'i sems dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba dus thams cad bskyed pa dang / chos kyi skyon med par 'das pa'i sems can rnams dus thams cad du ye shes khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams
10a8(phal chen): cad du sangs rgyas kyi mdzad pa dus thams cad du rgyun mi 'chad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams 'jig rten gyi khams cad du dus thams cad du chags pa mi mnga' bar gshegs pa dang / son thams cad la thugs
10b1(phal chen): rje chen po dus thams cad du mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phru
10b2(phal chen): pa sna tshogs dus thams cad du thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i sangs rgyas dus thams cad du 'byung ba ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
10b3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi mdzad pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du 'byung zhing // dus thams cad gnas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs
10b4(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i tshul rnams ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni de de bzhin gshegs pa'i skus ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs
10b5(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las tshad med pa brnyes pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bco ma ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi spyan gyi yul mnga' bas
10b6(phal chen): shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba tshad med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi mar
10b7(phal chen): mngon par 'bebs pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yon tan dang / legs pa mang po mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
10b8(phal chen): 'das rnams ni sngon gyi mtha'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam dang khyad par mnga' bas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni phyi ma'i mtha'i mur 'gro ba thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrir
11a1(phal chen): las rgyun mi 'chad par sgrub pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi rigs thams cad ma lus pa'i sems dang spyod pa la ye shes rgya mtsho ma
11a2(phal chen): zad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thams cad mkhyen pa'i bsod nams zil gyis mi non pas ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag
11a3(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi ye shes rgya mtsho mi zad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul rnams te// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ pha rol
11a4(phal chen): tu phyin pa thams cad kyis mngon par byung ba 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ chos thams cad la mi mkhyen pa gang yang mi mnga' ba 'di ni// sangs rgyas bcom
11a5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad gas rje chen po dang ldan pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ang sa rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang stobs
11a6(phal chen): bcu tshad med pa dang ldan pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang bla na med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo rab tu bskor ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
11a7(phal chen): tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang sems can 'dul ba yang dag par zhugs pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ thams cad kyang 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du mngon
11a8(phal chen): par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lta ste/ 'dul ba'i sems can rnams 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mnga' ba 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul
11b1(phal chen): yin no// 'di lnga ste/ mi gnyis par yang dag par spyod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi chos la rab tu gzhol ba 'angan/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin no// 'di lnga ste ji ltar yongs su smin par gyur pa
11b2(phal chen): dang / dul bar gyur pa'i sems can rnams la/ sangs rgya ste yul mu med pas/ sangs rgyas kyi khongasu mya ngan las 'da' ba ston pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi tshul yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i
11b3(phal chen): sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi tshul lo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin
11b4(phal chen): tu bstan pa'i sgo rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can gyi khams shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
11b5(phal chen): ni sems can gyi spyod pa sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad kyi las dang / rnam par smin pa shin tu
11b6(phal chen): bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can thams cad la gdams ngag dang / man ngag shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
11b7(phal chen): ni sems can mtha' yas pa rnam par sbyong ba'i nan tan gyi sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la gdams ngag dang / man ngag gis yongs su
11b8(phal chen): gzhog pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa'i khyad par gyi smon lam rnam pa tha dad pas 'byung ba shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas
12a1(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus pa'i 'du ba dang / 'jig pa shin tu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
12a2(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa ni byang chub sems dpa'i bsam pa dang / mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongasu bstan pa'i sgor mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'jig rten gyi khams
12a3(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad du 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu rgyud pa ni bskal pa yangs pa de dang de dag tu bstan cing brjod pa dang / yongasu bshad pas/ sangs rgyas
12a4(phal chen): kyi ye shes thams cad khong du chud par bya ba'i sgor mtha' yas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa shin
12a5(phal chen): tu bstan pa'i sgo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas
12a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku yongasu bstan pa ni/ sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
12a7(phal chen): sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzad pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams len pa mdzin pa yang sems can rnams la sangs
12a8(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sa dang / chu dang / me dang / rlung gis kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byin gyi rlangs
12b1(phal chen): kyi yul dang mangs dmigs pa thams cad yul du mdzad pas kyang // sem+ba na rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin
12b2(phal chen): las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni// zhing la dmigs par mdzad pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par
12b3(phal chen): dag pas kyang / sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub po// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams mi gsung bar bzhugs pa yang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sbyang ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
12b4(phal chen): po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sems can rnams la sgrub po// / ma pa dwags pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni
12b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos te/ bcu gang zhe na/ smon lam chen po la rab tu brtan zhing smon lam zhig pa mi mnga' bas ji skad du gsung ba de lngar mdzad cing gnyis su mi gsu
12b6(phal chen): ba 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dang po'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i nur thug pa'i skal pa thams cad du/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la yon tan thas cad yongasasu rdzogs par mdzad par rab tu brtson zhing sgying lug pa mi mnga'
12b7(phal chen): ba'adi ni// sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gnyis pa'o// sems cad 'dul bar 'gyur ba gcig cig gzigs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par gshegs shing 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
12b8(phal chen): dugashegs pa la thags thogs med pa 'di ni// sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos gsum pa'o// zhe sdang ba'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa dang / ngang pa'i sems can rnams la thugs rje chen pos snyoms pa
13a1(phal chen): 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// gang gi tshe bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu yang dag par zhugs nas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon
13a2(phal chen): par sangs rgyas kyi bar du de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas su 'gyur ro snyam du/ byang chub kyi sems ma nyams pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos lnga pa'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba
13a3(phal chen): thams cad yang dag par sgrub cing thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yongasu sngobs 'jug gi/ 'jig rten pa'i rgyud la ma yin pa 'di ni// sems can gyi gtso ba'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rjesu sngon/ sangs rgyas
13a4(phal chen): kyis spyad pa'i sems su lus kyi las dang // ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis slob cing nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa sa thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du yong su sngob med pas/ bla na med pa yang dag
13a5(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par sangs rgyas pa 'di ni sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos bdun pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i sems rnam par dag cing // 'od gsal la dngas pa/ thams cad
13a6(phal chen): du snang zhing kun tu 'od 'byung ba// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la snang zhing thams cad du snyoms pas thams cad mkhyen pa nyid yongasasu rdzogs par byed pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos brgyad pa'o// 'jig rten pa'i bde
13a7(phal chen): thams cad yongasu spangs te// 'jig rten pa'i dga' ba thams cad la ma chags pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis gos pa med pa'i smon lam thams cad du mnyam pa nyid kyis 'jig rten thams cad bde ba thams cad dang ldan
13a8(phal chen): par byas te/ sdug bsngal dang / spros pa thams cad rab tu 'jom pa 'di ni/ sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos dgu pa'o// sdug bsngal gyi mi bde ba thams cad nyams su bab ste/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi don du dka' thub kyis
13b1(phal chen): shin gdungs kyang bla bar sems bskyed pas/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs yongs su bsrung ba dang ldan pa dang / stobs bcu'i sa'i bar du/ sangs rgyas kyi yul la mos pas mthar thug pa 'di ni// sems can gyi gtso bo'i
13b2(phal chen): chos bcu pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sems can gyi gtso bo'i chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam
13b3(phal chen): par spyod pa chags pa med pa rnams ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du gshegs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan
13b4(phal chen): 'das rnams ni// 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad na ba zhugs pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
13b5(phal chen): na bzhugs pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / bzhud pas chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das na mas ni// 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du chos ston pas
13b6(phal chen): chags pa mi ma' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dga' ldan gyi gnas na bzhugs kyang / chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin// sangs
13b7(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / da ltar byung ba'i mtha' la chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
13b8(phal chen): ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad tsam gyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor na bzhugs kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems dang / 
14a1(phal chen): dang spyod pa la gajigs shing thugs kyi skad cig gcig la/ cho 'drul chen po gsum gyis/ sems can rnam par 'dul yang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
14a2(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig gis kyang tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chen por rnam par spyod kyang chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can
14a3(phal chen): gyi khams 'bum klas pa ma lus pa thams cad du/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos ma lus pa thams cad kyi mthar thugs pa bsam gyis mi khyab par ston cing gsung yang / chags pa mi mnga' bar rnam par spyod pa yin te/ kye
14a4(phal chen): rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni// sadus bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa chags pa med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bucu po 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
14a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa rnams te/ bcug zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku / maN+Da na dang dpe byad bzang po sna tshogs kyis rnam par brgyan pa ni/ sangs rtsa
14a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung yan lag gi mchog dam pa drug cu dang ldan zhing yan lag lnga brgyas yongs su bzung ba dang / rgyan brgya
14a7(phal chen): stong du mas rab tu brgyan pa dang / dbyangs kyi yan lag mtha' yas mu med pas rnar dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi don dang / tshig dang / yi ge brjod du med pa'i yang brjod med pas rab tu tshim par mdzad
14a8(phal chen): pa dang / bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas seng ge'ing ro chen po spogs pa dang / 'jig pa med pa chen pos bsnyengs pa mi mnga' bar gyur pa dang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sem mdzang la grags cing bstsal te
14b1(phal chen): khang du chud par 'gyur ba dang / sems can bsam pa tha dad pa dang / dbang po tha dad pa rnams tshogs 'dul bar nye bar gnas pa 'din/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung gi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na mang pa'o// 
14b2(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi phrin las ni stobs bcus brgyan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzin chen po thams cad kyi me tog shin tu rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos ma 'dres pa bco brgyad kyi rgyan gyis shin tu
14b3(phal chen): brgyan cing bsgrubs pas chags pa med pa'i spyod yul dang ldan pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi la rab tu rten pa/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos gting med pa rab tu brnyes pa/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi rgyam
14b4(phal chen): gyur pa/ dus gsum gyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sa mas can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad skad cig gcigadang ldan pa'i shes rab kyi rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom
14b5(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs kyi rgyan mchogs dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od zer bye ba brjod med pa rab tu 'gyed pa mdzad de// 'od zer de dag re re la yang 'od zer
14b6(phal chen): gyi 'khor gyi dra ba brjod du med pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byed cing / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad mun pa med par ston pa sangs rgyas skye ba dang mi 'bral bas/ 
14b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog cing don yod pa/ sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pas gnas pa med pa rang bzhin rnam par dag cing kun tu snyoms par 'byung ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od zer
14b8(phal chen): kye rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams bzang mo 'dzum par ston na// zhal gyi sgo nas 'od zer kha dog sna tshogs kha dog dum dang ldan pa bye ba khwa khrag brgya spong brjod du med pa phyogs
15a1(phal chen): bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad snang bar byed pa/ sems can gyi khams tshad med grangs med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnam par ston pa/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
15a2(phal chen): byang chub tu rnam pa gzhan du mi 'gyur bar lung ston pa/ 'gro ba thams cad du shin tu gsal ba 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bzhad mo 'dzum pa bstan pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// 
15a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni tshad med pa ste/ bsgribs pa med pas rnam par dag pa chos thams cad chags pa med pa nyid kyi mthar thug pa/ mtha' dang dpung med pa'i chos kyi dbyings la gnas
15a4(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad dang ma 'dres pa/ 'jig rten thams cad ngang 'dzi ba med pa/ 'jig rten thams cad kyi de kho na nyid la yang dag par zhugs pa/ 'jig rten thams cad las gyen du 'phags
15a5(phal chen): pa/ 'jig rten las 'das pa'i chos kyis yang dag par spyod pa/ tshig gi lam dang bral ba/ brjod du med pa'i mthar phyin pa/ phung po dang / khams dang / skye mched dang bral ba ste/ 'di ni sangs
15a6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'od tshad med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du 'od ma 'dres shing
15a7(phal chen): rgyan dum dang ldan pa kha dog sna tshogs brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rgyan dang ldan pa/ 'od kyi snang ba kun tu thogs pa med cing thams cad du chags pa med pa 'od kyi dkyil 'khor bsgribs pa med pa tshad med pa'i
15a8(phal chen): mdzod du gyur pa 'od thams cad kyi 'byung gnas su gyur pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi 'od kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog mtha' yas
15b1(phal chen): pa mnga' ba ste/ kha dog yid du 'ong ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog 'od gsal ba mnga' ba'o// kha dog tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi bsam pa dang mos pa bzhin du rnam par dmigs
15b2(phal chen): pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// de ma yin pa'i kha dog gzhan khams gsum du gtogs pa thams cad zil gyis gnon pa'i kha dog mnga' ba'o// kha dog thams cad kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brnyes pas/ sangs rgyas bcom
15b3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni kha dog bla na med pa mnga' ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi kha dog rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge bas shin tu rnam par dag pa ste
15b4(phal chen): 'das pa dang / mabyon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs dge ba rin po che'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa la shin tu byung ba'o// chos nyid kyi rnam pa thams cad du khyad par yod pa dang / 
15b5(phal chen): khyad par med pa'i spod pas rnam par dag pa'i rgyan gyi ye shes skye ba/ thams cad nang du gtogs pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa/ 'i rigs bsgribs pa med pa'i rgyud rnam par dag pas 'jig rten gyi ma
15b6(phal chen): snyan pa thams cad kyis mi snyan pa porje du med pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang rgyud rnam par dag pa'i rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan
15b7(phal chen): 'das rnams ni byams pa chen po'i mthu dang / rang bzhin gyi rgyan mnga' ba ste/ shin tu dang ba yong su rtog pa'i rnyog pa mi mnga' ba sku'i phrin las yongs su gsal ba/ blta bas mi skyo bzugs shin tu rnam par bsal
15b8(phal chen): ba thugs rje chen po mnga' ba 'gro ba thams cad skyob pa yon gyi gnas kyi dam pa bla na med pa yong su 'dzin pa'i nang na thugs brtsi ba can phan par mdzad pa/ sems can thams cad kyi don du ye shes chen po bya
16a1(phal chen): gyis brlabs te/ bsod nams chen pos yong su 'phags pa 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi zhing du gyur pa/ sems can rnams kyi yon tan dang / ye shes kyi phung po thams cad rnam
16a2(phal chen): par 'phel bar mdzad pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi byams pa chen po dang / thugs rje chen po'i mthar thugs pa'i bsod nams kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ 
16a3(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi rgyan mchog dam pa bla na med pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos
16a4(phal chen): rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la mnga' ba dang / chos thams cad la snang bar mdzad pa'i mad sbyar bas/ tshig dang yi ge mtha' yas pa la
16a5(phal chen): thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i spobs pa mnga' ba dang / chos thams cadam lus par yongs su rjod pas mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sang sa rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos
16a6(phal chen): mnga' sbyar ba'i chos dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can ji ltar yongasu smin pa dang / smon lam ji ltar btab pa'i tshul bzhin du 'dul ba la thogs pa mi mdangs sa 9/ 'di ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen
16a7(phal chen): pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad sems can gcig la'ang gnod pa med par rnam pa drug la spyod pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams
16a8(phal chen): rkyen rnam par bkod pa grangs med tshang med pa dang ldan pa/ nam pa'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa thams cad gcig nas gcig tu 'phang ba dang / gcig nas cig tu gzhug pa dang / gcig nas gcig tu bsdu ba dang / gcig nas gas
16b1(phal chen): tu bsre ba 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang / gzhan dag gzhan dang gzhan gyi phyogasu rab tu bzhag kyang / sems can gyi khams rnams 'khor cing rmongs par mi 'gyur la the tsom du mi 'gyur bar mdzad pas// mnga' cha ba ste/ 'di
16b2(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mngang sgyur ba'i chos gsum pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad byin gyis rlob pa'i ye shes kyis 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyan phan tshun du byan
16b3(phal chen): gyis brlab pa dang / thugs skad cig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rgyan yang dag par bstan pa dang / bskal pa grangs med par brjod kyang yi ge shin tu bstan pa zad mi shes pa dang / 'jig rter gyi khams ma lus pa
16b4(phal chen): thams cad rgyan tha~Md kyis rnam par brgyan pa dang / mi mthun pa med cing nye bar nyon mongs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig tu yod su 'du bar sangs rgyas kyi zhing rnam par dag pa thams cad byin gyis
16b5(phal chen): brlab pa la mnga' chab ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi 'dul ba'i
16b6(phal chen): sems can gzigs na sems can gcig gi don du bskal pa brjod med pa'i yang brjod med par skyil mo krung gcig gis bzhugs na yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku la mi bde ba mi mnga' zhing thugs la mi dade ba mi mangs ste gang zag pa
16b7(phal chen): yang mi bsngal bas 'dul ba'i dus las mi 'da' ba dang // gang zag gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du rim pa rim pas 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i sku tsha la mnga' bar byin gyis brlabs ste/ 
16b8(phal chen): bzhugs kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la skyob mi mnga' ba ste/ de ltar sems can gyi khams thams cad mthar gyis rim pas/ sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba'i gang zag gi don du yongs sbyong ba mdzad pa la mnga' cha / 
17a1(phal chen): 'dini sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyang ba'i chos lnga pa'o// ba cwa bcom ldan 'das rnams na// 'dzag rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du yang dag par gsol
17a2(phal chen): ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i bzhud pas 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du bzhud pa la thags thogs mi mnga' ba dang / phyogs bcu'i chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud rgya mtsho 'byam klas
17a3(phal chen): pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud thams cad du thugs skad cig gcig dang ldan pas bzhud par byin gyis rlob cing chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa khong du chud par bya bas/ chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med pa rab tu bskor ba la
17a4(phal chen): mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bco ma ldan 'das rnams ni 'dul ba'i sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi don
17a5(phal chen): du thugs skad cig re re la bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang / chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar mnga' che ba ste/ de la chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'ang gang yang med la mngon par sangs
17a6(phal chen): be'ang med de/ mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ba med kyang / slob pa'i sa la gnas shing mngon par 'tshang rgya bar yang mi brjod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang bsgribs pa med pa rtogs par thug su
17a7(phal chen): tshud pas sems can thams cad 'dul ba'i don du ye shes tshad med pa'i tshul gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chen po'i yul yongs su rgyun mi gcod pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
17a8(phal chen): kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi spyan gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de snyan gyi skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad// 
17b1(phal chen): san gyi skye mched kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang bsgrub pa de shangs kyi skye mched kyis yong du grub pa mdzad do// shangs kyi skye mched kyi rangs rgyas kyi drin las gang sgrub pa de ljags kyi skye mched kyis yongs su grub pa
17b2(phal chen): mdzad do// ljags kyi skye mched kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de ni sku'i skye mched kyis yongasu grub par mdzad do// sku'i skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de thugs kyi skye mched kyis yongasu
17b3(phal chen): grub par mdzad do// thugs kyi skye mched kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gang sgrub pa de 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi dmigs pa 'jig rten pa dang // 'jig rten las 'das pa sna tshogs rnam par phye ba thams cad
17b4(phal chen): du grub par mdzad do// de bzhin du dmigs pa thams cad re re yang snrel zhing sgrub pas sangs rgyas kyi phrin las sgrub pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga'
17b5(phal chen): pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan/ 'das rnams ni rang gi sku'i ba spu'i bu gcig gi nang du semasacan gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad gzung bar mdzad cing khong su chud par
17b6(phal chen): mdzad pa dang // sems can re re zhing yang lus sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa tsam du yangs par mdzad kyang / sems can de dag la gnod pa dang / mi bde bar mi 'gyur ba dang / de dag du yang sems can re re zhing 'dzag rten
17b7(phal chen): gyi khams gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pas bskal pa grangs med pa zad par gnas par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams grangs med par gom pa gcig gis phyin pas 'jig rten gyi khams de dag du sangs rgyas byung ba rnams
17b8(phal chen): kyi spyan sngar 'gro bar bya ba dang / sangs rgyas de dag byung ba'i tshe yang brjod du med pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud dang gling de dag na sems can gyi gtso bos brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo
18a1(phal chen): bskor bar bya ba dang / ba spu'i bu ga de nas sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / sems can gcig nas gcig tu brgyud
18a2(phal chen): pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa 'byung bar bya ba dang / chos kyi 'khor lo gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor bar bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa
18a3(phal chen): brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa shin tu bstan par bya ba dang / 'das pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa dang / ma 'ongs pa gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa brjod med pa dang / da ltar byung ba gcig nas gca
18a4(phal chen): tu brgyud pa brjod du med pa yongasasu brjod par bya ba dang / namakha'i dbying ngas mtha' dang dpung med par bstan pa kun tu mtshams med par sems can thams cad 'ong zhing 'gro ba dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad
18a5(phal chen): du 'dod pa'i longs spyod rgya chen po bgegs med pa thams cad 'byung bar bya ba la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos dgu pa'o
18a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad pad+mo'i rgyan chen pos brgyan pa'i seng ge'i khri pad+mo'i snying po can la de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi chos kyi dbyings tshad med pa thams cad khyab pa'i skus
18a7(phal chen): byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par sangs rgyas te/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu bstan pa mdzad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi ji lta bar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu
18a8(phal chen): phra ba snyed kyi sems can gyi gtso bo thams cad kyang de bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig ma re re'i byin gyis brlabs kyis brlabs pa dang / dgongs pa skad cig la ji lta ba bzhin du dgongs pa skad cig thams cad la'ang pad+mo'i rgyud kyis/ 
18b1(phal chen): yongasu dag par mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya ba dang / de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings thams cad ma lus pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med gang dag pa rgyan sna tshogs dang ldan pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams su dmigs pa rnam pasna
18b2(phal chen): tshogs dang ldan pa'i zhing rnam par dag pa 'byam klas pa brjod du med pa mtshan nyid tha dad pa'i rgyud tshad med cing 'byam klas pa dus kyi rgyud grangs med pa dang ldan pa// bstan pa ma 'dres pa dang ldan pa/ blo tshad med pa dang / mos
18b3(phal chen): pa shin tu yangs pa dang ldan pa/ mtshan nyid sna tshogs kyi gnas med pa/ mtshan nyid bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang ldan pa// tshad med pa thams cad dgongs pa skad cig ma las dgongs pa skad ma gcig gis thams cad yod
18b4(phal chen): su bstan kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ched du sgrub pa mi mdzad pa la mnga' che ba ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sgyur ba'i chos bcu pa'o// 
18b5(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam/ sa kyi sangs rgyas kyi mnga' chen pos mnga' sbyar ba'i chos so// / kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
18b6(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yongs su rdzogs pa tshad med pa bsam gyis mo khyab pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na mtshan re re zhing bsod nams rgya ba'i mtshan yongasu dag par 'gyur ba 'di ni yong su rdzogs pa dang po ste/ des
18b7(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sangs rgyas kyi chos rnams yong su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// dge ba'i rtsa ba thams
18b8(phal chen): cad yongs su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas phun sum tshogs pa'i spyod pa yong su dag pa rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan
19a1(phal chen): 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// sems can yong su smin par bya ba dang / 'dul ba yong su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// 
19a2(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi mnga' 'gro ba thams cad kyis zil gyis mnon pa yongasu rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// zhing yong su dag par bya ba yong su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom
19a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yong su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po dang / gzugs
19a4(phal chen): kyi sku blta na don yod par yong su rdzogs pas sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// de bzhin ga shegs pa thams cad dang mnyam pa nyid yongs su rdzogs pas/ sangs rgyas
19a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ste sangs rgya/ sa kyi phrin las thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad nas yongasu mya ngan las 'da'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs
19a6(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos yong su rdzogs pa tshad mod bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// kye rtsa ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thabs mkhas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas
19a7(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad byin gyis brlabs pa med cing spros pa thams cad med par yang / thug su chud la dge ba'i sgo nas sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs kyang shin tu ston cing brjod de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
19a8(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dang po'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad la gzigs pa med cing phan tshun du mkhyen pa med do// ma bcings ma grol ba dang / gzungs pa med cing bsags
19b1(phal chen): pa mang de yong su rdzogs pa med par yang thug su chung la sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mang 'dam pa yang brnyes te/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams chos thams cad la mang 'gyur ba de 'ang drag pa de kho na nying mnor brnam pa
19b2(phal chen): gzhan du mi 'gyur ba dang / chos thams cad bdag gi med cing yongs su 'dzin pa med la de kho na nyid kyi mtha' las rnam par mi 'da' yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mnga' chen pos chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang ba
19b3(phal chen): la'ang rab tu mkhyen pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gnyis pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mtshan ma'i mtha' thams cad mi mnga' ste// mtshan ma thams cad dang mi
19b4(phal chen): 'grogs shing / mtshan ma'i mngon par shes pa thams cad dang / ma 'dras da la de'i rang bzhin du ngo bo nyid med pa dang / ji ltar ngo bo nyid med pa'i sgra'i tshul thams cang thug su chud kyang gzugs kyi mtshan ma'i sku gzugs
19b5(phal chen): rnam par dag pa grangs med pa dang / zhing gi mtshan ma dang / rnam par spyod pa'i mtshan ma zad mi shes pa rnam pa sna tshogs yang dag par bstan cing bshad pa'i ye shes kyi phung po mun pa med pa 'gro ba thams cad
19b6(phal chen): kyi sgron ma chen por gyur pas mun pa med pa'i snang ba ston pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa gsum pa'o// chags pa med pa'i mtha' ni sngon gyi mtha' yang ma yin/ phyi ma'i
19b7(phal chen): mtha' yang ma yin/ da ltar byung ba yang ma yin te/ chos kyi dbyings su gnas pa ni 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba yang ma yin pas/ de bzhin nyid kyi mtshan nyid kyis 'byung ba med kyang sangs rgyas 'byung ba rnams kyi
19b8(phal chen): rigs tshad med pa'i phyir shin tu bstan pa brjod du med pas 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bskye ba yang rab tu brjod cing kun tu gzigs pa'i sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis de bzhin du gzigs pa 'di na
20a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bzhi pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sku'i phrin las dang / gsung gi phrin las dang / thugs kyi phrin lnga
20a2(phal chen): kye mngon par 'du mdzad pa yang mi mnga' la yongasu blang ba mi mnga' bas bzhugs shing rnam par phye ba med pa'i mthar thugs pa ste/ dor ba med pa'i chos kyi gnas kyi pha rol tu phyin la bgrang ba'i tshul las rnam par 'das kyang tshul
20a3(phal chen): grangs med pa'i mdzod gyur cing // bgrang ba dang mngon par sgrub pa mtha' yas pa dang / 'jig rten pa dang 'jig rten las 'das pa rnam pa sna tshogs tha dad pa'i grangs kyi tshul thugasu chud pa ye shes bsgribs pa med pas gzigs pa
20a4(phal chen): rnam te/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can gdul ba rnam par dmigs pa la rdzu 'phrul sna tshogs tshad med mu med par mngon par sgrub pa mdzad pa 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
20a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa lnga pa'o// chos thams cad lta ba med pas// tha mi dad pa dang / bye brag med pa dang / 'byung ba med pa dang / mtshan nyid med pa dang / sna tshogs med pa dang / blang ba med pa dang / dor
20a6(phal chen): ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med par rab tu mkhyen kyang chos kyi rgyud shin tu nges pa yang dag par sgrub cing 'jig rten gyi tshul dang 'gal ba med pa dang / rang bzhin med pa yang yang dag par gzigs pas thams cad mkhyen pa
20a7(phal chen): thams cad gzigs pa mkhyen par bya ba thams cad ma lus par gzigs pas chos la mnga' sgyur ba thams cad kyang rab tu ston la/ de bzhin nyid kyi rang bzhin las kyang mi nyams pa 'di ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
20a8(phal chen): rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thug su chud pa'i rnam pa gcig gis gzhan dang gzhan mkhyen par bya ba/ chos de'i skyon med pa las rnam par ma 'das pa gnas
20b1(phal chen): pa med pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa mnyam pa nyid kyi chos skyon med pas dus thams cad du gnas pa rab tu mkhyen te/ de la yang nyi ma gcig gam// zla ba phye dam/ lo gcig gam/ lo brgya'am bskal pa 'jig
20b2(phal chen): pa dang / 'du bas rje su bsnyag pa dang / phyir phyogs pa mi mnga' bar dus tshad med pa dang / nyi ma gcig dang / yud tsam gcig gi dus dang / snga dro nas nyi ma phyed kyi dus dang / phyi dro nas snga dro'i dus dang / nyi ma gung
20b3(phal chen): nas phyi dro'i dus dang / nyi ma 'grang ba'i dus dang / nyi ma bdun dang / zla ba phye gyi dus dang / zla ba dang / lo dang / lo brgya'i dus dang / bskal pa gcig gi dus dang / tshad med grangs med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i dus nas/ phyi ma'i
20b4(phal chen): mtha'i mur thugs pa'i dus su chos bstan pa dang / chos kyi 'khor lo thogs pa med cing phyir mi ldog/ rgyun chad par mi 'gyur/ bral ba dar mi 'gyur/ bar chad par mi 'gyur med par mi 'gyur// 'jig par
20b5(phal chen): mi 'gyur/ g.yo bar mi 'gyur/ ring du mi 'gyur/ 'khor de na gan sa pa nyi du yang rgyun chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa bdun
20b6(phal chen): pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad rtag tu dus la bab par bzhugs pa ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mi 'jig pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad
20b7(phal chen): pa yang dag par mkhyen pa grangs med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshad med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa zad mi shes pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa thogs pa med pa mang
20b8(phal chen): ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mtha' yas pa mnga' ba'o// thun mong ma yin pa'i tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mthar thug pa med pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang
21a1(phal chen): dag par mkhyen pa de khon dang ldan pa mnga' ba'o// tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa tshig gi tshul thams cad rab tu rtogs pa mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa mnga'
21a2(phal chen): ba'o// bsam pa dang mos pa dang / dbang po ji lta ba bzhin du/ chos kyi tshul dang / rnam grangs tshul ji ltar rnam par dkod pa bzhin dus mtsham pa med par ston te/ mdo sde bye ba khrag khrig brjod du med pa'i yang rjod
21a3(phal chen): pa med pa rnams mdo sde de dang de la thog ma dang / tha ma dang / dpung gi tshul gyis yang dag par ston te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ad
21a4(phal chen): rnams ni ming med kyang / ming dang rigs su byung ba'i chos thams cad tshig dang / yi ges shin tu dbyangs pa'i dbyings mngon par sangs rgyas da pa ste/ ming 'das pa ma yin pa dang / ming ma 'ongs pa ma yin pa dang / 
21a5(phal chen): ming da ltar byung ba ma yin pa dang / ming sems can ma yin pa dang / ming zhing ma yin pa dang / ming chos ma yin pa dang / ming yon tan ma yin pa dang / ming byang chub sems dpa' ma yin pa dang / ming
21a6(phal chen): sangs rgyas ma yin pa dang / ming grangs ma yin pa dang / ming grangs med pa ma yin pa dang / ming skye ba ma yin pa dang / ming 'gag pa ma yin pa dang / ming med pa ma yin pa dang / ming yod pa ma yin pa dang / ming gcig pa ma/ 
21a7(phal chen): yin pa dang / ming tha dad pa ma yin pa dang / ming thams cad ma yin pa dang / chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis brjod med pa dang / phyogs med pa dang / brda med pa dang / tshig gi lam med pa dang / sgra dang bral ba/ sgra'i rnam pa/ 
21a8(phal chen): thams cad mi 'byung ba yong su bsgrubs pa med pa/ byas pa dang rnam par byas pa med pa/ rnam pa gcig ma yin pa/ rnam pa mang po ma yin pa yang thug su chud la brjod pa dang / spyad pa thams cad la yang pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog
21b1(phal chen): brnyes pa dag snga/ rnam par rtog pa'i yul mi mnga' ba dag go// mngon par 'du mdzad pa med pa la rab tu brtson pa dag go// rtog pa dang kun tu rtog pa dang yongs su rtog pa 'gag pa dag go// spyod pa thas cad la mi gnas
21b2(phal chen): par spyod pa dag ste/ 'di ni sangs bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa dgu pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi gzugs ma skyes pa rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ tshor ba'i
21b3(phal chen): spros pa med pa dang / 'du shes kyi grangs med pa dang / 'du byed kun tu rgyu ba med pa dang / rnam par shes pa nye bar len pa med pa dang / rang bzhin gyis zhi bar rab tu mkhyen te/ chos thams cad skye mched kyi rgyud med pa dang / khams
21b4(phal chen): rnams mi darigs pa dang / chos thams cad mi 'jigs pa dang / chos thams cad bskyed du med cing rang bzhin gyis na mkha' lta bu dang / chos thams cad dben pa dang / las med pa dang / rnam par smin
21b5(phal chen): pa med pa dang / spyod pas 'byung ba med pa dang / ma grub pa dang / ma 'byung ba dang / grangs kyi mi brjod pa dang / yod pa ma yin pa dang / med pa ma yin pa dang / ma skyes pa dang / ma 'gags pa dang / kun nas
21b6(phal chen): nyon mongs pa red pa dang / rnam par byang ba ma pa dang / skyor med pa dang / gnas med pa dang / yongs su gnas pa med pa dang / yongs su smin par byas pa med pa dang / rnam par btul ba med pa dang / sems can med pa dang / 
21b7(phal chen): sems can med pa ma yin pa dang / srog med pa dang / srog med pa ma yin pa dang / rkyen med pa dang / rkyen med pa ma yin pa dang / rten pa med pa dang / rtswa med pa ma yin par chos thams cad thug su chud kyang chos kyi dbyings
21b8(phal chen): thams cad shin du bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i dam pa brnyas pa dag ste/ nges pa dang ma nges pa dang / log par nges pa'i phung po gsum rnam par dgod pa rnams la stobs bcus thug su chud pa'i ye shes mi 'jigs pa
22a1(phal chen): bzhis rnam par dadag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi dul chen po dang ldan pas seng ga'i sgra klog pa 'dzin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyisangs rgyas kyi thabs ma thab bcung ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras
22a2(phal chen): bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi thabs mkhas pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgya chen po
22a3(phal chen): tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten dang / 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas
22a4(phal chen): thams cad kyis 'jug par mi nus pa'o// bcu gang zhe na/ phyogs bcu'i na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa'i chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du dga' ldan
22a5(phal chen): du skye ba bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mu med pa dag la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ kha dog tshad med pa gzi brjid tshad med pa/ snang ba tshad med pa/ dbyangs tshad med pa
22a6(phal chen): dbyangs kyi yan lag rnam par dag pa tshad med pa/ gsung brjod pas rnam par dmigs pa tshad med pa'i ting 'dzin tshad med pa la spyod pa/ shes rab dang / ye shes yul tshad med pa mnga' ba'i rnams lnga dang bcas pa'i 'jig
22a7(phal chen): rngan la phan 'dog pa mdzad de/ bdud dang bcas pa/ tshangs pa dang bcas pa/ dge sbyong dang bram ze'i skye dgu dang bcas pa/ lha dang mi dang lha ma yin du bcas pa'i 'jig rten la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// byams pa
22a8(phal chen): chen po'i spyod yul thogs pa med pa dang / thabs thugs rje chen por sgo'i mthar zhugs pas sems can la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// bsod nams kyi stobs dang / mang 'a phun su mtshogs pa dang / dbang po rnam par
22b1(phal chen): spyad pa dang / cang shes kyi sems yong su dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa sna tshogs rnams par dag pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad do// theg pa chen po
22b2(phal chen): yong su rdzogs par bya bas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs par mdzad do// 'gro ba thams cad gdon pas kyang sems can rnams la phan 'dogs pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi
22b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi phrin las dang po'o// dga' ldan gyi pho brang nas 'phos pa med kyang yum gyi skur gshegs shing / byang chub sems dpa'i sku tha ma skye bar bstan pa// sgyu ma lta bur yongs su spyod pa sprul pa lta bu'i ting 'dzin
22b4(phal chen): gyi mthar thug pa/ mig yor lta bur rnam par dmigs pa/ namakha'i yu'ang yin par khyab pa/ bzhed pa bzhin du skye yang chags pa mi mnga' ba/ smig rgyu ba lta bur bstan pa// nyon mongs pa med pa'i
22b5(phal chen): chos la yang dag par gzhol ba// gnas med pa'i ye shes la gnas pa rang bzhin gyis 'dod chags dang bral bas rnam pa dag pa/ rgyan shin tu rgya che ba'i mdzod kyis sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
22b6(phal chen): mdzad do// khang pa brtsegs pa rin po che las byas pa'i pho brang chen po rin po che'i rgyan mang po ldan la bzhugs pas kyang sang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
22b7(phal chen): mdzad do// yid la bya ba byin gyis brlabs chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rnam par 'phrul pa'i mdzod chen po yang dag par bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ye shes kyi
22b8(phal chen): nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen pos kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yum sku skyed pa'i sku na bzhugs pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi spyod yul chen po brnyas pas kyang sadra
23a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'jig rten byin du brlabs pa mtha' yas pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ting 'dzin chen po grangs med pa la rnam par
23a2(phal chen): spod cing snyoms par 'jug pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// ting 'dzin las bzhengs pa de dang de dag gis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// spong pa'i thog ma la yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po'i
23a3(phal chen): mthar thugs pa'i bar du thog ma dang / dbus dang tha ma'i tshul gyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sa 'di la gnyis su med pa thams cad mthar phyin par byas nas tha mar 'jig rten gyi grangs kyis skye ba yongasu
23a4(phal chen): ston te/ skyabs kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// gzhon nur gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// byang chub sems dpa
23a5(phal chen): gyur pas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mngon par 'byung bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mngon par 'tshang rgyabs kyang
23a6(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang 'jig rten thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// thabs mkhas pa sna tshogs kyis kyang 'jig rten sna tshogs
23a7(phal chen): 'jig rten tshad med pa 'jig rten tu mtha' yas pa/ phyogs kyi dra ba'i rgyud dang / rigs thams cad kyi 'jig rten ma lus pa thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// zhing gi rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten
23a8(phal chen): du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// las tsa rnam par rlon pa ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du rangs rgyas kyi drin las mdza da // sems can gyi rgyung ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// skye ba
23b1(phal chen): dang shi 'pho ba'i rgyud ma lus pa'i 'jig rten du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sprul pa chen po'i rgyud dang / sangs rgyas kyi rigs dang / chos dran pa'i sgo'i 'khor los kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// 
23b2(phal chen): 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gnyis pa'o// dge bar spyod pa'i las rnam par dag cing / gdung rabs thams cad du ye shes kyi tshul rnam par dag pas sku tsher rgyud kyi tshul dang ldan
23b3(phal chen): pa/ sems can thams cad gdul ba thug su chud pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongs su rdzogs par mdzad cing btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang na bzhugs pa ston kyang // sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'dod chags dang bral ba'i tshul
23b4(phal chen): gyi gnas la bzhugs pa rnams sgra dang / tshig thams cad dang bral par brtags pas dngos po thams cad dngos po med pa las byung da bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / dngos po thams cad shes pa la gtsu
23b5(phal chen): par bya ba dang / tshul khrims thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa ni da kyi mthar thugs par yongs su rdzogs par bya ba dang / snying rje chen pos 'gro ba mu med pa la rnam par blta bar bya ba dang / byam
23b6(phal chen): pa chen pos sems can med pa'i yul la rab tu rtog par bya ba dang / dga' ba chen pos 'jig rten brjod du med par khong du chud par bya ba dang / btang snyoms chen pos sems la dbang sgyur ba la gnas par bya ba dang / 
23b7(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan gyis rang yongs su rgyas par byed par bya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi lus ma yus pa mngon par sgrub par bya ba dang / thams cad du gnas med pa'i lus yongasu rdzogs par bya ba dang / 
23b8(phal chen): 'khor thams cad rnam par dag par nan tan du byed par bya ba dang / chos bstan pa rnam par brjod pa rab tu brjod par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi dngos po la smod par bya ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi nyes pa la rtog par
24a1(phal chen): pa mdzad cing spyod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa bas rnam par smin pa yang dag par bstan pa dang / ji lngar bkod pa'i rdul du sems can 'dul ba dang / yongs su ma ston pa'i sems can yong su smin par
24a2(phal chen): bya ba dang / yongs su smin pa rnams tshul bzhin du gdul ba dang / grangs med pa'i thabs mkhas pa mngon par sgrub pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las phyir mi ldog pa yongs su bstan pa dang / sgo sna tshogs nas chos kyi spyod pa rab tu
24a3(phal chen): brjod pa dang / sems can rnams gya bsam pa sna tshogs rnam par sbyang ba dang / thugs rje chen po las byung ba'i chos kyi sprin gyis mngon par spang ba dang / thams cad la skyob pa'i byams pa chen po bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul gsum
24a4(phal chen): gyis yongs su brlan pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad mthong ba dang / rnam par dmigs pa'i btsun mo'i 'khor gyi nang du bstan pa yan cad du 'jig rten mtha' dang dpung med par sangs rgyas kyi phrin las
24a5(phal chen): yongs su bstan pa mdzad cing / ye shes mthu chen po thogs pa med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi mngon par mkhyen pa bsgribs pa med par bsgrub sa pa dang / chos rnam pa gsum gyis thabs mkhas pa dang ldan pa'i
24a6(phal chen): phrin las kyi mtha' dang / sku'i phrin las kyi mtha' shin tu rnam par dag pa dang / gsung gi phrin las ye shes nyams pa med pas rnam par dag pa dang / thugs kyi phrin las kyi mtha' zab cing chags pa med pa'i mthar thugs
24a7(phal chen): pa'i thabral mkhas pas sems can rnams kyi don mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las gsum pa'o// / bam po drug cu lnga pa// rnam par rgyal ba chen po mang
24a8(phal chen): ba rnams ni btsun mo'i 'khor rgyan rnam par phye ba tshad med pa dang ldan pa/ yid du 'ong ba spangs te mngon par 'byung ba'i spyod pa yongs su bstan pas sems can rnams 'jig rten gyi gnas las bskyod pa dang / 'jig
24b1(phal chen): rten gyi mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten du gtogs pa thams cad mi rtag par shes par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi tshul la mngon par zhen pa rnam par bzlog pa dang / 'jig rten gyi dga' ba la srang
24b2(phal chen): pa yongs su bcad pa dang / 'jig rten nyon mongs pa byang zhing nub pa la yang dag par spod par bya ba dang / sems can gyi don rjesu dran par bya ba'i phyir/ mngon par 'byung ba'i don la rab tu gzhol ba dang / khyim pa'i
24b3(phal chen): tshul yongasu spang pa bstan pa dang / nyon mongs pa med pa'i chos kyi sbyor ba la yang dag par gnas par bya ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam yong su rdzogs par bya ba dang / yon tan gyi dkyil 'khor tshad med pa yod
24b4(phal chen): su snang bar bya ba dang / ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor chen po brnyas pas sems can rnams kyi mi shes pa'i sgrib pa rab tu bsal ba dang / bdag nyid bsod nams kyi zhing bla na med par gyur par 'gro ba thams cad
24b5(phal chen): la bstan pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'i nang du 'dus par 'gro ba thams cad la yang dag par brjod pa dang / bdag nyid kyis ye shes kyi don gzi
24b6(phal chen): par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams rnam par dag pa'i sgor brjod pa dang / sems can rnams kha na ma tho bo med pa'i sgor sgrub pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ba'i sgo rab tu bstan pa dang / thams cad mkhyen
24b7(phal chen): pa'ang kyi rgyal mtshan yang dag par bsgreng ba mdzad cing mngon par 'byung ba ste// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bzhi pa'o// don gcig ma yin pa mkhyen pa dang ldan pa thams cad mkhyen
24b8(phal chen): nga'i ye shes kyi mthar thug pa rnams ni// chos thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o zhes/ byang chub kyi shing drung du byon te/ byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bas kyang bdud kyi dpung thams cad rab tu bzhom pa dang / skur
25a1(phal chen): byin gyis brlabs kyi mdzod kyi chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du rgyas par dgang ba'i phyir/ byin gyis brlabs zad mi shes pa'i mthar thugs pas mtha' rnam par spangs pa spyod pa tshad
25a2(phal chen): med pa rab tu brnyes pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i yul gyis rnam par rol pa'i ye shes kyi don dang ldan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i yon tan yang dag par sgrub pa yongasasu rdzogs pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad
25a3(phal chen): du gdan rnam par bkram pas yongasu rgyas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing ma lus pa thams cad du/ byang chub sems dpa' rnam par dmigs pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dam pa thob pa rnams kyis zhal du blta ba/ byang chub
25a4(phal chen): sems dpa' thams cad kyi rnam pa dang / smon lam khyad par can dang ldan pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad kyis yang dag par bsam pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo zab mo
25a5(phal chen): rab tu skor ba/ sangs rgyas kyi yul tshad med pa bsams pas/ byang chub sems dpa' brjod du med pa'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa sna tshogs spyod pa la yang dag par
25a6(phal chen): gzhol ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par dag pa mnga' ba 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis byin du rlob pa'i yul mnga' ba/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa'i sems can gyis
25a7(phal chen): rnam par dmigs pa dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad tha mi dad pa dang ldan pa 'byung ba'i sa byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa mtha' yas pa'i mthu'i gnas la yon tan gyi khyad par thams cad rab tu brnyes pas bzhugs pa 'jig rten
25a8(phal chen): gyi rnam pa thams cad ma lus pa'i mthar zhugs pa/ sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad dang // zhing gi rnam pa thams cad dang / chos kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam pa thams cad dang / yongs su smin par
25b1(phal chen): bya ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / dus kyi rnam pa thams cad dang / 'dul ba'i rnam pa thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnam pa thams cad ma lus par mthar thug pa'i rnams 'gro ba ma lus pa thams cad
25b2(phal chen): du mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par 'tshang rgya bas/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las lnga pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi
25b3(phal chen): 'khor lo bskor ba mdzad pa phyir mi ldog pa'i tshul gyis phyir mi ldog pa'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis tshad med pa'i 'khor lo dang / mi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen
25b4(phal chen): po'i tshul gyis thams cad ma lus par mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos kyi mdzod mun pa med pa'i sgos snang bar byed pa'i tshul gyis chos thams cad mkhyen pa'i mdzod kyi 'khor lo dang
25b5(phal chen): ye shes na mkha'i dbyings lngar tshad med pa'i tshul gyis chags pa med pa'i 'khor lo dang / chos thams cad kyi dngos po med pa'i rang bzhin rab tu rtogs par bya ba'i tshul gyis bsgribs pa med pa'i
25b6(phal chen): 'khor lo dang / sems can thams cad kyi chos kyi mig rnam par sbyong ba'i tshul gyis 'jig rten thams cad kyi sgron ma'i 'khor lo dang / 'jig rten thams cad du rgyas par 'gengs pa'i tshul gyis thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos
25b7(phal chen): brjod pa'i 'khor lo dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang mi 'gal ba'i tshul gyis// sangs rgyas thams cad 'dab 'dres par gyur pa'i 'khor lo dang / de dag la sogs pa rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong du chos kyi
25b8(phal chen): 'khor lo bskor bas sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa'i rnam pa chos kyi 'khor lo bskor te/ de ltar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bas
26a1(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa mdzad de/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi phrin las drug pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni grong dang grong khyer dang / grong rdal dang / rgyal po
26a2(phal chen): gan su gshegs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de mi'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lha'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / klu'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / dri za'i rgyal po'i
26a3(phal chen): gnas dang / lha ma yin gyi rgyal po'i gnas dang / nam mkha' lding gi rgyal po'i gnas dang / mi 'am ci'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / lto 'phye chen po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / srin po'i rgyal po'i gnas dang / sha za'i rgyal po'i gnas
26a4(phal chen): ngag tu gshegs kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ 'di lta/ ste grong khyer gyi sgor byon na/ sa g.yo ba dang / 'od zer snang ba dang / long ba rnams mig 'thob pa dang / 
26a5(phal chen): 'on pa rnams sgra thos par 'gyur ba dang / smyos pa rnams dran pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / gos med pa rnams gos 'thob par 'gyur ba dang / sdug bsngal ba rnams de ba 'thob pa dang / rol mo'i cha spyad ma
26a6(phal chen): dkrol ma brdungs par sgra yid du 'ong bar 'byin pa dang / rgyan snod na 'dug pa dang / gnas nas ma phog pa dang / ma bskyod ma dkrol bar bskyod cing dkrol ba'i sgra 'byung ba dang / bya sna tshogs mang po snga skad yid du 'ong ba 'byung ba dang / 
26a7(phal chen): lha na gtang mi phra zhing mi 'thun pa med pa'i sku mthong bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// mtshan dang dpe byad bzang po bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom
26a8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de// yong su gzigs pa dang / rnam par gzigs pa dang / brkyang ba dang bskum pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// gshegs
26b1(phal chen): pa dang slar bzhud pa dang / bzhengs pa dang / 'chag pa dang / bzhugs pa dang / gzigs pas kyang sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// chos bstan pa dang / mi gsung bar bzhugs pas kyang sems can
26b2(phal chen): rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul dang / yongasu bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rje su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul gyis kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten gyi khams kyi yul
26b3(phal chen): sems can bsam pa sna tshogs rgya mtsho dang ldan pa// 'jig rten gyi spyod pa thams cad rgyu zhing 'byung ba dang ldan pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba chen pos shin tu bstan pa/ sangs rgyas rje su dran pa dang ldan pa/ sngon 'grogs 'grogs
26b4(phal chen): pa byang chub sems dpa' dang gnas pa'i sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams ni sku gzugs bldan mi ngoms pa'o zhes bya bar
