26b5(phal chen): gzhol ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams skye bar dkon no zhes bya b.rayid ches par byed pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mthong zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos pa ni bsod nams kyi chos
26b6(phal chen): dkar po'i 'byung gnas su gyur pa'o zhes sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa yid la byed pa dang / 'jig rten thams cad rnam par dag pa ni// de bzhin gshegs pa skye ba yin no zhes bya bar khong du chud par byed pa dang / sangs rgyas
26b7(phal chen): rdza sa namatha'a'as pa nas bya bar dag pas khang / mardza 'ims ca 'byung ba mgasags pa gas pa dag pa pa / 
26b8(phal chen): tsatsal/ rangs rgyas bco na das rnams mnyes par byed pa dang / de badzin gshegs pa rnamasani yon namatha' las pa 'o gas yod chung par byed pa dang / de 'dzin gsags pa na sems can pa bcad
27a1(phal chen): mngon du gyur par rtog pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni sems can gyi rigs bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas su gyur par sems pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa ni zhing thams cad na snang bar
27a2(phal chen): khong du chud pa dang / de lta bu'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad 'byung bas/ 'jig rten thams cad na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// dad par byas pa dang / 
27a3(phal chen): phyag 'tshal ba dang / thal mo sbyar ba byas pa dang / rje su bstod pa dang / spyan drangs pa dang / mchod pa dang / mngon du mthong ba dang / 'dzum pa byas pa dang / sangs rgyas la dga' ba'i sems kyis mos par byas pa'i dge ba'i rtsa
27a4(phal chen): ba'i sgo nas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgyas rjes su dran par gyur pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
27a5(phal chen): ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// sangs rgya sa mthong bar 'dod par bya bas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan tshwa ni sem sa can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin
27a6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i sku kha dog dang dbyibs kyi rnam pa tshad med pa bstan pas kyang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad do// de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung thos par bya
27a7(phal chen): bas kyang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sems can rnams la sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad de/ de dag la sogs pa/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rnam pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong
27a8(phal chen): brjod du med pa dag 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad du sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / mthu dang 'dul ba ji lta ba'i tshul las mi 'da' bar 'byung ngo // de ltar sangs rgyas kyi phrin las 'jig rten
27b1(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems can kun gyi sems dang spyod pa dang / bsam pa la gnas pa dge ba rgya che ba tshad med pa dag phyir mi ldog pa'i yul dang / snying rje chen pos rab tu bskul ba dang / sngon gyi smon lam gyis yongasu
27b2(phal chen): skyo ba med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mkhyen pa'i stobs dang shugs kyis 'jig rten thams cad du 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bdun pa'o// sangs rgyas
27b3(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dgon pa la bzhugs sam/ zhi bar bzhugs sam/ dben par bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa la bzhugs sam/ ting 'dzin chen po'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ gcig pu
27b4(phal chen): dgyes par bzhugs sam/ sku mi snang bar bzhugs sam/ ye shes zab mo'i gnas la bzhugs sam/ sangs rgyas kyi yul gyi stob sa tshad med pa la bzhugs sam/ sku'i yongasu spyod pa mi mthong
27b5(phal chen): bas bzhugs kyang rung ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis sa rgyas kyi phrin las gzhan gyis mi tshugs pa'i ye shes dang / smon lam gyi tshul gyis mos pa bzhin du 'dul ba'i sems can rnams
27b6(phal chen): la rgyun mi 'chad par 'byung ste/ sangs rgyas lha yongasu tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas klu yongasu tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo // sangs rgyas gnod sbyin
27b7(phal chen): yongasu tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi 'am ci yongasu tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas lto 'phye chen po yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas srin po yongs su tshol ba dang / sangs rgyas mi dang mi ma yin pa yongs su tshol ba dang / 
27b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas nyan thos dang / sangs rgyas rang sangs rgyas dang / sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' yongs su tshol bas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// chos ston pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun
28a1(phal chen): mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas gcig brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas thams cad brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chang ngo do// byang chub
28a2(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyod pa'i khyad par dang / smon lam thams cad gcig tu brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa gcig rnam par phye ste/ spyod pa tha dad pa brjod pas kyang sangs
28a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// 'jig rten gyi yul sangs rgyas kyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas kyi yul 'jig rten gyi yul du brjod pas kyang sangs rgyas kyi phrin
28a4(phal chen): las rgyun mi 'chad do// yul ma yin pa sangs rgyas kyi yul du ba rjod pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin la rgyun mi 'chad do// nyin mtsha na dang / yud du yan man dang / zla ba dang / lo 'grangs par/ bzhugs
28a5(phal chen): pa dang / yongasu bzhugs pa nas de bzhin du bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i bar du bzhugs pas kyang / sangs/ rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sems can rnams la sangs rgyas
28a6(phal chen): kyi phrin las mdzad de// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las brgyad pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la 'byung gnas lta bu sems can thams cad
28a7(phal chen): kyi bsam pa kun la rnam par sbyong ba lta bu/ sangs rgyas rnams la dad pa lta bu/ sems khong du chud par bya ba la shin tu mos pa lta bu/ dbang po rnams la sgrub pa lta bu/ sems can skye dgu thams cad la 'dul ba lta bu/ 
28a8(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad la mos pa lta bu/ byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la 'byung ba lta bu/ byang chub tu zhugs pa rnams la skul ba lta bu/ gzhan gyi dring mi 'jog pa rnams la ye shes snang ba lta bu dag ste/ sangs
28b1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten mi rtag par ston pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun chad par brjod pa dang / phrin las mdzad pa'i mthar thug par bstan pa dang / chos kyi rgyud nyams pa med pa'i dngos
28b2(phal chen): por brjod pa dang / srid pa'i tshul rtsa ba nas chad par brjod pa dang / sems can thams cad skyo bar bya bar bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi rje su 'gro ba'i sems su 'thun par bya ba dang / sku tshe'i mtha' lta bur sems
28b3(phal chen): can rnams kyis shes par bya ba dang / sems can rnams kyis 'jig rten thams cad du dga' bar bya ba med par bstan pa dang / sems can rnams la ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas gcig nas gcig tu brgyud pa mnyes pa
28b4(phal chen): gyis shig par bstan pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam sa chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba bstan tu mi rung bar khong du chud par bya ba dang / 'jig rten rnams kyi rtsol ba bskyed pa dang / sangs rgyas
28b5(phal chen): la dmigs par brtson pa'i sems la dgod pa dang / yun du dran pa rnam par dag pas de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ba'i rnam par rtog pa bskyed pa dang / skyo ba'i dbang po phyir bzlog cing
28b6(phal chen): yong su dag par mdzad pa dang / sangs rgyas la mos pa bskyed pa dang / skyo bar gyur pa'i sems la byin gyis brlab par bya ba dang / sangs rgyas la dmigs pa'i rkyen 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad
28b7(phal chen): du phyin par dgongs pa mdzad pa dang / sku thams cad bshig ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gdung gis sems can rnams yongasu gzung ba mdzad pa dang / 'jig rten rnam par 'khrug pa dang // dregs shing
28b8(phal chen): myos pa'i sems can rnams sdom pa la dgod pa mdzad cing yongs su mya ngan las 'da' bar ston pas kyang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun mi 'chad te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs
29a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi phrin las dgu pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ 'jig rten thams cad na sems can rnams sgra sngags 'don cing du ba dang / mya ngan byed pa dang / mchi
29a2(phal chen): ma 'byin pa dang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas zhe 'am/ thugs rje chen po zhe 'am/ ded dpon chen po zhe 'am/ phan par bzhed pa thugs brtse ba can zhe 'am/ lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyi sems can thams cad
29a3(phal chen): kyi skyabasu gyur pa/ mgon du gyur pa/ rten du gyur pa// bla na med pa bsod nams kyi zhing nub par gyur to zhes 'am/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'byung bar dka'o zhes rnam pa de lta bur smre sngags 'don pa dang / mya ngan
29a4(phal chen): byed pa dang / sangs rgyas mthong ba rje su dran pa'i sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / yid la bya ba de dang de dag gi sgor/ sangs rgyas kyi phri na las tshad med pa rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'ad
29a5(phal chen): rnams yongs su mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshe/ 'di lta ste/ sems can rnams kyi sems dad par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams dang / pas mchod par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems cad rnams lhag pa'i
29a6(phal chen): bsam pa rnam par sbyong bar bya ba'i dbang dang // sems can rnams yongasu smin par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams yongs su spang bar bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams 'dul ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams bsod
29a7(phal chen): nams kyi tshogs yongs su rdzogs par bya ba'i dbang dang / sems can rnams de bzhin gshegs pa la mchod pas dmigs par bya ba'i dbang dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten dam pa sna tshogs su brgyan pas/ phyog
29a8(phal chen): dang yul sna tshogasu sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags par bya ba'i dbang gis sems can rnams kyi bsam pa dang / mos pa ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang / ring bsel byin gyis rlob ste// lha dang klu dang / gnod sbyin
29b1(phal chen): dang / dri za dang / lA ma yin dang / namakha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / mi'i gnas thams cad du 'dul ba dang / mos pa'i tshul ji lta ba bzhin du sku gdung dang / ring bsel byin gyis rlob bo// rang gi sku
29b2(phal chen): rnam par phye ste/ sku gdung dang ring bsel tshad med pa grangs med pa// dpag tu med pa/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa byin gyis rlob po// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mchod rten gyis sangs rgya
29b3(phal chen): kyi sku gdung 'jig rten thams cad du rnam par phye ba de'i yul dang / phyogs kyi klu'i gnas dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po'i gnas dang / maM'i gnas dang
29b4(phal chen): srin po'i gnas dag tu/ sku gdung dang ring bsel mchod par byed par 'gyur bas// sku gdung gi ring bsel dang / dbu dang phyag sen gyi mchod rten dang / sangs rgyas bzhugs pa'i mchod rten la 'gro
29b5(phal chen): ba thams cad nges par sangs rgyas dran par 'gyur te/ chos la rab tu rten pa ra 'gyur ro// dge 'dun la dad pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyuraro// yul dang phyogs kyi gnas de dang de dag tu'ang rgyun mi 'chad
29b6(phal chen): par sangs rgyas mchod pa la brtson pa'i bsam pas sbyin pa yongasasu gtong bar 'gyur ro// bsod nams byed par 'gyur ro// mtho ris de dang de yongs su dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// rigs dang rgyud kyi bdag nyid che
29b7(phal chen): ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// longs spyod chen po dang 'khor rnam par dag pa rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// lha dang mi'i phun sum tshogs pa nyam su myong bar 'gyur ro// log par ltung ba med pa'i lam yongs su rdzogs
29b8(phal chen): par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas 'byung ba don yod pa rab tu sgrub par 'gyur ro// chos dkar po la gnas pa yongs su rdzogs par byed par 'gyur ro// khams gsum pa las 'byung ba'i lam yongs su sbyong bar 'gyur ro// 
30a1(phal chen): theg pa gang la dad pa'i smon lam gyis nges par 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa de dang de dag la drin du gzo ba rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams la
30a2(phal chen): rten pa dang / skyabs btsal ba dang / mgon btsal ba dang / dpung gnyen btsal ba'i sems bskyed par 'gyur ro// de ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yongasu mya ngan las 'das kyang yon bsam gyis mi khyab pa
30a3(phal chen): spyong pa/ bsod nams zang mi shes pa'i yon gyi gnas dag ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni 'jig rten du byung na/ de ltar sems can rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam pa mang po rab tu bsags pas bsod nams kyi
30a4(phal chen): tshogs rab tu rdzogs par 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi phrin las bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dam gyis kyi phrin lnga
30a5(phal chen): rgya chen po tshad med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so// de dag ni sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi rlabs ma gtogs par lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten gyis tshad gzung bar mi nus pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma 'ong
30a6(phal chen): pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'jug par mi nus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyi su med par spyod cing dngos po rnam pa
30a7(phal chen): gzhi su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ lung bstan pa thams cad ston pa la gnyis su med par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
30a8(phal chen): rnams ni// sems can sangs rgyas kyi rje su dran pa la brtson pa rnams kyi sems dang bsam pa brjod du med pa 'byam klas pa rnams la gnyi su med par spyod do// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyi don ma lus par
30b1(phal chen): mngon par sangs rgyas pas gnyi su med pa'i sku rnam par dmigs par mdzad do// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad la rang bzhin gnyi su med par thugs su chud ba mnga'
30b2(phal chen): ba'o// 'byung ba dang / 'byung ba'i mtha' gnyi su med pa dang / sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha' dang / nga ltar byung ba'i mtha' gnyis su med par thug su chud pa mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gnyi su med pas
30b3(phal chen): dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad gcig par rab tu mkhyen cing ston pa thugs su chud par mnga' ba'o// sangs rgyas gcig dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gnyi su med par thug su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 
30b4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis thugs su chud pa dang / 'dul ba mdzad pa'i rnam par dmigs pa gnyis su med par thugasu chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'jig rten gyi chos thams cad/ sangs rgya skyem ga'i su
30b5(phal chen): med par thugs su chud pa mnga' ba'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad dge ba'i rtsa ba gcig ste/ gnyis su med par thugasu
30b6(phal chen): chung par mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gnyis su med par spyod cing / dngos po gnyi su med pa'i chos kyi dbang phyug gi chos so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag
30b7(phal chen): ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa/ chos thams cad la rab tu bzhugs pa rnams so// bcu gang zhe na sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings gnas pa'i ye shes
30b8(phal chen): chubadu rung baya dumab pa'o// pas rgyas bcom ldan 'ad rnam sa thugs chen mong gam pal 'azhugs pa'o// pangs rgyas bcom ma 'das nangangamatsham ma rtsab banan du byung bam bas
31a1(phal chen): rnams ldan sa nasan na mas pa gnas pa ma tsho na 'dapar 'azhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bca lnga 'das man rgyas ma par ma
31a2(phal chen): thugs la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams na chos thams cad nyams pa med par gzhol ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis rnam par spyod
31a3(phal chen): ba la bzhugs pa'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos thams cad kyi mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pas grub pa med pa'i yang dag pa'i mtha' mtshan nyid la bzhugs pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu
31a4(phal chen): po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa chos thams cad la bzhugs pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
31a5(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa rnams te/ bcu ga pa zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'das pa 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen
31a6(phal chen): pa dang / ma 'ongs pa 'brangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / da ltar byung ba 'grangs pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / tshig gi las mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen par
31a7(phal chen): nga na kyi rgya ma das pa chad ma par ma khyen pa dang/ mas can kyab mi ba dang / gas pa 'dag pa cad na pa rgyan pad/ byang na pa yang dag pa ca bzung dang / 'a
31b1(phal chen): dang chen po dang / rnam pa sna tshogs rnam par gnas pa'i mtshan nyid kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams la bsam pa tshad med pa yong su mi bdang bas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes 'bar bar bya ba dang / yongs su rdzogs par bya
31b2(phal chen): ba mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos thams cad 'tshang rgya ba'i mkhyen pa mtha' dag thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / 'jig rten gyi rgyud thams cad rnam par dbye ba'i ye shes gzigs pa mtha' dag
31b3(phal chen): thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa dang / chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi mig 'phrul gyi rnam pa lta bur dbye ba thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos
31b4(phal chen): thams cad ma lus par mngon par mkhyen pa'o// bam po drag cu rtsa drag pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi stobs chen po// stobs dam pa
31b5(phal chen): stobs tshad med pa/ stobs bdag nyid che ba/ stobs thub pa med pa// stobs mnyam pa/ stobs snying po dang ldan pa/ stobs mi shigs/ pa/ stobs 'jig rten thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ stobs
31b6(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyis mi 'phrogs pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rgyal mtshan stobs po che dpa' bo chen po'i stobs ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi sku ni pha rol gyi gnod pa thams cad kyis mi shigs mi chod pa'o// 
31b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi yul thams cad kyi sku tshe'i dbang po nyams par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ci skal pa'i me'i gdung bas 'tshig par mi nus pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'jig par gtogs
31b8(phal chen): ba chung phung por 'drongs par mi 'gyur ba'o// bdud thar sa cad dang / bdud rtsa snga thams cad dang / lha thams cad kyi drung dang / klu dang gnod sbyin dang / dri ba dang lha ma yin dang / namakha' lding dang / ma 'batsangang / 
32a1(phal chen): lto 'phye chen po dang / mi dang mi ma yin pa thams cad kyi dpung dang / sha za dang / srin po thams cad kyi dpung dang / sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi dpung gis brgal bar dka' ba'o// 
32a2(phal chen): rdo rje ri rab kyi raM tsam gyi char pa dang / khor yug gi raM chen po tsam dang / stong gsum gyi stong chen po tsam gyi rdo rje'i char bab kyang / bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs
32a3(phal chen): rgyas kyi ba spu gcig kyang 'gul bar mi 'gyur// g.yo bar mi 'gyur te/ bag tsha ba'i shas mi mnga' ba'o// bzhugs sam/ bzhengs sam/ bzhud dam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ spyod lam 'gyur ba med do// de bzhin
32a4(phal chen): gshegs pa gang na bzhugs pa'i yul de dang // de'i 'khor dag tu yang de bzhin gshegs pa dgyes na kun tu 'bab par mi 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi zhabs 'bring rnams la yang gnod par mi 'gyuraro// 
32a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyis byin gyis brlabs pa'i sems can rnams la yang / gnod par mi 'gyur zhing mi g.yon/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku lta la smos kyang ci dgos te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan
32a6(phal chen): 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dang po'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dgyes na/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas pa'i 'jig rten
32a7(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad ri rab kyi ri dang bcas pa/ khor yug dang khor yug chen po'i ri dang bcas pa/ rgya mtsho dang ri dang nags tshal thibs po dang / sems can gnas pa'i gnas tha dad pa kun dang bcas pa/ de lta bu'i
32a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ba spu'i bu ga gcig tu btsud de/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bzhag kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyi brlabs ma gtogs par sems can rnams
32b1(phal chen): byas shes par mi nus so// de bzhin gshegs pa de dag ni de sbed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams sku'i baspu'i khung bu gcig gis bzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bsnams shing / gshegs sam bcu
32b2(phal chen): sam/ bzhengs sam/ gzims kyang rung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i thugs skang cig tsam yang skyob ma mnga'o// chad cing dub par mi 'gyur ro// mthu dang stobs la yongs su nyam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// 
32b3(phal chen): lam rnam par 'gyur ba mi mnga'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di lta sde dper na/ nam pa' ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'dzin kyang skyo ba med do// dub par med do// gnod pa med do// ma
32b4(phal chen): par mi 'gyur ro// mi g.yo mi 'byung / mi 'jig go// de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang ba spu'i khung bu gcig du 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad bsnams kyang
32b5(phal chen): de'i rgyus thugs skad cig tsam du yang mi bde ba'i sku nyams mi 'byung ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan
32b6(phal chen): gyi chos gnyis pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams gshegs stabs gcig tu bzhud pas sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten
32b7(phal chen): gyi khams yongs su 'da' zhing thugs bskyed pa gcig gis bskal pa tha dad pa'i rim pa// sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed 'byung bar mdzad do// de lta bur
32b8(phal chen): gshegs pas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du gshegs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems kyi rgyud ji snyed pa'i skal par bzhud de/ 'jig rten gyi bcwa
33a1(phal chen): thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams tsam du 'khor kun tu rgya che zhing yangs pa'i 'khor yug chen po'i rdo rje'i ri dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rnam pa brjod
33a2(phal chen): du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa la bsgres pa snyed kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang de la bsgres pa de snyed pa spu'i khung du gcig tu btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu gcig tu ji lta ba bzhin du sku'i ba spu'i khung
33a3(phal chen): bu thams cad du btsud de/ ba spu'i khung bu yang sems can thams cad snyed du gyur la de dag thams cad bsnams te/ de snyed kyi ba spu'i khung bur tshul de bzhin du bshams te/ thugs bskyed pa de lta bus de bzhin
33a4(phal chen): gshegs pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ phyogs kyi dra ba thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam na mkha'i dbyings thams cad du rgyu zhing gshegs sam/ 'jig rten gyi
33a5(phal chen): khams kyi rgyud 'grangs pa sngon gyi mthar gtogs pa nas gzung ste/ phyi ma'i mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par de bzhin du gshegs pa sa bskal pa thams cad zad par gyur kyang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhud
33a6(phal chen): pa la brtson pa ni nyams par mi 'gyur ro// sku nyam chung bar mi 'gyur ro// thugs rnam par 'khrug par mi 'gyur ro// ting 'dzin nyams par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongs su nyams par mi 'gyur
33a7(phal chen): te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos gsum pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni bsod snyoms gcig bzhes nas
33a8(phal chen): bskal pa brjod du med par dkyil mo krung gcig bcas pas nyin mtshan gyi rgyud du sngon gyi mtha' dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur gtogs pa'i bskal pa 'das par bzhugs kyang sku mi g.yo zhing bde ba'i dam pa la spyod pa dang / 
33b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pas/ rnam par spyod kyang sems can 'ga' tsam la'ang / sangs rgyas kyi phrin las rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku de la 'jig rten gyi
33b2(phal chen): khams thams cad yongs su bkod de/ 'jig rten gyi khams de dag gi sems can gcig gi lus kyang 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed tsam du che ba de
33b3(phal chen): lta bur gyur la/ sems can gcig gi lus kyi tshad ji tsam pa de tsam gyi lus su sems can thams cad kyang gyur la/ sems can de dag re re'i gzugs kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi lcid ji tsam yod pa de tsam du
33b4(phal chen): gyur te// sems can gcig ji ltar lci ba bzhin du sems can tham sa cad re re'i ljid kyang de tsam du 'gyur te/ sems can de dag tham sa cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig la phyi ma'i
33b5(phal chen): mtha'i bskal pa'i mur thug par bsnams te/ phyag sor gyi rtse mo gcig gis ji ltar bsnams pa de bzhin du phyag sor thams cad kyi rtse mo la'ang de tsam re re bsnams kyang / de'i phyir de bzhin
33b6(phal chen): gshegs pa la sku mnyel ba 'am/ thugs dub par mi 'gyur te thugs bskyed pa'i cha shas shin tu phra ba gcig tsam du yang sdug bsngal mi bde ba skye bar mi 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug
33b7(phal chen): pa dang / na mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa dang / phyogs kyi dra ba'i rnam pa la 'jug pa re re dang / de lta bu la 'jug pa/ na mkha'i khams ma lus pa'i dbyings kyis klas pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa/ sgra'i
33b8(phal chen): rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams la 'jug pa thams cad re re zhing yang / skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis gzhal te/ nam mkha'i dbyings kyi kun tu khyab pa thams cad ma lus pa'i skra'i rtse mo'i cha shas
34a1(phal chen): kyi tshad kyis na mkha'i dbyings la 'jug pa thams cad du zhugs te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod lam 'di'i tshul dang / skyil mo krung gcig tu bzhugs pa'i spyod pas/ sngon gyi mtha' dang
34a2(phal chen): phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad par mdzad de/ bskal pa 'da' bar mdzad cing bskal pa la rab tu 'jug ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod
34a3(phal chen): pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bzhi pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sku gcig la dbu sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs te/ 
34a4(phal chen): dbu re ra la ljags sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang bajo dadu med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed byin gyis brlabs nas de dag re res kyang dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung
34a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang rjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed re re brjod de/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams thams cad go bar mdzad cing dbyangs kyi yan lag
34a6(phal chen): dang / sgra skad kyi gsung re res kyang mdo sde sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed bshad la mdo sde re re la yang chos bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod
34a7(phal chen): du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rab tu gzhol bar mdzad de/ chos bstan pa gcig las kyang chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba sbed brjod par/ 
34a8(phal chen): gyur la/ chos bstan pa gcig la ji lta ba bzhin du chos bstan pa thams cad las kyang de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge brjod de/ de ltar brjod pas bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod/ 
34b1(phal chen): du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad par gyur kyang / da dung gzhan yang bskal pa sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjo/ 
34b2(phal chen): du med pa'i yang brjod du bla'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du brgyud cing rab tu ston pa'i tshul gyi rnam grangs 'dis bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du rab tu bstan la rnam grangs 'di 'ang
34b3(phal chen): bas bskal pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed zad la sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi spyod pa snyed kyi bskal pa 'das par gyur te/ phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal pa zad cing
34b4(phal chen): 'das par byas kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa chos thams cad snang ba'i 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad rab tu shes bar bstan cing lung bstan pa dang / the tsom thams cad rab tu
34b5(phal chen): gcod pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / chos thams cad snang bar byed pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / byang chub sem sa dpa'i spyod pa thams cad brjod pa'i rgyun dang ldan pa'i cho
34b6(phal chen): kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / ye shes kyi nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor chen po'i rgyan dang ldan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad ma lus pa'i ye shes kyi sgron ma chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor
34b7(phal chen): lo bskor ba dang / tha dad pa yang dag par mkhyen pa dang / mi 'jig pa chen pos brgyan pa'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba rgyun mi 'chad do// sangs rgyas kyi sku gcig gi byin gyis brlabs kyis ji lta ba de bzhin du
34b8(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo'i sprin chen po dpe thams cad la dpe med par rab tu 'byung bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas gtugs pa sna'i rtse mo'i cha shas kyis
35a1(phal chen): gnal ba ma lus pa thams cad chags pa med par rnam par dbyebs/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi sprul pa de snyed de snyed du thugs
35a2(phal chen): skad cig re re la phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bskal par sprul pa mdzad cing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprul pa'i sku thams cad las de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi dbu mnga' bar gyur la
35a3(phal chen): gzhung de bzhin du sku re re la'ang de snyed de snyed kyi ljags mnga' bar gyur te/ ljags re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa'i sems can gyi khams
35a4(phal chen): thams cad go bar mdzad pa byung la dbyangs kyi yan lag dang / sgra skad kyi gsung de dag re res kyang de snyed de snyed kyi mdo sde bshad par gyur la/ mdo sde de dag re re la yang de snyed de snyed kyi chos
35a5(phal chen): bstan par rab tu gzhol ba mdzad de/ chos bstan pa de dag re re las kyang de snyed de snyed kyi chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge brjod par gyur la chos kyi tshig dang / yi ge de dag re res kyang chos kyi dbyings ma
35a6(phal chen): lus pa thams cad dbyangs kyi rgyas par bkang ste/ sems can gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad go bar mdzad kyang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbyangs la dub pa mi mnga' ste/ nyams par mi 'gyur la thogs pa ni mnga'
35a7(phal chen): zhing dma' bar mi 'gyur te/ de lta bu'i chos kyi 'khor lo bskor yang bskal pa phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug pa'i bar du rgyun 'chad par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i
35a8(phal chen): stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos lnga pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs dpal gyi be'us brgyan pa rdo rje chen po ltar shin tu bstan par grub pa mnga' ba dag
35b1(phal chen): ste/ de dag byang chub kyi shing drung du byon na bdud sdig to can gyis sems can thams cad snyed kyi bdud kyi sde gzugs sna tshogs can shin tu mi sdug pa// 'jigs 'jigs lngar 'dug pa rab tu sdang ba'i gzugs can
35b2(phal chen): 'jig rten thams cad shin tu 'jigs pa'i gzugs can rab tu skye g.ya' ba skyed pa'i gzugs can/ bdud shin tu mi sdug pa'i gzugs 'chang ba/ rab mchog por 'jigs pa 'jigs pa chen po skyed pa/ 
35b3(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad gsod pa/ 'jig rten thams cad phung par byed pa/ de lta bu sha stag gis byang chub kyi shing drung dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthar thugs par gang bar
35b4(phal chen): gzigs kyang byang chub kyi shing drung na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin ga/ shegs pa rnams la bsnyungs pa mi mnga'o// bag tsha ba mi mnga'o// ba spu gcig kyang g.yo ba med do// thugs kyi cha shwa
35b5(phal chen): shin tu phra ba 'ga' tsam gyis kyang de ltar rnam pa tha dad pa'i gzu gsal mtshan ma rnam pa tha dad pa 'dzin pa mi mnga' ste/ shin tu bstan no// g.yo ba med do mi skul to// 'gyur ba
35b6(phal chen): med do// rnam par rtog pa med do// shin tu zhi ba'o// bsnyengs pa dang / bag tsha ba thams cad dang shin tu bral lo// sdug pa dang khong khro ba shin tu spangs so// sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa rgyun mi 'chad do// / 
35b7(phal chen): byams pa chen po'i stobs dang ldan pa'o// thugs rje chen po'i gnas kyis dbang po shin tu dben pa'o// bag tsha ba mi mnga' ba'i thugs dang ldan pa'o// thugs shin tu bstan zhing nyams pa mi mnga' ba'o// 
35b8(phal chen): tshu rol gyi gnon la pas zil gyi mo non pa'i thugs dang ldan pa ste/ bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi rigs su gtogs pa'i lha thams cad dang / bdud kyi sde thams cad shin tu zil gyis gnon to// shin tu
36a1(phal chen): wa 'gong ngo // de ltar zil gyis mnan te spa gong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa la sbubs tshol lo// de dag la bcom ldan 'das de dag cho 'phrul chen po gsum gyis de bzhin gshe
36a2(phal chen): ba'i 'dul ba mdzad pa nye bar sgrub ste/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur ro// 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i spobs/ sangs rgyas
36a3(phal chen): kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos drug pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi gsung thogs pa med pa ni 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa de dang de dag thams cad du sems can rnams 'dul
36a4(phal chen): ba'i don gyis rnam par dmigs par kun tu khyab par 'byung ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung de ni ri rnams la thogs pa me do// ri rab la thogs pa med do rin po che'i ri la thogs pa med
36a5(phal chen): do// khor yug dang khor chen po la thogs pa med do// lha'i khyim la thogs pa med do// klu'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gnod sbyin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do// dri ba'i khyim pa
36a6(phal chen): thogs pa med do// lha ma yin gyi khyim la thogs pa med do// nam mkha' lding gi khyim la thogs pa med do// mi 'am ci'i khyim la thogs pa med do// lto 'phye chen po'i khyim la thogs pa med do// mi dang mi ma yin
36a7(phal chen): pa'i khyim la thogs pa med do// gal te brgya la 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yod pa'i sgra chen po 'jig rten rnam pa tha dad pa'i sgras 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad gang ste/ ca co 'dres par gyur kyang de la de bzhin
36a8(phal chen): gshegs pa'i gsung ni 'dul ba'i sems can rnams kyi na pa'i rnam par dmigs pa la bsgribs pa med pa yin te/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung 'ba' shig de dag gi rna ba'i rnam par dmigs pa la lhang nge snyam/ 
36b1(phal chen): ldan ne ste/ go bar mdzad pa'i tshig dang / yi ge rnams kyang rlag par mi 'gyur te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bdun pa'o// 
36b2(phal chen): gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thugs ni chags pa mi mnga' ba ste/ bskal pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med par yongasu sbyangs pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / 
36b3(phal chen): da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang / rgyan gcig tu gyur pa'o// rnyog pa med cing rnam par dngas te shin tu gsal ba'o// bdag gi zhes la mi mnga' ba'o// chos thams cad la mi gnas pa'o// nang na gnas pa
36b4(phal chen): ma yin pa'o// phyi rol na gnas pa ma yin pa'o// ma skyes pa'o// dmigs pa thams cad kyis dben pa'o// zhi zhing gnas pa me dpa'o// rtsom pa med pa'o// 'du shes sna tshogs thams cad la ma
36b5(phal chen): gnas pa'o// dngos po'i rnam par rtog pa thams cad 'gags pa'o// rang bzhin gyis 'od dang zhing gsal ba'o// yongasu dag pa'o// dmigs pa dang / yid la bya ba thams cad dang ma 'dres pa'o// chos
36b6(phal chen): thams cad nyon mongs pa med pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o// yang dag pa'i mtha' 'dod chags dang bral bas dag pa'o// chos kyi dbyings shin tu bstan pa'i mthar thug pa'o// chos kyi dbyings kun nas mi zad pa dang ldan pa'o// 
36b7(phal chen): 'du shes kyi rnam pa thams cad kyi tshad ngam nga bral ba'o// 'dus byas dang 'dus ma byas kyi brjod pa thams cad 'gag pa'o// tshig gi lam gyis brjod med pa'i mthar thug pa'i yul lo// mi zad pa dang chags pa med
36b8(phal chen): pa'i dbyings kyi mthar thug pa'o// ye shes sngon du 'gro ba'o// sbubs bcu rgyan du gyur pa'o// chos thams cad kyis rnam par dag pa'o// thabs mkhas pas byung ba'o// chos sna tshogs dang / chos dum dang / chos
37a1(phal chen): thams cad shin tu bstan pa dang mi 'gal ba'o// dus gsum du tha dad pa med pa'o// chos kyi dbyings thams cad chos gni med pa thams cad kyi mnga'i pha rol tu phyin pa gnyis pa'o// 
37a2(phal chen): chos thams cad la mnga' ba'i 'byung gnas dang mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi tshul thams cad la dgongs pa khyad par du rmongs pa med pa'o// zhing gi rgyud du gtogs pa thams cad dang phyogs kyi dra ba dang / rgyud 'byam
37a3(phal chen): klas pa ma lus pa thams cad la mi gnas pa bstan zhing mi g.yo la nyams pa med pa'i ye shes kyis rab tu gzigs pa chos ma lus pa thams cakyi mthar thug pa zag pa thams cad yongs su zad pa thugs rnam par grol zhing
37a4(phal chen): zas mi mnga' ba dang / shes rab rnam par grol bas shin tu rnam par grol dpa yang dag pa'i mtha' mi zad pas klas pa/ chags pa med par rnam par spyod pa rtag tu mnyam par bzhag pa/ dus gsum
37a5(phal chen): thams cad du bsgribs pa med par 'byung ba/ sems can thams cad kyi dus gsum gyi sems dang spyod pa thams cad ma lus par thugs skad cig gis rab tu mkhyen pa ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas
37a6(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos brgyad pa'o// gzhan yang sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi chos kyi sku ni sku mi mnga' ba ste/ rang bzhin gcig tu
37a7(phal chen): gyur pas sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yul tshad med pa'i sku'o mtha' dang dpung med par yongs su grub pa'i sku'o// 'jig rten thams cad kyis zad par mi nus pa'i sku'o// khams gsum pas gos pa med pa'i sku'o// 
37a8(phal chen): brtan pa'i sus rnam par dmigs pa'o// lhag pa'i bsam pa dang rjem dran pa'i byin gyi brlabs kyis sku'i rang bzhin yang dag par smon pa'o// bden pa med pa dang / brdzun pa med pa'i su mnyam pa nyid kyi 'o
37b1(phal chen): dag pa'o// chos kyi mu bzud pa dang / byon pa med pa'i bu'o// 'dus ma byas pas 'jig pa med pa'i sku'o// mtshan nyid med pas mtshan nyid gcig pa chos kyi sku'i rang bzhin no// yul na mi gnas pa dang / byams
37b2(phal chen): na mi gnas pa'i sku'o// ma lus pa thams cad kyi lus kyi sku'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / rnam par 'phrul pa mtha' yas pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// lus thams cad du yongs su gzhol ba'i
37b3(phal chen): sku sna tshogs su rnam par dmigs pa mdzad kyang chos kyi sku'i tshul gyi rje su 'brang ba'o// ye shes kun tu snang ba'i snying po can no// sku yongs kyi mdzod du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings rnam pa tha dad pa med pa shin tu
37b4(phal chen): bstan pa'i sku'o// khams gsum ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par 'gengs pas kun tu khyab pa'i sku'i rang bzhin no// mi g.yo mi dgongs pa'i sku rnam par dag pa'o// yod pa yang ma
37b5(phal chen): yin med pa yang ma yin pa'i tshul dang tshul ma yin par rab tu brjod pa'i sku'o// sems can gyi mos pa rnam pa sna tshog sa 'dul bar 'gyur ba'i sku'o// 'gag pa gang yang ma yin/ 
37b6(phal chen): ma 'gag pa gang yang ma yin pas 'dul ba ston pa'i sku'o// yon tan rin po che thams cad yang dag par byung bas shin tu 'phags pa'i sku'o// chos thams cad sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi de bzhin nyid du yang dag
37b7(phal chen): bsgrubs pa'i sku'o// rang bzhin gyis/ rab tu zhi zhing bsgribs pa med pa'i mthar thug pa'i sku'o// thogs pa mi mnga' bas chos thams cad thugasu chud pa'i sku'o// thams cad kyi rjesu song ba'i chos kyi
37b8(phal chen): dbyings kyis rnam par dag cing / 'jig rten thams du shin tu rnam par phye ba'i sku'o// phyir mi ldog cing bsgribs pa mi mnga' la/ sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pas ye shes thams cad kyi rje su 'brang zhing yang yang
38a1(phal chen): dag par gzhol bas thug su chud pa'i sku ste/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos dgu pa'o// gzhan yang sangs
38a2(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi ye shes mnyam pa med pa dang / mnyam pa ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi thugasu chud pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis byung ba'o// mngon par 'grub pa'i spyod
38a3(phal chen): pa khyad par du 'phags pa'i smon lam dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pas rnam par dag pa'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis yong su rdzogs par byas pa'o// tha dad pa med pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad
38a4(phal chen): kyi byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad kyis bzung ba'o// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgya mtsho'i spyod pa'i tshul thams cad thugs chud pa'o// smon lam dang spyod pa chen pos yongasu mi dog pa'o// spyod
38a5(phal chen): pa thams cad mi mnyam pa med pas yong su rdzogs par byas pa'o// spyod pa'i stobs la thub par dka' ba'i spyod pa thams cad kyis mngon par 'byung ba'o// spyod pa thams cad kyi rnam par dag pa'o// 
38a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa legs par spyad pas rgyud dma' ba med pa'o// sangs rgyas thams cad kyis tshad med par spyad pa'o// ting 'dzin thams cad kyi spyod yul mtha' yas pa'o// lam thams cad kyis rab tu brjod
38a7(phal chen): pa ma yin pa'o// lam gyi yul med pa'o// lam thams cad la rab tu zhugs pa'o// ye shes dam pa'i stobs kyi tshul mkhyen pa'o// bag tsha ba mi mnga' bas chos kyi char 'bebs pa'i 'khor lo dang ldan pa'o// dge 'dris
38a8(phal chen): pa dang ma dris pa la rje su 'thun pa'i chos kyi tshul ston pa mkhyen pa'o// mnyam pa med pa dang mnyam pas shin tu dag pa'o// sku dang thugs dang / gsung gi yang dag par spyod pa rnams la phrin las gsum yongs su
38b1(phal chen): dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bsgom pas bsnyes pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par spyod pas bsnyes pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs thams cad bskyed pa'i don du sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyis mdzad pa thams cad rab tu
38b2(phal chen): 'byung ba'o// thams cad mkhyen pa'i gnas kyi bstan pa tshad med pa'i gnas rtsa ba med pa dang ldan pa'o// mngon par shes pa'i ye shes thams cad kyis mthar thug par mi 'gyur ba'o// 'jig rten gyi sems kyis spyad pa'i
38b3(phal chen): shes pa thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab pa'o// chos thams cad ma lus par mkhyen cing gzigs pas sems can thams cad yongasu skyob pa'o// dus gsum yangs pa tha dra cand kyi tshul shin tu phra ba mtha' dang
38b4(phal chen): dpung med pa ma lus par mkhyen pa'o// 'jig rten las 'das pa'i don mkhyen pa'i phyir phra ba'i ye shes thug su chud pas 'jig rte/ na gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad rnam par dag pa/ phyir mi ldog
38b5(phal chen): pa'i ye shes kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi phrin las brjod du med pa 'jig rten thams cad du sbyor ba'o// sangs rgyas kyi sku 'grangs pa tha mas cad thugasu chud pa'i ye shes kyis yi ge med pa'i chos thugasu du
38b6(phal chen): pa'o// yi ge sna tshogs rnam par phye ba dang / yi ge thams cad smos shing brjod pa mkhyen pas brjod du med pa thug su chud pa'o// kun tu bzang po'i ye shes kyis dge ba'i chos spyad pa thams cad rnam par dag pa'o// dam
38b7(phal chen): bcas pa'i tshul bzhin du sems can thams cad kyi lus dang / skye mched ji lta bar thugs skad cig dang ldan pa'i shes rab kyis chos thams cad khong du chud par ston pa mkhyen pa'o// chos thams cad kyi don du chos yong
38b8(phal chen): su btang shing rim gror bya bas thug su chud pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// dus gsum thams cad la thugs skad cig
39a1(phal chen): gis chags pa med par mkhyen cing thugs su chud pa'i yul dang ldan pa'o// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas 'byung ba ma lus par yul du gyur pa'o// 'jig pa med par
39a2(phal chen): 'dul ba thams cad yul du gyur pa'o// thams cad kyi rje su song zhing rnam par dag pa'i yul thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas pa'o// sa mtshams med cing thugs pa'i mngon par shes pa rnam par sangs rgyas pa'o// 
39a3(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi sems dang yid dang / rnam par shes pa'i rnam pa dus gsum du brjod pa ma lus pa thams cad thugs skad cig gis mkhyen cing thugasasu chud pa'o// sems can gyi rnam pa thams cad la sa mtsham
39a4(phal chen): ma bcad pa'o// 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rnam pa thams cad la mu med pa'o// dus gsum gyi rnam pa thams cad la mtha' yas pa'o// sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba'i rnam pa thams
39a5(phal chen): cad la tshad med pa'o// shes bya'i rnam pa thams cad la lhag ma ma lus pa ste/ de dag thams cad lhag ma med par mngon par sangs rgyas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ye shes sangs rgyas kyi rdzu 'phrul
39a6(phal chen): dang / rnam par 'phrul pas byung ba thams cad thug su chud pa dang / mkhyen pa thams cad rgyun 'chad pa med de/ de la sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams sangs rgyas kyi khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba'i skus/ mtha'
39a7(phal chen): dang dbus med par spyod pa yin// chags pa med pa'i thugs kyis spyod pas/ mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin/ thugs rje chen po'i sbyor bas dus thams cad du rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par chos bstan pa la spyod
39a8(phal chen): bas mtha' dang dbus med par spyod pa yin te/ 'di ni sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi sangs rgyas kyi mthu bo che chen po'i stobs/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de
39b1(phal chen): dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis mthu bo che chen po'i stobs sangs rgyas kyi spyod pa'i rgyal mtshan gyi chos rnams te/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems can thams cad dang / nyan thos dang
39b2(phal chen): rang sangs rgyas thams cad kyis bsam gyis mi khyab cing dpag tu mi nus pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba rnams te/ sangs rgyas bcom
39b3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni dga' ldan gyi tshe ji srid par bzhugs nas/ 'pho ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni// zla ba bcus bltam pa bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das
39b4(phal chen): rnams ni/ mngon par 'byung bar dgyes pa'i thugs kyi mngon par 'byung ba la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldana'/ dus rnams ni byang chub kyi shing drung du bzhugs nas/ sangs rgyas kyi cho
39b5(phal chen): thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni thugs skad cig gis sa / sa kyi chos thams cad mngon par sangs rgyas nas// 'jig rten gyi
39b6(phal chen): khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu bstan pa la thog pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dus bzhin du 'dul ba rnams la chos kyi 'khor lo skor ba la
39b7(phal chen): thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa'i tshul bzhin du dus la bab par bshad cing lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
39b8(phal chen): ni dus la bab pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi phrin las mdzad pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni byang chub sems dpa' yongasu grub pa lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi mnga'o// sangs
40a1(phal chen): rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni skadang cig gcig tu sems can thams cad kyi dri ba 'ong su dris pa skad cig gcig gis lung bstan pa la thogs pa mi ma / ce rgyal ba'i sras bcu ma
40a2(phal chen): ngag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi thogs pa mi mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos
40a3(phal chen): rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du ngan song dang bral bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni// mthong ma thag tu sems
40a4(phal chen): can rnams myur du bsod nams yongasu rdzogs pa 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du dge ba'i rtsa ba la yongs su smin par 'gyur
40a5(phal chen): ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu/ sems can rnams myur du mtho ris su skye ba yongs su dgapa 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni
40a6(phal chen): mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du yid gnyis dang / nem nur yang dag par bsal ba 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du byang chub kyi sems
40a7(phal chen): bskyod nas phyir mi ldog pa 'thob par 'gyur te/ sems can mos pa yangs pa dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyis 'dul ba las byang chub tu sems ma bskyed pa'i rnams kyang bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub
40a8(phal chen): tu sems bskyed do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu skyon med par ma 'das pa dmigs pa'i lta ba can gyi sems can rnams myur du skyon med pa 'da' ba'i rgyu rab tu 'dzin to// sangs rgyas bcom
40b1(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa'i dbang po rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems
40b2(phal chen): can rnams myur du bsgribs pa thams cad byang ba 'thob par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mthong ma thag tu sems can rnams myur du snang ba 'thob cing mi 'jigs pa zhum pa med pa'i spobs pa rab
40b3(phal chen): tu rtsom te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi de bzhin gshegs pa mthong ma thag tu myur du 'byung ba'i chos rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas
40b4(phal chen): bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rjesu dran pa rnam par dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi sngon gyi sbyor bas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par
40b5(phal chen): bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni spyod pa rnam par dag pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni pha
40b6(phal chen): rol tu phyin pa yongs su rdzogs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni smon lam chen po yongs su rdzogs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa'
40b7(phal chen): rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni yang dag par bsgrubs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams
40b8(phal chen): ni sngon gyi mthar sangs rgyas kyi tshangs par spyad pa la spyad pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i sgo nas kyang / 
41a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni gzugs kyi sku tshad med mu med pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjes dran
41a2(phal chen): par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni sangs rgyas kyi yul gyis rnam par 'phrul pa tshad med mu med pas kyang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin/ sangs rgyas bcom
41a3(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams ni stobs bcu dang mi 'jigs pas kyang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis rjesu dran par bya ba yin te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyis rjes
41a4(phal chen): su dran pa rnam par dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag na/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyi kyi rnam par spyod pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings
41a5(phal chen): thams cad dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi sems sna tshogs dang / sems du ma dang / spyod pa dang / g.yo ba'i rgyud thams cad ma lus par zhugs gcig gis thug su chung
41a6(phal chen): ba dang / dus gsum gyi sems can thams cad kyi las dang / las kun nas blangs pa sna tshogs cho mcho dgu rnam pa tha dad pas mngon par 'gro zhing nyo bar sogs pa mang nyung dang / rnam par smin pa tha dad pa ma lus
41a7(phal chen): par thugs gcig gis thug su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can gyi rigs sna tshogs dang / sems can gyi rigs du ma'i sems can ma lus pa thams cad 'dul ba'i dus ji bzhin du yongs su bstan
41a8(phal chen): pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rje su bstan pa'i cho 'phrul dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi cho 'phrul gyis byin gyis brlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus par thugs su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / phyogs dra ba'i rgyud
41b1(phal chen): thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams kyi rgyud thams cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi sems kyi mtshan ma bzung ste/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / skye ba dang / rnam par dbye ba ma lus par thug su chud pa dang / 'jig
41b2(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba dang / mos pa ji lta ba dang / 'dul ba ji lta ba bzhin du rnam pa tha dad pa tshad med par skad cig tu/ sangs rgyas bstan pa dang / rnam par dmigs par
41b3(phal chen): bya ba dang / byin gyis brlabs pa ma lus par thug su chud pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi sems can pha rol gyi bsam pa la/ sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs yang dag par bstan pa ma lus pa zhug du chung
41b4(phal chen): pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems cad rnams 'dul ba ji lta bzhin du nye bar len pa med pa'i sangs rgyas nyid du 'gyur/ bar gdams ngag dang / rjesu bstan pas de bzhin gshegs pa
41b5(phal chen): 'byung ba bstan pa ma lus par thug su chud pa dang / chos kyi dbyings su mas cad kyi sems can thams cad kyi thams cad 'gro ba dang / de dang der 'gro ba'i lam ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig
41b6(phal chen): gis thugs chud pa dang chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyis/ sangs rgyas rjesu dran pa phyogs thams cad du btang ba'i tshul ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig cig gis thug su chud pa dang / 
41b7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi sems can rnams kyi mos pa dang / sems kyi tshad ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi sku kha dog mu med pa/ dbyibs mtha' yas pa bstan pa ma lus par thugs kyi skad cig gcig gis thur
41b8(phal chen): su chung pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi rnam par spyod pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
42a1(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzin tshad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams te/ bcug
42a2(phal chen): zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos thams cad la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can rnams la 'di skad cig gcig tu chos ston pa mdzad
42a3(phal chen): do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sems can thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang skad cig gcig gis/ sems can gyi khams sna tshogs rnam pa tha dad pa
42a4(phal chen): rnams kyang bdag med pa'i mtha' la gnas par yongasu ston to// / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi dus gsum la mnyam par bzhag kyang
42a5(phal chen): thugs skad cig gcig gi cha shas la'ang mnyam par bzhag tu/ nga rnam par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi phyogs 'byam klas
42a6(phal chen): pa'i dra ba thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rgyud/ rnam pa thams cad la mnyam par bzhag kyang mi zad pa'i zhing gi mtha' la yang bzhugs shing rnam par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ 
42a7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi sku mu med pa la mnyam par bzhag kyang 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyis kyang sangs rgyas kyi sku sna tshogs rnam par dmigs par yang dag par
42a8(phal chen): ston pa mdzad do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad sku dang / gsung dang thugs kyis yongasu rgyas par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang / sems can thams cad kyi sem
42b1(phal chen): 'byung ba'i mdzod sna tshogs la yang mos pa dang yid la byed pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnam ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin la
42b2(phal chen): rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang 'dod chags dang bral ba'i mtha'i mur thug pal bzhugs pa yang yongasu mi gtong ngo // sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad kyi 'jig rten thams
42b3(phal chen): cad kyi brten pa la rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang thugs skad cig gcig gis rten cing 'brel bar 'byung ba brjod pa yang rab tu ston to// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni/ chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams ca
42b4(phal chen): kyi 'jig rten pa dang / 'jig rten las 'das pa 'byam klas pa la rtag/ tu mnyam par bzhag kyang thugs skad cig gcig gis sems can thams cad la sangs rgyas mu med pa bstan pa rnam par dgod pa'i
42b5(phal chen): tshul mu med pas/ sangs rgyas bstan pa rgyun mi gcod do// sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni// chos kyi dbyings ma lus pa thams cad du bsgribs pa med par rtag tu mnyam par bzhag kyang
42b6(phal chen): thugs skad cig gcig gis sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyang rtogs par thugasu chud cing / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par thar pa mu med pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog brnyes par bzhugs te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de
42b7(phal chen): ngag ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzin chad med bsam gyis mi khyab pa rnams so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom
42b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sangs rgyas skye ba brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la
43a1(phal chen): 'bya/ chos kyi 'khor lo brjod du med pa'i yang brjod du med pa bskor ba yong su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la sems can yong su smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba brjod du med
43a2(phal chen): pa'i yang brjod du med pa yongasasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la zhing brjod du med pa'i yang brjod med pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon
43a3(phal chen): pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad yongasasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i zhing gi rgyud yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / 
43a4(phal chen): rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ra ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rdzu 'phrul dang / rnam pa ra 'phrul pa yongs su bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra
43a5(phal chen): ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sa can gyi khams thams cad yongasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar
43a6(phal chen): byung ba'i sangs rgyas kyi phrin las thams cad yongasu bstan pa'i rnam par thar pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi rnam par thar pa'o// shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs
43a7(phal chen): rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las/ sangs rgyas kyi chos bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa'i le'u ste/ sum cu dgu pa'o// / bam po drug cu rtsa bdun pa// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po/ 
43a8(phal chen): mtshan rgya mtsho brjod pa'i don du/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la smras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul mi chen po'i mtshan chos kyi rgyan rin po che sna tshogs sum cu rtsa gnyis mnga' bas/ de
43b1(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu de ni 'khor kun nas 'od zer gyi dra bas shin tu 'phro ba'i sprin rab tu 'byung zhing rgyas par 'gengs pa ste/ de la mi chen po'i mtshan rin po che dang po dbu'i dbu mtshams na/ rin po che sna tshogs
43b2(phal chen): thams cad kyi rgyal po las 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad snang ba bkye bas/ dpal gyis yongs su rgyas shing yan lag dang / nying lag thams cad nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin rnam par bkye ba yongs su 'khyil pa'i
43b3(phal chen): glong gi dbyings kyis phyogs thams cad 'od kyis rnam par snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la 'phro ba'i 'od kyi dkyil 'khor glog gi 'phreng ba lta bur 'byung bas/ phyogs mtshams thams cad du de bzhin
43b4(phal chen): gshegs pa snying po byang chub tu bzhugs pa ston cing // thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi namakha'i sprin kun tu 'dal pas chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i rgyal po sna tshogs
43b5(phal chen): mdzod spu g.yas phyogasu 'khyil pa'i dbyings las gser gyi kha dog bzang por 'od zer 'bar bar 'jig rten gyi khams/ su byung ba'i 'od kyis/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhin gshegs
43b6(phal chen): pa'i dbu dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan gsal ba'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul rin po che'i 'od kyi glong g.yas phyogs su yongasu 'khyil pa chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / 
43b7(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i bsod nams dang / ye shes kyi sgron ma snang bas 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi sprin rnam par 'dal ba byang chub sems dpa'i mchog
43b8(phal chen): rnams la snang bas/ chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gser yid du 'ong ba'i sprin sna tshogs kyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba
44a1(phal chen): rab tu 'bar bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snang bar byas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bsam gyis mi khyab pa snang bar bstan pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'
44a2(phal chen): dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che bai DUr+ya'i 'od zer dang / me tog gi mdog gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad snang bar rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin/ nor bu rin po che'i rgyal po'i
44a3(phal chen): mtshan nyid lta bu'i dbu skra/ rin po che sna tshogs snang ba'i mtshan nyid kyi 'od chags pas/ phyogs thams cad rnam par snang bar byed pas/ sangs rgyas kyi sngon gyi dka' thub dang / dpal gyi ye shes las rnam pa de lta bur
44a4(phal chen): byung ba'i rin po che'i 'od zer rab tu bkye ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dang / rin po che'i 'od zer g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing 'phro bas byang
44a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa// rin po che'i cod pan gyi 'od de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs kyi rnam par rgyas pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rin po che'i 'od tshad med par de bzhin
44a6(phal chen): gshegs pa'i chos kyi rang bzhin gyis/ rnam par 'phrul pa yang dag par ston pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu de la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che rnam par 'phrul pas// nor bu rin
44a7(phal chen): che rgya mtshos bkye ba'i 'od dang / 'od zer dri ma med pa rab tu 'phros pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i chos bstan pa rgya mtsho rnam par snang bar 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi ye
44a8(phal chen): shes rgya mtsho shin tu yangs pas chos kyi dbyings kun tu de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi sprin 'byung ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la/ rin po che'i rgyal po sems kyi rgyal po dang / in+da ni la
44b1(phal chen): las 'od bkye ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil pas 'jig rten gyi khams dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i 'od 'phro ba sngon ma'i sprin/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yon tan rdza
44b2(phal chen): mtsho rab tu sgrog pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du nga ro 'byin cing / sangs rgyas kyi stobs yongasu dag pa rgya mtsho dang / sang+yas rgya mtsho 'byin pa'i sprin shin tu yangs pa'i 'od ces bya ba mnga' ba dang
44b3(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i me tog sna tshogs dang rin po che'i rgyal po baiDUr+ya'i 'od zer rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer kun tu 'byung ba'i dra ba/ mngon par 'phags pa las chos kyi lus dang ldan pa'i byang chub
44b4(phal chen): sems dpa' 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad dang / phyogs rgya tsho ra de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa yang dag par ston cing sangs rgyas kyi stobs chos kyi dbyings la mngon du gyur pa rab tu ston par bzhugs
44b5(phal chen): pa/ sems nacad la yongs su ston pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa tshad med du med pa yang dag par 'phags shing yongasu dag la dri ma med pa yongasu mnan te/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od kun tu snang ba'i
44b6(phal chen): rang bzhin rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer dkyil 'khor gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi mtshan rin po che las 'od
44b7(phal chen): rab tu bkye bas/ zhing thams cad kun nas yog cing bsgribs pa med de/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du sangs rgyas kyi gsung rin po che'i me tog shin tu rgyas pa'i 'od zer 'phro ba rab tu bkye bas/ chos kyi rgya mtsho chen po
44b8(phal chen): ra' gyur ba ma/ byang du ba mams dang 'i spyod pa thams cad kyi kyang po dang / blang ba can gyi smin langs pa 'a ces bya mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i yan na po'i dren tu dang / maldan pa dang / rdorje
45a1(phal chen): mang po las nor bu rin po che rnam par gton te/ rab tu bkram pa'i kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od rnam par dag pa/ rin po che bai DUr+ya'i 'od kun tu 'byung ba las sgra skad/ rgya mtsho thams cad kyis
45a2(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings su sangs rgyas kyi snang ba rnam par ston pa'i chos rgya mtsho'i ye shes sangs rgyas sprul pa'i 'od kun tu 'gyed pa'i sprin rab tu snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i
45a3(phal chen): mtshan rin po che'i 'od g.yas phyogs su 'phro ba'i me tog rin po che'i lhab lhub kyis brgyan pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po byang chub kyi rgyan gyi sprin mngon par 'thon pa
45a4(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du/ chos rnam par dag ste/ bskal pa thams cad du rnam par thar pas chos kyi dbyings rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang
45a5(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sems kyi rgyal po'i 'od zer dam pa/ rgya mtshos brgyan pa'i chos kyi rgyan tu mtshan rnam par bkod pa las 'jig rten gyi khams
45a6(phal chen): na 'khod pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i sprin la snang ba shin tu 'byung zhing ye shes kyi sku dang / chos kyi skus de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan rgya mtsho la spyod pa'i byang chub sems dpas yongs su khyab pa'i sprin dang / 
45a7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rdo rje'i gzhi/ me tog dang ldan pa'i bai DUr+ya kun tu snang bas// chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur
45a8(phal chen): te/ rnam par snang bas chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho yongs su rgyas par 'gengs shing / 'jig rten gyi khams su rin po che thams cad kyi pad+mo'i 'od kyi rgyan thams cad kyis chos kyi dbyings thams cad du khebs par byang chub sems
45b1(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa bzhis rnam par 'phrul pa dang / nga ros chos kyi dbyings thams cad du rgyas pa'i mtshan rgya mtshos thams cad du brgyan pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul/ de bzhin
45b2(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings rgya mtsho'i gzhi gang chen mtsho thams cad kyi rgyan dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyan tshad med pa thugs skad cig gis yang dag par ston cing / chos kyi dbyings dang kaM 'jig rten
45b3(phal chen): gyi khams thams cad du/ bsam gyis mi khyab par 'gengs pas/ sangs rgyas kyi ting 'dzin rgya mtsho'i spyod pa rnam par gzigs pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul/ de bzhin
45b4(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan pad+mo'i gzhi dang / rgyan gyis me tog ri rab rgya mtsho'i 'od zer rin po che'i gzhi sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa las byung ba dang / rnam par snang mdzad kyi sprul pa rgya mtsho mi zad pa'i
45b5(phal chen): 'od kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin ga/ shegs pa'i dbu la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dpal rin po che dri ma med par sang+yas kyi 'od sna tshogs de bzhin gshegs pa
45b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi seng ge'i khri dang / rgyan dang sangs rgyas kyi sku'i gzugs brnyan khong na srel cing / rin po che'i 'od 'phro ba'i gni rgya mtsho dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos khyu mchog gi mthu phyung ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi tshul gyis
45b7(phal chen): zhing rgya mtsho thams cad du snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rnam par grol ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan bai DUr+ya'i rin po che'i me tog dang / 
45b8(phal chen): gser gyi pad+mo las chos kyi 'od ze gyi sprin dang / rin po che'i rgyas sgron ma ltar de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'od rnam par dag pas snang ba'i rgyan bstan pas/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du dmigs shing rnam
46a1(phal chen): par bkyebs mdad cing sangs rgyas kyi dbu'i rin po che'i sprin dang / rdo rje 'od 'phro ba'iri/ 'od zer stug po'i sprin gyis chos kyi dbyings la 'jug cing / chos rgya mtsho'i tshul gyis rnam pa
46a2(phal chen): 'phrul pas snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'khor lo rtsibs stong pa rin po che'i 'od zer sna tshogs tshad med pa dang ldan cing rnam pa thams cad du
46a3(phal chen): rnam par dag la dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad kyi phyogs bcu thams cad du shes rab kyi nyi ma shin tu gsal ba dang / ye shes kyi 'od kyi chos rgya mtsho'i dbyangs dang ldan pa sangs rgyas kyi gdung rnam par dag pa'i sprin ces
46a4(phal chen): bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshe gas pa'i mtshan rin po che'i 'phreng ba rnam par bkye ba dang / rin po che'i me tog dang / rin po che bai DUr+ya'i 'ong du 'phro ba'i sangs
46a5(phal chen): rgyas kyi 'od seng ge rnam par snang ba'i mthu dang ldan pas// chos kyi/ dbyings thams cad du rnam par gnon pa'i mtshan rgya mtsho'i/ sprin gyi rdul gcig las sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul snyed
46a6(phal chen): du yang dag par 'phro bas/ sangs rgyas kyi mtshan yang dag par ston cing de'i dkyil 'khor gyi ye shes ston pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi mtshan dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang
46a7(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de kho na thug su chud pa'i mtshan nyid rin po che'i rgyan rnam par dag pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi snying po tshad med pa dang /

46b1(phal chen): ba dang / rin po che'i rgyal po 'od zer brgya pa kun tu snyoms par dpal gyi sprin gyis// chos kyi dbyings dang / namakha' khyab pa'i sangs rgyas kyi 'od zer snang bas// zhing dang 'jig rten mang por de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs
46b2(phal chen): pa'i 'od rnam par snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas kyi snang ba rin po che thams cad kyi 'od 'phro ba'i sgron ma chos kyi dbyings kyi 'khor
46b3(phal chen): lo'i rgyud kyis kun tu rnam par dag pas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od kyi sprin phyogs bcur bkye ba kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che'i

46b7(phal chen): cad sgrog pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad sgrog pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyan yongs su dag pas/ zhing thams cad/

47a1(phal chen): kyi sprul pa mang po kun tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbul de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i sprin chos kyi dbyings thams cad du bsgrubs pa mi mang
47a2(phal chen): pa phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du bzhugs pa'i 'od rab tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhi/ 
47a3(phal chen): gshegs pa thams cad dang / sems can rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa'i tshul mang po chos kyi dbyings thams cad du snang ba'i sangs rgyas kyi sprin kun tu mched pa dang / rin po che'i sprin
47a4(phal chen): gyi sgron ma'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i da shu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan ye shes kun tu yangs pa nga'i sangs rgyas kyis dang / byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor
47a5(phal chen): dang chos rgya mtsho lam tshad med pa dang / zhing gi dkyil 'khor dang / byang chub sems dpa'i sngob/ sems can gyi rgyud thams cadakyi bsam pa ci bzhin du/ sangs rgyas kyi spyod yul gyis zhugs pa dang / 
47a6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i smon lam dang / spyod pa'i nga ros sangs rgyas kyi ye shes kyi gzhi kun gyi mthar thug cing thams cad mngon par mkhyen pas// chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu thug par 'gyur ba'i
47a7(phal chen): sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan chos kyi dbyings dang / namakha'i dbyings thams cad du rin po che snang ba'i sprin yid du 'ong ba/ snying po byang chub kyi gzugs brnyan
47a8(phal chen): yongs su ston par mngon par 'phags pas/ byang chub sems dpa' dang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku'i yang dag par ston pa'i sprin kun tu bkye bas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du sprin gyi 'od du gnas
47b1(phal chen): ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsug tor 'od kun tu snang ba tshad med pa ston pas byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od rnam par dag
47b2(phal chen): pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par gnon pa dang / gzi chen pos chos kyi dbyings kyi gzhi kun tu snang bar rin po che'i rgyal po ltar// 'od kun nas 'byung ba yongs su grub ste/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du 'od zer
47b3(phal chen): gyi sprin dang / 'od kyi rgyan phyogs thams cad snang bas rnam par snang bar byung zhing / byang chub sems dpa' rgya mtsho dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stob shin tu 'phel ba'i mthu dang / sangs rgyas kyi rnam par gnon pa'i sprin
47b4(phal chen): gyi phyogs bcu'i zhing gi dra ba dang / na mkha'i khams thams cad rgyas bar khyab pa'i byang chub kyi sems rin po che'i 'od zer gyi sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i dbu la de bzhin
47b5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan gtsug tor dbu'i gtsug nas mtho ba/ rim gyis mngon par 'phags shing 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang rin po che'i tshon gyis kha dog sa so nas sna tshogs kyi 'od dang ldan
47b6(phal chen): par gyur pa/ gser gyi thig le dri ma med pa'i mig 'phrul gyis kun nas shin tu brgyan pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na bzhugs pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad thugs kyi skad cig re re la yongs su ston
47b7(phal chen): ba'i sprin gyis kun tu khyab par khyab cing / zhing gi dkyil 'khor snang bar gyur pas/ zhing gi dkyil 'khor byang chub sems dpa'i gnas su gyur pa rgyan thams cad kyi rab tu brgyan pa kun tu snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs
47b8(phal chen): ba'i gtsug tor mtshan sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi rgyan du gyur cing // chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi rgyan du gyur pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas kyi mdze sbru la de bzhin gshegs
48a1(phal chen): pa'i mtshan// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho thams cad kyi 'od rab tu snang ba/ rin po che thams cad mdog lngar snang ba nyi ma dang zla ba ltar snang zhing shin tu rnam par dag pas/ phyogs bcur 'od zer
48a2(phal chen): mtsho rab tu 'gyed pa kun nas rin po che'i 'od zer 'byung ba/ 'od kun tu snang ba/ dpal kun tu rgyas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi sku rab tu 'bar ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i me tog shin tu rgyas shing / rin po che'i sprin chen po
48a3(phal chen): shin tu 'gyed pa phyogs kyi 'khor thams cad du rnam par snang zhing / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos rgya mtsho thams cad kyi dbyangs kyi sgra/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad du shin tu 'phags pa'i mar me rab tu snang bas/ 
48a4(phal chen): rin po che'i rgyal po'i me tog kun tu rgyas shing chos kyi dbyings than/ sa cad rgyas pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga' ba'o// de bzhin gshe gas pa'i spyan la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ mtshan rin po che
48a5(phal chen): sna tshogs sems can gyi khams su chags pa med pa'i ye shes kyi spyan rnam par dag pas grub pa/ 'od 'phro ba'i sprin rin po che dngul gyi mdog tu kun tu ston pas rnam par 'phrul pa'i sprin ces
48a6(phal chen): bya ba mnga'o// / de bzhin gshegs pa'i shangs la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis yongs su dag pas/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od dang / mdog dang kha dog dang ldan par gyur pa de bzhin
48a7(phal chen): thugasu chud pa// rin po che'i me tog gi sprin gyis kun tu rgyas shing / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi sangs rgyas kyi chos rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang / sems can gyi 'jig rten thams cad mngon par mkhyen pa'i
48a8(phal chen): ye shes kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// sangs rgyas kyi ljags yangs pa la 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad ljags yangs pa'i sprin gyis kun tu khyab pa'i mtshan nyid yongs su rdzogs pa'i dge ba'i rtsa bas yongs
48b1(phal chen): grub pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi rgyal po'i gzhi las 'od 'phros pas chos kyi dbyings thams cad rnam par snang mdzad pa'i ngang tshul can/ 'das pa dang / ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sems kyi gzugs brnyan dang / de
48b2(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi rgyan thams cad shin tu ston pa'i gsung dang ldan pa'i sangs rgyas kyi mtshan gyi ljags yangs pa'i sgo rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog dang / mdog gis rab tu brgyan pa'i
48b3(phal chen): 'od zer rgya mtsho bsam gyis mi khyab pa rab tu snang ba/ bzhad mo 'dzum pas phyogs bcur rab tu bkye zhing 'gro ba thams cad shin tu dang ste/ rin po che'i rgyal po'i 'od 'phro bas rab tu brgyan par/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
48b4(phal chen): gsung sna tshogs rnam par dag pa rab tu brjod cing / shin tu rgya che ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho thams cad du/ chos kyi nga ro// 'byin pa bskal pa tshad med par/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sgra 'byin pa
48b5(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings gnas pa thams cad dung ro yangs pa 'byin pa/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du dbyangs shin tu sgrog cing snang ba yang dag par ston pa'i dbyangs kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de
48b6(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa'i ljags kyi 'og gi drung na de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che sna tshogs thams cad ltar snang zhing mdzod spu yongs su 'khyil pa'i dbyibs lta bu/ rin po che thams cad kyi rang bzhin lta bu/ sangs
48b7(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor phyogs bcu nas btang ba'i dbyangs dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi sbubs can ljags kyi mtshan nyid yongs su dag pa/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad kyi rdul gyi

49a1(phal chen): rin po che gser gyi 'od 'phro bas/ sangs rgyas rgya mtsho'i dbyings thams cad du snang zhing yid du 'ong ba'i rin po che'i rgyal po'i dbyangs kyi yan lag 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad
49a2(phal chen): du sgrog cing gsung snyan pa'i ro myong bas/ sems can go bar mdzad cing bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab par mnyan du yod par dbyangs kyi yan lag gi sgra yang dag pa s+ho// de sprin sems can thams cad la yid du 'ong /

49a4(phal chen): gsung rin po che'i rgyal pos kun nas brgyan cing sna tshogs su gyurapas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi dbyings kyi glong du bsngags pa rab tu 'jug pa rnam par phye ba gzhan dang gzhan du/ byang chub

49b2(phal chen): gyi rgyan gyis chos kyi dbyings yangs pa 'od zer snang ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo sna tshogs kyi de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems/ mche ba rin po tshe rnam pa thams cad du mdzes par byung ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i
