49b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi tshims mche ba de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin ces bya ba dmanga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshams mche ba g.yas pa gong ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rdo rje spos kyi 'od 'phro ba'i/ 
49b5(phal chen): sprin kun tu snang ba'i 'od zer rin po che'i rgyal po rnam par snang ba snying po can chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyi tshad kyis klo ba rin po che'i 'od zer sna tshogs rab tu bkye ba'i 'od zer re re'i khongasu
49b6(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rnam par 'phrul pa chud par ston pa/ zhing thams cad kyi snying po byang chub kyi rgyan gyi sprin kun tu nar cing me chad pas 'od kyi sprin rin po che'i 'od du 'phro ba ri rab kyi snying po can
49b7(phal chen): zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa 'og ma la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan tha dad pa'i mtshan nyid shin tu ston pas/ spos dang rin po che yid du 'ong ba'i me tog sna tshogs thams
49b8(phal chen): cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul sna tshogs kyi 'khor lo dang / rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer rnam par snang ba kun tu 'phro ba'i sgron ma dri ma med pa'i sprin yang dag par bstan pas/ 'jig rten gyi khams rgya mtsho
50a1(phal chen): thams cad du rab tu gsal bas/ rnam par snang zhing de bzhin gshegs pa gang na seng ge'i khri bad+mo'i snying po can/ dri ma mang ba la bzhugs pa'i sprin/ byang chub sems
50a2(phal chen): dpa'i rgya mtsho'i dbyings su/ rin po che sna tshogs thams cad kyi ri rab kyi mar me rab tu snang ba'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems mche ba g.yon pa gong ma la// de bzhin gshegs pa'i ma
50a3(phal chen): rin po che gser gyi 'od sna tshogs kun nas rnam par dag pa/ 'dzam bu chu klung gi rin po che'i rgyud kyi dra ba'i 'khor lo dang / rin po che'i me tog shin tu snang ba'i 'khor lo sna tshogs yongs su 'khyil ba/ chos kyi

50a5(phal chen): brgyan thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan gyi sprin zad mi shes pa kun tu mched par 'gyed pas/ chos rgya mtsho rab tu sgrog pa'i sangs rgyas kyi gsung dang / rin po che thams cad kyi tshon du snang
50a6(phal chen): ba'i sangs rgyas nam mkha'i dbyings la// gsung gi sgra 'byin pa/ chos kyi sgron ma'i 'od/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i sprin du snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshems kyi mtshams na/ de bzhin
50a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i mtshan tshems kyi mtshams thams cad mtshan gcig par me tog gi mtshan dang / rgya mtsho'i sgo'i mtshan gyi sprin rin po che thams cad kyi kha dog tu 'dal ba las/ rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho
50a8(phal chen): rab tu tu 'gyed cing / bzhad mo 'dzum pas/ sangs rgyas kyi 'od nor bu rin po che'i 'od du 'phro ba g.yas phyogs su 'khyil zhing / chos kyi dbyings rgyas par khyab par rin po che'i 'od zer rgya mtsho khongs su chud
50b1(phal chen): ba'i snying po can gyis/ sangs rgyas kyi tshems kyi mtshams thams cad rgyas par gang bas/ skad cig tu 'od kyis rgyas par kun tu rgyu ba'i 'od zer/ sangs rgyas kyi gsung gi dkyil 'khor rgya mtsho kun tu
50b2(phal chen): 'gyed pa'i sprin snang ba zhes bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i spros la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan 'dzam bu chu klung gi gser dang / pad+mo'i mdog dang / 'od ltar snang ba/ chos kyi dbyings thams cad
50b3(phal chen): du mdangs rab tu snang bas dpal phun sum tshogs pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi 'od zer dang mdangs kyi kun tu khyab par rnam par snang zhing / gser dang / pad+mo'i mdog yongs su dag pas kun tu spangs
50b4(phal chen): pas// rin po che thams cad kyi mdangs dang / mdog tu snang ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mgur la/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan dung gi mgur/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'od lam ma
50b5(phal chen): lam mer yongs su snang bas mdog shin tu gsal zhing / gan thams cad rin po che'i rgyal pos rnam par snang bar byas pas// phyogs thams cad du rnam par gsal ba'i 'od zer rab tu 'a
50b6(phal chen): cing / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi snang bar mdzad pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa g.yas pa la/ de ba zhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rin po che thams cad kyi 'od dang / gser

50b8(phal chen): rgung pa'i sprin rab tu snang bas/ sangs rgyas rab tu mang po thams cad snying por byas pa/ rin po che thams cad kyi gzhi dang ldan pa'i sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku phrag pa'i dbus na/

51b3(phal chen): la gnas pa'i dpal rgya mtsho kun gyi gzhung gi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// de bzhin gshegs pa'i dpal gyi be'u'i g.yas phyogs mdab chags na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan// chos kyi dbyings rnam par dag pa'i

52a8(phal chen): mtshan rgya mtshos yongs su gang ba'i rin po che rgya mtsho'i nang na// zhing thams cad gzugs brnyan du 'khor bar ston cing / byang chub sems dpa' sprin gzhan dang gzhan mngon par phyung bas chos kyi dbyings rnam par snang
52b1(phal chen): ba'i sprin kun tu ston pa'i 'od kyi sprin ces bya ba mnga'o// rje su 'gro ba'i dpal gyi be'u bzhi pa la de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan mtshan nyid kyi rnam pa rgya mtshos chos kyi dbyings thams cad du de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam pa

61a1(phal chen): de dag 'di snyam du gyur te/ bdag gis byang chub sems dpa' de ma mthong ngam// de dang ma smras te/ bag dbab pa mthob na/ sems skad cig du yang dga' ldan gyi gnas na 'khod
61a2(phal chen): par dga' ba'i sems bskyed pa'i mchis 'dzam bu'i gling du mi 'dod du mi rung ngo zhes nas/ lha'i bu de dag re re zhing yang lha'i bu mo bye ba phrag bcu'i 'khor dang bcas te 'dong bar byas pa dang / lha'i bu de dag gis de
61a3(phal chen): ltar 'dong pa'i sems bskyed ma thag tu/ lha'i rnga de las sgra 'byung ba/ lha'i sras po dag byang chub sems dpa' de ni skye ba'ang med/ shi 'pho ba'ang med de/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po dag ni/ shi 'pho
61a4(phal chen): ba med pa'i mngon par shes pa dang ldan pa dag ste/ de dag ni sems can rnam ras kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du/ mig lam du snang bar 'gyur ro// lha'i sras po dag 'di lta ste dper na/ bdag ni khyed kyi
61a5(phal chen): mig lam gyis mi mthong ste/ mig gi lam las 'das kyang lha'i sras po khyed la sgra brjod do// lha'i sras po dag de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin dri ma dang bral ba la nya par bzhag pa
61a6(phal chen): ni mig gis snang ba ma yin yang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad du snang ste/ 'on kyang byang chub sems dpa' la rtog pa med do// rnam par rtog pa med do// g.yo ba med do// sems pa med do// de bas na lha'i sras
61a7(phal chen): po dag khyed kyis// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems skyed la bsam pa yongs su sbyong ste/ spyod pa la mnos la las kyi sgrib pa dang / nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang / rnam par smin pa'i sgrib pa dang / 
61a8(phal chen): lta ba'i sgrib pa bshags pa gyis te/ lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kun tu bzang po chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pas sems can gyi khams su ming dang lus byin gyis rlobs shig/ sems can
61b1(phal chen): gyi khams dang / mnyam pa'i lus kyis sems can gyi khams dang / mnyam pa'i mgo byin gyis rlob shig/ sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i mgos sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i lce byin gyis rlob
61b2(phal chen): shig/ sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i lces sgrib pa de dag nyes pa la nyes par shog shig/ de skad ces brjod pa dang / lha'i bu de dag ngo mtshar dang rmad du gyur te/ rab tu dga' zhing sems bde bar gyur nas/ 
61b3(phal chen): yang lha'i rnga de la byang chub sems dpa' rnams sdig pa 'chags pa'i rnam pa ji lta bu zhig yod ces phyir 'dri'o// de nas lha'i rnga de byang chub sems dpa' de'i ting 'dzin gyi byin rlabs dang / lha'i bu de dag gi dge ba'i
61b4(phal chen): rtsa ba'i stobs dang / byin gyi brlabs kyis rnam pa 'di lta bu'i sgra 'byin to// lha'i sras po dag/ las ni shar phyogs nas 'ongs te/ sems la gnas pa ma yin/ 'dug pa ma yin/ tshogs su bsags pa ma
61b5(phal chen): yin/ phung por gyur pa ma yin te/ lho phyogs nas ma yin/ nub phyogs nas/ ma yin/ byang phyogs nas ma yin// las de ni phyogs bcu ku/ na nas kyang 'ongs te gnas ma yin no// de ltar de ni byang
61b6(phal chen): chub sems dpas phyin ci log las byung ba ste/ gnas med par yang dag par shes pas de'i phyir de la 'gyod pa med do// lha'i sras po dag 'di lta ste dper na/ lha'i rnga bdag ni las kyi rnam par smin pa ji
61b7(phal chen): lta ba dang / spyod pa ji lta ba dang / tshul khrims ji lta ba dang / dga' ba ji lta ba dang / shin tu byang ba ji lta ba dang / ting 'dzin ji lta ba bzhin du bdag ces brjod do// lha'i sras po dag de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom
61b8(phal chen): ldan 'das rnams dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyang bdag ces bya ba 'am/ bdag gi zhes bya ba 'am/ sems can zhes bya bar gsung brjod cing / 'dod chags dang / zhe sdang dang / gti mug dang / las dang / 
62a1(phal chen): bya ba'i gsung yang rjod de/ lnga'i sras po dag bdag ces bya ba med do// bdag med par bdag gi zhes bya ba mi dmigs so// de dag gi las kyi rnam pa lam gyi rgyung drug du na ma
62a2(phal chen): par smin par 'gyur bar byas pa de dag kyang shar phyogs nas mi dmigs so// lho phyogs nas ma yin/ nub phyogs nas ma yin/ byang phyogs nas ma yin te/ phyogs bcu kun nas kyang dmigs par mi rung ngo // 
62a3(phal chen): lha'i sras po dag 'di lta ste/ dper na/ bdag gi sgra ni lha'i bu yongs su ma dag pa rnams kyi rna lam du mi 'gro bas/ sems can dmyal ba nas bskul kyang thos par mi 'gyur te/ sgra de ni ma skyes me'u gags pa'o
62a4(phal chen): lha'i sras po dag de bzhin du las thams cad kyang ma skyes ma 'gags pa ste/ ji ltar yongs su sbyangs pa dang / ji ltar bsags pa'i tshul du 'bras bu'ang rnam par smin par byed de/ lha'i sras
62a5(phal chen): po dag 'di lta ste dper na/ bdag gi sgra ni bskal pa khrag khrig du brjod kyang rnam par rtog pa med pas zad pa med do// thugs pa med do// 'gro ba med do// 'ong ba med do// lha'i sras
62a6(phal chen): po dag gang la 'gro ba dang / 'ong ba yod pa de dag la ni rtag pa'am chad pa dag kyang yod par snang ste/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams ni ldem po dag gis// sems can smin par mdzad pa'i don du ston pa
62a7(phal chen): ma gtogs par rtag pa'am chad pa'i chos ston pa mi mdzad do// lha'i sras po dag 'di lta ste dper na/ sgra de ni bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med par dbyangs kyis go bar byed do// lha'i
62a8(phal chen): sras po dag de bzhin du sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyang sems can rnams kyi bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du mngon du ston pa mdzad do// lha'i sras po dag 'di lta ste dper na/ shel gyi me
62b1(phal chen): long gi dkyil 'khor sgron ma zhes bya ba/ 'jig rten gyi khams bcu'i tshad dang mnyam pa dag cing gsal la mdog shin tu bzang ba yod de/ de la 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa dag nas kyang / ri thams
62b2(phal chen): cad kyi gzugs brnyan dang / sems can de dag thams cad kyi gzugs brnyan yang rab tu snang na/ lha'i sras po dag de la ji snyam du sems// de ltar me long gi dkyil 'khor de la// sems can dmyal ba
62b3(phal chen): dang / byol song gi skye gnas pa dang / gshin rje'i 'jig rten pa'i sems can mang po snang bas yongs su ma dag par mi 'gyur ram/ lus shin tu mi sdug par gnas pa de dag kyang / me long de la 'phos pa 'am/ 
62b4(phal chen): gnas pa 'am/ sems dang ldan par gyur pa yod dam med/ smras pa de lta bu ni med do// smras pa lha'i sras po dag de bzhin du/ las rnams kyang 'pho ba yang med do// 'gro ba yang med/ gan+da
62b5(phal chen): pa yang med de/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par smin pa yang mi snang ba ma yin no// 'di lta ste dper na sgyu ma ni mig sgrub byed do// lha'i sras po dag de bzhin du gang gis las rnams shes te/ 
62b6(phal chen): mthong ba dang / khong du chud pa de dag gi sdig pa bshags pani shin tu rnam par dag par 'gyur ro// shin tu bstan pa 'di bstan pa'i tshe/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong
62b7(phal chen): gi rdul shin tu phra ba skad kyi dga' ldan gnas kyi lha'i bu de dag thams cad mi skye ba'i chos la bzod pa rab tu thob par gyur to// 'dod pa la spyod pa'i lha'i ris drug gi lha'i bu tshad med grangs mang bsam
62b8(phal chen): gyis mi khyab pa dag gis kyang / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu sems bskyed do// 'dod pa la spyod pa'i lha'i ris drug po de dag gi lha'i bu mo rnams kyang bud med kyi lus de las
63a1(phal chen): gyur te/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nges par gyur to// de nas lha'i bu de dag gis kun tu bzang po'i yongasu bsngo bas rgya cher bshags te/ sa bcu 'thob pa dang / 
63a2(phal chen): ting 'dzin stobs kyi rkyen yongs su 'thob pa'i don du/ sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i lus kyi las dang / ngag gi las dang / yid kyi las kyis rgya cher bshags pa byas nas/ de dag las kyi sgrib pa rnam par
63a3(phal chen): dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong / rin po che bdun gyi pad+mo rdul shin tu phra ba snyed la 'khod cing 'od chen po rab tu gtong ba mthong bar gyur te/ de dag gi dpe byad bzang po re re nas
63a4(phal chen): kyang sems can gyi khams dang / mnyam pa'i 'od zer mang po byung ste/ 'od zer de dag la yang sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs shing / sems can rnams la bsam
63a5(phal chen): pa ji lta ba bzhin du chos smon pa mthong bar gyur kyang / de tsam gyis/ ting 'dzin dri ma dang bral ba'i spyod yul gyi cha shas tsam yang legs par mthong bar ma gyur to// de nas lha'i bu de dag
63a6(phal chen): gis me tog gi sprin la sogs pa snga ma de dag dang / ba spu'i bu ga re re nas kyang sems can gyi khams dang mnyam pa'i me tog gi sprin me ngon par sprul te/ byang chub sems dpa' rnam par snang mdzad dang / de bzhin
63a7(phal chen): gshegs pa mtha' yas pa la mchod ge 'gyur to// me tog ji snyed cig gtor ba de dag thams cad kyang de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs su gnas par gyur to// spos kyi sprin gyi char rab tu phab pa de dag gi
63a8(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing tshad med pa'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyad du sems can gang gis lus la bab pa de dag kyang 'od lta ste dper na/ bsam gtan bzhi pa la mnyam par bzhag pa'i dge slong gi
63b1(phal chen): lus kyi bde de lta bu dang ldan par gyur to// gang la las kyi bsgribs pa'i nyes pa med pa de dag ni spos kyi dri de tshor ba tsam gyis/ gzugs dang / sgra dang / dri dang / ro dang / reg bya las byung ba'i nyon mongs pa thams cad byang
63b2(phal chen): bar gyur te/ nang gi dngos po'i nyon mongs pa lnga brgya dang / phyi rol gyi dngos po'i nyon mongs pa lnga brgya dang / 'dod chags la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / zhe sdang la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa
63b3(phal chen): stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / gti mug la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gcig dang / de bzhin du 'phral gyi 'dod chags la spyod pa dang / 
63b4(phal chen): 'phral gyi zhe sdang la spyod pa dang / 'phral gyi gti mug la spyod pa dang / 'bral gyi cha mnyam pa la spyod pa'i nyon mongs pa dang / mi shes pa de dag thams cad kyang byang bar gyur to// gang gis 'od
63b5(phal chen): zer spos kyi phung po gzi brjid rnam stsal ba'i 'od rab tu 'tho ba pa'i don du dge ba'i rtsa ba yongs su sbyangs shing bskyed pa de dag gis gdugs kyi sprin de dag mig lam du mthong bar gyur te/ 
63b6(phal chen): de dag gis kyang 'khor los sgyur ba chu klung 'gang 'ga'i bye ma snyed kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed par gyur to// de ni 'di ltar 'khor los sgyur ba'i sa gser gyi dra bas dag pa 'thob pa'i phyir dge ba'i rtsa ba rab
63b7(phal chen): tu bskyed par gyur te/ de la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgya smin bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed du 'khor los sgyur ba byed do// der sa su
63b8(phal chen): can mang po yongs su smin par 'gyur ro// 'di lta ste dper na/ bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa 'khor lo'i blo gros kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams me long gi dkyil 'a
64a1(phal chen): ltar snang ba zhes bya ba de na/ bcom ldan 'das de'i sprul pa/ dge slong pha dang / dge slong ma dang / dge bsnyen pa dang / dge bsnyen ma'i gzugs dang / gzhung de bzhin du skyes pa'i
64a2(phal chen): rabs kyi sde'i khyad par thams cad kyis 'jig rten gyi khams tshad med pa dag tu mi 'gro ba de lta bu'i skad cig med do// thang cig med do// yud tsam med do// de bzhin gshegs pa de'i mtshan kyang grag ste/ 
64a3(phal chen): thos nas kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing der skye bar 'gyur ro// de bzhin du 'khor los sgyur ba'i sa sar gyi dra bas dag pa la gnas pa'i byang chub sems dpa' rnam par 'phrul pa shin tu gsal ba'i mtshams med pa'i
64a4(phal chen): 'od zer gyis phogs pa'i sems can de dag thams cad kyang dge ba'i rtsa de dag gis sems can yongs su 'dul shing sa bcu 'thob par 'gyur ro// 'di lta ste dper na/ tshad med pa'i bsam gtan thob pa ni/ 
64a5(phal chen): ji srid du bsam gtan yongs su nyams par ma gyur pa/ de srid du tshangs pa/ 'i gzhal med khang yang mthong la/ tshangs pa'i 'jig rten na bde ba gang yod pa de dag kyang myong ba yin/ de bzhin du byang
64a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' 'khor los sgyur ba'i sa gser gyi dra bas dag pa la gnas pa'i gtsug gi rin po che'i 'od kyis su la phog par gyur pa de dag sa bcu 'thob par 'gyur te/ chos tshad med pa snang ba chen po
64a7(phal chen): 'ang rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// stobs rnam par dag pa'i ting 'dzin shin tu bsgrubs pa'i phyir mig yongs su sbyangs pa bcu'ang rab tu 'thob par 'gyur ro// gzhung de bzhin du yid yongs su sbyangs pa bcu
64a8(phal chen): yang rab tu 'thob ste/ sha'i mig rnam par dag pa 'di lta ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed cig rdul shin tu phra bar bya ste/ rdul shin tu phra mo de dag byed
64b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa' de dag gis lag pa g.yon pas blangs te khyer la de snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams 'das pa dang / rdul gcig bor te/ de ltar gcig nas gcig tu bzhag pa'i tshul dang thabs de lta bur 'grang ba'i
64b2(phal chen): tshul gyis shar phyogs su rdul de dag thams cad zad par gyur la de lta bu'i tshul du gang du bor ba dang / gang du ma bor ba'i 'jig rten gyi khams de dag thams cad shin tu phra ba'i rdul du glags la de ltar mang ba'i rdul
64b3(phal chen): shin tu phra ba de dag kyang khyer te/ shar phyogs logs su 'jig rten gyi khams 'das nas/ rdul shin tu phra ba gcig bor la tshul de 'dra bar phyogs bcu kun tu rdul shin tu phra de dag zad par gyur nas/ 
64b4(phal chen): de snyed kyi 'jig rten de dag thams cad gcig tu sdoms te/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig gi chu nang du gyur na/ lag na rin po che de la ji snyam du sems sangs rgyas kyi zhing de che zhing tshad med la bsam gyis
64b5(phal chen): mi khyab pa yin nam/ gsol pa bcom ldan 'das de ni de bzhin te/ btsun pa bcom ldan 'das gang gis dpe bstan pa'i 'di thos par gyur la/ thos nas kyang glo ba ches shing ngo mtshar
64b6(phal chen): gyi 'du shes dang / rmad kyi 'du shes skyed pa mchis na/ sems can de dag kyang ngo mtshar dang ldan par 'gyur ro// bka' stsal pa/ lag na rin po che de de bzhin no// de de bzhin te/ lag na rin po che khyod kyis rdza
64b7(phal chen): skad du smras pa bzhin no// lag na rin po che rigs kyi bu dang / rigs kyi bu mo de dag ni ngas bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lung bsten pa/ de lta bu dag ni sangs rgyas kyi ye shes thob par gyur to// 
64b8(phal chen): red do// 'gyur ro// lag na rin po che 'di lta ste dper na/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing bye ba phrag stong gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing ji snyed pa de snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis dra
65a1(phal chen): rgyas kyi zhing dper rnam par bkod pa de dag thams cad kyang // rdul shin tu phra bar glags la/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing re re zhing yang sangs rgyas kyi zhing de dag na/ rdul shin tu phra ba ji snyed
65a2(phal chen): yod pa de snyed kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing zhig yod par gyur te/ zhing de dag na ji lta ba de bzhin du zhing thams cad na'ang de snyed cig yod par gyur la/ rdul de dag thams cad kyang tshul de bzhin du bkod de/ rnam grangs 'di/ 
65a3(phal chen): 'dra bar rdul shin tu phra bar dgod pa'i tshul gyis lan brgyad bcur bsgres te/ rdul gyi 'bru re re la yang zhing thams cad kyi rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'bras bu mngon par grub par gyur kyang / de dag thams cad byang
65a4(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i sha'i mig gis bsgribs pa med par mthong ste/ lag na rin po che byang chub sems dpa'i sha'i mig las kyi rnam par smin pas yongs su grub pa des ni/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing khrag
65a5(phal chen): khrig brgya'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa sems skad/ cig gis mthong ste/ de ni 'jig rten gyi khams bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyi 'jig rten gyi khams la dbang sgyur zhing
65a6(phal chen): 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po'i sa gser gyi dra bas dag pa thob pa'i bsod nams rnam par smin pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba dang / ting 'dzin gyis yongs su grub pa'i shel gyi me long sgron ma zhes bya ba mdog
65a7(phal chen): dag ste/ bzang zhing gsal ba bzhin no// // shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo sangs rgyas pha la che zhes bya ba las// dpe byad bzang po'i 'od zer bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi bcu rtsa gcig pa'o// 
65a8(phal chen): bam po drug cu dgu pa// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos/ byang chub sems dpa' de dag la spras pa/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ni sems can gyi snod ji lta ba bzhin du yang dag par rdzogs/ 
65b1(phal chen): pa'i sangs rgyas la dmigs ste/ rdul tsam zhig brjod du zad do// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems can mi mkhas pa 'gyod pas kun nas non pa/ bdag dang bdag gir bya ba la mngon par zhen pa/ 
65b2(phal chen): 'jig tshogs la shin tu chags pa phyin ci log la rab tu rten pa// the tsom la rab tu gzhol ba log par lta ba yongs su rtog pas byung ba/ rmongs pas bsgrubs pa/ 'khor ba'i rgyud du gzhol ba de bzhin gshegs
65b3(phal chen): pa'i lam dang / mi ldan pa rnams kyi don du/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams 'jig rten du 'byung ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras dag 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' gzhan la zhe sdang skyed pa tsam du kha na ma tho
65b4(phal chen): bache ba'i chos ni 'ga' tsam yang bdag gis ma mthong ste/ de ci'i phyir zhe/ na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag gzhan la khong khro ba skyed pa'i byang chub sems dpa' ni sgrib pa'i chos kyi sgo brgya stong phrag bcu
65b5(phal chen): po 'di dag yongs su 'dzin par 'gyur te// brgya stong phrag bcu gang na na 'di lta ste/ byang chub sems dpa' mi mthong ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// chos mi thos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// 'jig
65b6(phal chen): rten gyi khams kun nas nyon mongs par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// ngan song du gnas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// mi khom par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// nang mang ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// skur pa mang ba 'dzin
65b7(phal chen): par 'gyur ro// ngang tshul gyi mi gsal ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// brjed ngas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// blo chung ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// mig gi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// rna ba'i sgrib pa 'dzin par
65b8(phal chen): 'gyur ro// sna'i slob pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// lce'i sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// lus kyi sgrub pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// yid kyi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sdig pa'i bshes gnyen 'dzin par 'gyur/ 
66a1(phal chen): sdig pa'i grogs po 'dzin par 'gyur ro// theg pa dmar ba dang 'dre ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// skye bo ma rabs dang phrad ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// bdag nyid che ba'i skye bo la ro/ 
66a2(phal chen): pa med par 'gyur ro// yang dag pa'i lta ba mi mthong mi rnyed pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// mu stegs can gzhan gyi nang du skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// bdud kyi yul dang snyan pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi
66a3(phal chen): bstan pa dang ring du 'gyur ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// dge ba'i bshes gnyen mi mthong ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// dge ba'i rtsa ba'i bar du 'gyur ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// mi dge ba'i chos rnam par 'phel ba 'dzin par
66a4(phal chen): 'gyur ro// skye mched dma' ba 'thob pa 'dzin par 'gyur/  ro// mtha' 'khob kyi yul du gnas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// mi'i nang na kun ldo byed par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// lha'i nang
66a5(phal chen): na mi srun par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// klu dang gnodadang / dri za dang lha ma yin dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / srin po mi srun par skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sangs
66a6(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos la dad pa med pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byis pa'i chos la brten pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// theg pa dma' ba la mos pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// theg pa chen po la yid ches pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// 
66a7(phal chen): bskal par gnas pas 'jigs pa mang ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// 'khor bas skyo ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos la spong ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi rnam par 'phrul ba yongs
66a8(phal chen): mi 'dzin pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'a'i dbang po la dga' ba med pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa' dang / spyod pa la thun mong du spyad pa mi 'thob pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang
66b1(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i bsam pa yongs su ma dag pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i lhag pa'i bsam pazhum zhing dma' ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa yongs
66b2(phal chen): mi 'dus par 'gyur ro// yongs su sgyid lug pas rab tu zhig pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// las kun nas nyon mongs pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// rnam par smin pa ma dag pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// ye shes kyi stobs
66b3(phal chen): bdag nyid che ba ma yin pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// ye shes kyi rgyud byang bar mi nus pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rgyun chad pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// thams cad mkhyen pa'i gdams ngag
66b4(phal chen): yongs su mi zin pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu 'grub par mi 'gyur ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de bzhi na gshegs pa'i yul dang ring ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// bdud kyi yul
66b5(phal chen): la gnas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i/ yul lam gnas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sam/ sa dpa'i go cha la mos pa med pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub
66b6(phal chen): sems dpa'i gnas kyi 'jigs pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i dge ba'i las kyis skye ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// lta ba dang the tsom la mngon par zhen pa 'dzin par 'gyuraro// sems yongasu
66b7(phal chen): rmongs par bsgribs pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa' dang / 'grogs pa'i las drungs phyung ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i tshul khrims nyams par gyur pas tshul khrims ngan pa 'dzin
66b8(phal chen): par 'gyur ro// bzod pa'i sgo mthar ma phyin pas gnod sems dang gti mug dang / khro ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i brtson 'grus chen po las mi ldog par bya ba la zhum pa 'dzin par
67a1(phal chen): 'gyur ro// ting 'dzin mi 'thob par 'khrug pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang mi mthun pa'i phyogs shes rab 'chal pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// gnas
67a2(phal chen): dang gnas ma yin pa la mi mkhas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sems can gyi thabs la thabs mi mkhas pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes la rnam par mi dpyod pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// / 
67a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i chos kyis 'byung ba khong du mi chud pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i mig 'byam klas pa bcu'i 'grub pa'i dmus long lta bu 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sgrib pa med pa'i
67a4(phal chen): chos kyi rgyud mngon par sgrub pa glen zhing lkugs pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// dbang po gzhan dang nor ba'i dbang po 'ji ngan pas sna yongs su nyams pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sems can
67a5(phal chen): pha rol gyi tshig gi rgyud mi shes pas lce'i sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sems can gang zag pha rol la zhe sdang ba/ sa las kyi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// myos pa'i sems 'thob
67a6(phal chen): par 'gyur ba sems kyi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// sdom pa gsum dang mi ldan pas las kyi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// ngag gi nyes pa bzhis kun nas nyon mongs pas skye mched kyi sgrib pa 'dzin
67a7(phal chen): par 'gyur ro// chags sems dang / gnod sems dang / log par lta ba mang bas yid kyi las kyi sgrib pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// chos yongs su btsal ba la rku sems 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub
67a8(phal chen): sems dpa'i dmigs pa la thogs pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i mthu la shin tu zhum pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa la sgyid lug pa 'dzin par
67b1(phal chen): 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i ye shes kyi sgo snang ba rgyun 'chad pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// dran pa'i stobs dang shugs nyams chung ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de bzhin gshegs pa'i snyan pa yong/ 
67b2(phal chen): su mi 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i skyon med pa'i gnas rnam par spong ba 'dzin par 'gyur ro// byang chub sems dpa'i chud mi za ba'i gnas la mi ston pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// nyan thos
67b3(phal chen): dang rang sangs rgyas kyi skyon med pa yid kyis mchod pa 'dzin par 'gyur ro// 'das pa dang ma 'ongs pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i byang chub sems dpa'i tshul dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs dang ring ba
67b4(phal chen): 'dzin par 'gyur ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de ltar byang ngachub sems dpa' gcig la gcig ngan sems bskyed pa ni de dag la sogs pa sgrib pa'i chos kyi sgo brgya stong phrag bcu rnams
67b5(phal chen): 'dzin par 'gyur ro// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa'i theg pa la zhugs pa rna/ mas ni/ phan tshun du ngan sam chims skyed pa lta bur kha na ma tho ba che
67b6(phal chen): ba'i chos 'ga' tsam yang ma mthong ngo // de bas na rgyal ba'i sras dag byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa myur du rdzogs par bya bar 'dod pa'i byang chub sems dpas chos bcu la brtson par bya'o// bcu gang
67b7(phal chen): zhe na sems can thams cad yongs su mi gtang ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la sems su bya ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad mi spang ba dang / zhing thams cad la mi zad pa'i ye shes
67b8(phal chen): kyis 'jug pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la mos pa dang / dad pa chen po dang / na mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i chos kyi dbyings mnyam pa nyid rnam par bsgoms pa'i byang chub kyi
68a1(phal chen): sems mi gtang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs la 'jug pas/ sangs rgyas kyi byang chub la rnam par dpyad pa dang / tha dad pa yang dag par shes pa la brtson
68a2(phal chen): par bya ba dang / sems can thams cad yongs su smin par bya bas yongs su mi skyo ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du gnas pa la mngon par chags pa med pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag byang
68a3(phal chen): chub sems dpas chos bcu po de ga la mngon par brtson par bya'o// de chos bcu po de dag la gnas pas rnam par dag par byed pa'i chos bcu rab tu 'thob ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di lta ste chos zab mo
68a4(phal chen): la 'jug pa rnam par dag pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen dang 'grogs pa rnam par dag pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa yod sa su bzung ba rnam par dag pa dang / na mkha'i dbyings rnam par sgom pa
68a5(phal chen): rnam par dag pa dang / chos kyi dbyings la 'jug pa rnam par dag pa dang / mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sems rnam par dpyad pa rnam pa dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
68a6(phal chen): kyis grogs byang ba'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rnam par dag pa dang bskal pa thams cad la mngon par chags pa med pa rnam pa ra dag pa dang / dus gsum thams cad rab tu brtag pa rnam par dag pa
68a7(phal chen): dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs su nan tan bya ba rnam par dag pa ste/ rnam par dag par byed pa'i chos bcu po de dag rab tu 'dzin to// de de lta bu'i chos bcu po de dag la gnas pas// ye shes 'byam/ 
68a8(phal chen): klas pa bcu la 'jug par 'gyur te/ bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste sems can thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa la 'jug pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi las kyi rnam par smin pa rab tu phye ba la 'jug pa dang / 
68b1(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la ye shes sdang bas 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi tshul dang ldem po dag la ye shes kyi 'jug pa dang / gzungs kyi sgo thams cad la ye shes kyi 'du
68b2(phal chen): dang / ye shes thams cad la spobs pa'i ye shes kyi 'jug pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi skad dang / tha skad dang / tshig la mkhas pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams
68b3(phal chen): cad du lus bstan pa'i ye ge la 'jug pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad du gzugs brnyan 'byung ba bstan pa'i ye shes la 'jug pa dang / skye mched thams cad thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes
68b4(phal chen): la 'jug pa ste/ ye shes 'byam klas pa bcu po dag rab tu dzin to// de de ltar ye shes 'byam klas pa bcu la rab tu ga nus pas yang dag par gzud pa la 'jug pa bcu 'thob ste/ bcu gang
68b5(phal chen): zhe na 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sgra'i sbubs su gzud pa la 'jug cing / sku'i sbubs gcig 'jig rten gyi khams bsam gyis mi khyab par mngon par sgrub pa la 'jug pa dang / 
68b6(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi lus sems can gcig gi lus su bsdu zhing / sems can gcig gi lus brjod du med pa'i lus su mngon par bsgrubs pa la 'jug pa dang / bskal pa brjod du med pa sems kyi skad cig tu
68b7(phal chen): gzung ba la 'jug cing / sems kyi skad cig brjod du med pa'i bskal par 'jug pa bstan pa dang / chos gcig sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad du yang dag par gzhol ba la 'jug cing / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams
68b8(phal chen): cad chos gcig tu gzung pa la 'jug pa dang / skye mched gcig brjod du med pa'i skye mched du bya ste/ brjod du med pa'i skye mched du bya ba la 'jug cing / skye mched brjod du pa skye mched gcig tu bstan pa la 'jug pa
69a1(phal chen): pa dang / dbang po gcig brjod du med pa'i dbang por bya ba la 'jug cing / dbang po brjod du med pa dbang po gcig tu gzud pa la 'jug pa dang / dbang po thams cad dbang po med pa dang / 
69a2(phal chen): tha mi dang por 'jug cing / dbang po med pa dbang por bya ba la 'jug pa dang / 'du shes thams cad 'du shes gcig tu byin gyis brlab pa la 'jug cing / 'du shes gcig tu 'du shes thams cad du byin gyis brlab
69a3(phal chen): pa la 'jug pa dang / tshig gcig rnam par brjod tshig brjod med pa rnam par brjod par bya ba la 'jug cing / tshig rnam par brjod pa thams cad sgra gcig gi dbyangs su byin gyis brlab pa la 'jug pa dang / dus
69a4(phal chen): gsum thams cad bsam gtan gcig tu bsdu ste/ bsam gang na gcig po dus thams cad du kun tu spro bar bstan pa la 'jug pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag yang dag par gzud pa bcu po de dag sems
69a5(phal chen): kyi bsam pa bcu la gnas te/ rnam par dpyad par bya'o// bcu gang zhe na 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kyi spyod pa la mi spyod pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad
69a6(phal chen): kyi 'du shes dang / yid la byed pa la mi gnas pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / lhag pa'i bsam pa na mkha'i dbyings kyis klas pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus
69a7(phal chen): med pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa la/ mkhas pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / chos zab mo tha mi dad pa la mkhas pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas
69a8(phal chen): pa dang / dogs pa thams cad la lan med par bya ba'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / dus thams cad tha mi dad cing mnyam pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / 'das pa dang ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung
69b1(phal chen): ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad mnyam pa nyid kyi sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi stobs tshad med pa'i sems kyi bsam pa la gnas pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sems kyi bsam
69b2(phal chen): pa bcu po de dag la gnas ste/ byang chub sems dpas yang dag par gzud pa bcu po de dag rnam par dpyad par bya'o// de sems kyi bsam pa bcu po de dag la gnas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos la mkhas pa'i snang
69b3(phal chen): ba bcu 'thob po// bcu gang zhe na 'di lta ste/ sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo snang ba la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi chos yangs pa mngon par sgrub pa la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas kyi chos
69b4(phal chen): sna tshogs shin tu bstan pa la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos mnyam pa nyid la 'jug pa la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos tha dad pa'i snang ba la 'jug par
69b5(phal chen): mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos tha mi dad pa la 'jug par mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi rgyan la 'jug par mkhas pa rab tu 'thob bo// sangs rgyas
69b6(phal chen): kyi tshul gcig pa'i mos pa la 'jug par mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos mtha' yas pa'i tshul la 'jug par mkhas pa rab tu 'thob po// sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad rang gi sems la
69b7(phal chen): rag lus pas rang gi stobs dang phyir mi ldog pa la mkhas pa rab tu 'thob ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras dag sangs rgyas kyi chos la mkhas pa'i snang ba bcu po de dag rab tu 'thob po// kye rgyal ba'i sras dag de bas na/ 
69b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos chos de dag thos nas/ rim gro dang zhes chen po'i bsam pas gzung bar bya'o// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ byang chub sems dpa' chos 'di la gnas pa la ni// bla na med pa
70a1(phal chen): yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyang dkon pa ma yin te/ las gron chung ngus sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par 'grub pa'i byin gyis brlabs rab tu 'thob bo// 'das
70a2(phal chen): pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das dang / mnyam pa nyid du yang 'jug par 'gyur ro// de nas de'i tshe sangs rgyas kyi mthus/ 'jig rten gyi khams sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du
70a3(phal chen): med pa bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed rnam pa drug tu rab tu g.yos so// sangs rgyas kyi mthu dang chos nyid rab tu thob pas lha rdzas las 'das pa'i me tog gi sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// 
70a4(phal chen): lha rdzas las 'das pa'i spos kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bang po// gzhung de bzhin du phye ma dang / na bza dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / gdugs dang / nor bu rin po che dang / sbrul gyi snying po'i tsan
70a5(phal chen): ngan dang / rgyan dang lgab sgrub thams cad kyi sprin gyi char mngon par bab bo// lha rdzas las 'das pa'i rol mo dkrol ba'i sprin dang / mas mam 'a ju ma can las su tshums las
70a6(phal chen): hI ma so/ rdzas las las pa'i zhig bye 'i nyon gyi rnam pa da ung pa'i sprin gyi char ngo sa po lta sbal sa pa da nid bye pa les son pa gsus pa'i rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// lha rdzas las 'das shing chos kyi dbyings
70a7(phal chen): su rgyas par khyab pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung gi dbyangs mngon par brjod pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// 'jig rten gyi khams yongs su dag pa rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par ba
70a8(phal chen): po// byang chub nye bar brtan pa'i rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab po// 'od zer snang ba'i rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin gyi char gyi mngon par bab po// shin tu bstan pa'i byin gyi brlabs
70b1(phal chen): kyi char rnam pa brjod du med pa'i sprin gyi char mngon par bab ste/ ji ltar 'jig rten gyi khams 'di'i gling bzhi par/ de bzhin gshegs pa byang chub kyi shing drung du de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i snying po
70b2(phal chen): byang chub la byang chub sems dpa'i pho brang na bzhugs par snang ba de bzhin du/ phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa rgyas par gang bar bzhugs ste/ chos bstan pa 'di'ang thams cad du byung ngo // sangs
70b3(phal chen): rgyas kyi mthu dang / phyogs bcur de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par sangs rgyas pa'i chos nyid rab tu thob pas/ sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod du med pa phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyad kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'das pa'i
70b4(phal chen): pha rol nas/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyang 'ongs par gyur te/ phyogs bcu bkang nas de dag 'di skad zer ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras de ltar de bzhin gshe
70b5(phal chen): pa'i smon lam lung bstan pa'i chos nyid brjod pa legaso lag so// kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kyang thams cad kun tu bzang po zhes bya bar ming 'thun pa sha stag ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams
70b6(phal chen): kun tu dpal zhes bya ba dag nas de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan kun tu dpal gyi dbang phyug ces bya ba sha stag gi drung nas 'dir phyin te/ thams cad na yang chos bstan pa 'di nyid sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis 'khor
70b7(phal chen): gyi rnam pa 'di lta bu dag tu tshig 'di dag dang / yi ge 'di dag dang / go bar bya ba 'di dag dang / brjod pa 'di dag gis lhag chad med par byung bar gyur te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bdag cag kyang dbang du gyur pa sha stag
70b8(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi byin gyi brlabs kyis 'khor 'dir phyin to// ji ltar bdag cag 'khor 'dir phyin pa de bzhin du 'jig rten gyi khams ma lus pa thams cad kyi gling bzhi pa kun gyi de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par 'tshang
71a1(phal chen): rgya ba'i bzhir/ byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi zhing bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed kyis phyogs bcu bkang ste phyin par gyur to// de nas byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang pos
71a2(phal chen): phyogs bcur blta ste/ chos kyi dbyings la rnam par bltas nas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rab tu brjod pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i dbyings yongs su brjod pa dang / smon lam chen po
71a3(phal chen): dbyings kun tu grags par bya ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams dang / bskal pa thams cad kyi grangs yongs su brjod pa dang / dus ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas 'byung ba bstan pa dang / sems can gyi khams dbang po ji ltar
71a4(phal chen): yongasu smin pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas byung ba mnyes par bya/ ba brjod pa dang / byin gyis brlabs pa'i tshul bzhin du sangs rgyas 'byung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa don yod pa yongasu
71a5(phal chen): brjod pa dang / dge ba'i rtsa ba ji ltar bskyed pa bzhin du gsal/ bar bya ba yang dag par bstan pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' mang po'i mthu chen po bstan pa dang / sems can thams cad la
71a6(phal chen): rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi sgras bskul bar byed cing / dge ba'i rtsa ba'i stobs dang shugs dang / sangs rgyas kyi byin gyis brlabs kyis de'i tshe tshigs su bcad pa 'di dag smras so// thams cad shin tu dang sems kyi/ 
71a7(phal chen): sgrib pa ma lus thams cad rnam par bsal gyis la// yon tan 'byung gnas 'jig rten gtso bo yi// smon lam dam pa bshad kyis mnyan par gyis// mkhas mchog skyes bu seng ge dag/ spyad pa ci 'dra sngon spyad spyod par
71a8(phal chen): 'gyur ba'i rnams// byang chub sems dpa' gtso rnams kyi// spyod pa thams cad rim gyis brjod par bya// 'di la dpe med mchog rnams kyi// bskal pa'i grangs dang 'jig rten grangs dang chos bstan dang // rgyal ba rnams kyi
71b1(phal chen): 'byung ba dag yongasu brjod kyis dang pa'i yid kyis nyon// de dag sngan chad smon lam gyis// sems can ji ltar sdug bsngal rnams las dgrol bya zhes// sems can rnams la phan pa'i phyir// 'jig rten sgron ma skye ba
71b2(phal chen): rnams kyang mthong // spyod pa ji ltar shes gyur te// gsung gi mchog rnams kun la mchod pa byas pas// sangs rgyas mnyam pa nyid rnyed de// thams cad mkhyen nyid rab la mngon sangs rgyas// sngon gyi mi yi seng ge rnams// 
71b3(phal chen): sangs rgyas phyogs bcur 'od snang rab tu 'bar mdzad cing // 'od zer dra ba rab 'gyed pas// phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten snang mdzad mthong gyur nas// bdag cag rgyal ba'i yon tan gyis// brgyan pa'i 'jig rten sgron ma'i
71b4(phal chen): dam par 'gyur bya ste// stobs bcu mnga' ba kun mkhyen par/ mi'i sang ger bya zhes smon lam 'dabs// nged kyis sems can thams cad kyi/ 'dod chags zhe sdang gti mug rab tu 'bar gyur pa'i// sdug
71b5(phal chen): bsngal rnams las rab dkrol te// ngan song thams cad yongs su bcang bya zhes// 'di 'dra'i smon lam rdzogs byas te// de nas dpa' ba chen po spyod pa rab la spyod// blo brtan phyir ldog ma 'gyur ba/ rdos
71b6(phal chen): bcu rnams kyi chags med rab tu 'thob// skyes bu seng ga gang rnams kyis// 'di 'dra'i smon lam sngar btab phyir ldog mi 'gyur bar// 'jig rten rnams na spyod mdzad pa// de dag don yod spyod pa brjod pa bya// bskal pa bza
71b7(phal chen): po gcig la yang // sangs rgyas stong 'grangs tshang bar kun kyang 'byung 'gyur// kun tu gzigs pa gang brjod pa// de dag rim gyis bshad pa 'di 'dra'o// bskal pa bzang po gcig bzhin du// brjod du med pa'i bskal
71b8(phal chen): pa khrag khrig de bzhin te/ sangs rgyas ma byon de dag gi/ bzang po'i spyod pa bdag gis bstan par bya// zhing rgyung gcig po ji bzhin du// brjod med pa'i zhing rnams thams cad kun bzang ste// ma byon stobs bcu'i
72a1(phal chen): skyon med pa'i// spyod pa thams cad de bzhin bshad par bya// rgyal ba gang 'og gang 'byung dang // ci mtshan de'i smon lam rnam pa ci 'dra dang / rgyal ba gang gis gang gi lung / bstan
72a2(phal chen): mdzad mkhas pa'i sku tshe ji tsam dang // chos kyi rnam pa dge ba ni// gang gis bsgrubs te dam pa brnyes par gyur pa dang // 'jig rten ji ltar btul ba dang // rgyal ba rnams kyi dam chos cir gnas dang // rnam dag zhing
72a3(phal chen): yang ci 'dra dang // sems can rnam par dag dang chos kyi 'khor lo dang // bstan pa'i dus dang dus min dang // de las gang zag rnam par dag 'gyur dang // sems can rnams kyi las gang dang // spyod pa gang dang rnam grol
72a4(phal chen): tshe'adrar 'gyur ba dang // dbang po rno rtul bar ma dang // spyod ma chog sems can 'dul ba'ang bstan par bya// 'di 'dra'i shes dpar 'jug pa la// spyod pa'i dam pa rnams kyis rab tu zhugs gyur cing // 
72a5(phal chen): bzang po'i 'byung gnas spyod pa dang // 'gro kun ye shes 'khor lo spyod zhugs pa/ lus kyi las la chags med cing // ngag la chags mang sgra dbyangs thams cad rnam dag la// sems spyod chag pa med pa/ 
72a6(phal chen): yis// dus gsum ma lus rgyas par khyab par byed// 'di 'dra kun tu bzang po yi// spyod pa'i mchog la pha rol phyin pa thob gyur pa// brjod du med pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams// chos dbyings kun tu rab tu brjod pa byed// ma
72a7(phal chen): 'ongs dus kyi bskal pa dang // 'byam klas zhing rnams brjod du med pa thams cad kyang // skad cig sems kyis rab tu shes// chos nyid de la rnam par rtog pa med// gang rnams spyod pa'i sa 'di la// spyod pa'i dam pas
72a8(phal chen): rjes su zhugs par gyur pa'i rnams// byang chub sems dpa' mchog rnams kyi// yon tan spyod pa phyogs tsam bshad par bya// mtha' dang dbus med ye shes can// stobs bcu rnams kyi spyod yul mchog la zhugs
72b1(phal chen): gyur pa// thams cad shes byed mkhas pa'i rnams// mi ldog spyod pas rab tu zhugs gyur cing // 'od byed blo gros dam pa dang // kun tu bzang po'i smon lam mchog la zhugs gyur pa// dpe zla med pa de dag gi
72b2(phal chen): ye shes tshul dang spyod pa brjod par bya// rdul phran gcig go cha shas la// 'jig rten khams rnams ji snyed de dag shes pa dang // spyod pa rgya che thos gyur na// 'jig rten de dag thams cad mos par 'gyur/ wa
72b3(phal chen): ni ba ji lta ba// de bzhin rdul phran thams cad ma lus gzung bya ste/ ye shes bzang po de dag ni// 'jig rten khams la 'jug pa bsam mi khyag de dag dus kyi rnam pa la'ang // rdul phran gcig gi khyon gyi cha la yang dag
72b4(phal chen): 'jug/ rdul phran gcig la de bzhin du// zhing yangs rnam pa tha dad kun la 'jug/ rdul phran thams cad re re la// zhing rnams brjod du med pa mang po 'dzud pa byed/ rnam pa tha dad du ma dang // gcig
72b5(phal chen): dang tshad med de bzhin rab tu shes/ ji snyed ci yang ma lus pa 'i// chos dbyings gzung ba thams cad yang dag gzung byedacing // mtshan nyid tha dad sna tshogs te// sems can grangs kyi bskal pa
72b6(phal chen): rlung mi mnyam// 'jig rten phra bar 'jug pa la// phra la shin tu gzhol bas phra bar 'jug bya ste// brjod du med pa rab bstan pa'o// bskal pa thams cad ma lus mdzud pa byed// de dag ring dang thung ba dang // dus kyi skad cig
72b7(phal chen): sems can skal ba mi mthun shes// shes spyod mi mnyam ma yin pa'i// shes pas de dag thams cad khong du chud// yangs dang yangs min mkhas pas na// 'jig rten zab mo rnams la rab tu jug pa byed// lus la zhing rnams
72b8(phal chen): de shes te// zhing la'ang de bzhin gcig min lus mdzud do// phyogs rnams bcu po thams cad du// phyogs rnams kun la 'jug cing skad dus dang // 'jig rten khams rnams 'byam klas la// tshad med gzi brjid ldan
73a1(phal chen): pa rab tu 'jug/ gang yang zhing rnams mtha' yas shing // dbus med gzung ba byas shing dus kyi dbyings su 'dzud// zhing gi rgyud la mkhas pa'i rnams/ shes dang ldan pas ye shes rab tu 'byung / 
73a2(phal chen): bzang po'i yon tan ldan pa'i rnams// phyogs dang 'jig rten khams kyi rgyud du gyur pa dag / ji snyed yod pa der 'jug ste// brjod du med pa de dag rab tu shes// zhing dang zhing gis rnams kyi// brjod du med pa'i zhing rnams
73a3(phal chen): kun kyang rab tu 'thob// de dag tshul yang rab tu shes// las rnams gang gis sbyangs pa'ang khong du chud/ gang yang zhing rnams du ma dag/ las rnams khrag khrig kun gyis kun nas nyon mongs par// 'gro bas kun tu bsgrub
73a4(phal chen): byas pa// de dag thams cad rgyud kyang ci 'dra shes// brjod du med pa yangs pa'i rnams/ zhing gcig bstan pas de dag yongs su shes par gyur// de 'dra'i zhing la 'jug pa dang // gang la grangs med de dag sun ma
73a5(phal chen): 'jug/ 'jig rten khams ni gcig la yang // 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad yang dag 'dzud pa byed// 'jig rten gcig tu bsgongs mi 'gyur// 'jig rten khams rnams de bzhin
73a6(phal chen): 'dres mi 'gyur// spyi'u tshugs rnams dang gong ma'i rnams// blo dang 'og gis rnams yongs su gzung bya ste// 'gro ba'i rnam par ming thogs pa// 'jig rten kun la 'jug cing rab tu shes/ spel zhing rgyu ba'i rgyud rnams
73a7(phal chen): dang // zhing rnams mtha' yas mtha' dang dbus yod ma yin pa// sna tshogs yangs pa rab tu shes// rnam pa gcig shes rnam pa tha dad shes// zhing gi grangs rnams rab tu shes// ye shes chags med mtha' ldan kun gyi grang
73a8(phal chen): rnams kyang // bzang po'i theg pa spyod pa yis// rgyal sras kun tu bzang rnams rab tu shes// 'jig rten thams cad sprul pa dang // sems can rnams sprul dang de bzhin zhing sprul dang // chos rnams sprul pa'i tshul shes
73b1(phal chen): ba/ sangs rgyas sprul pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa'i rnams// 'jig rten phra zhing zab pa dang // yangs shing sna tshogs yangs pas cho mcho dgu'i rnams/ sna tshogs tha dad rnams bsags pa/ las kyi rnam smin gnas pa'i
73b2(phal chen): 'di rten rnams// rdzu 'phrul rnam par 'phrul pa yis// chos dbyings 'jug par bya la shin tu bslabs pa yi// rgyal sras mtha' dang dbus med pa// phyogs bcu thams cad ma lus 'gengs par byed// 'jig rten khams
73b3(phal chen): rnams de dag gi/ ming ni bskal pa sems can snyed kyi mthar thug cing // zad par brjod par mi nus ste// ming bshad gal te sangs rgyas gsung na gsung // 'jig rten mgon po rnams kyi yang // mtshan rnams mtshan nyid mi mthun
73b4(phal chen): rnam pa sna tshogs mtshan/ bskal pa brjod med zang byas kyang / mtshan rnams gcig nas gcig brgyud mthar thug med/ 'on kyang dma' ba'i sems med par/ mkhas pa rnams ni dus gsum bde gshegs
73b5(phal chen): sangs rgyas phyir/ chos kyi dbyings la byung ba ste// sangs rgyas ye shes sa la'ang rab tu zhugs// dran pas chags med dag pa ste// chags med yid dang ldan zhing blo gros mtha' yas pas/ 
73b6(phal chen): ye shes blo gros mchog ldan pa// chos dbyings bshad la pha rol phyin pa thob// gang gis 'jig rten khams kyi rnams// yangs dang phra ba sna tshogs shes gyur cing // der ni 'das pa'i dus rnams la// sems gcig
73b7(phal chen): bskyed pas rab tu 'jug pa byed// mi yi seng ge de dag tu/ sangs rgyas spyod pa sna tshogs rnam pas chags med par// byang chub mchog tu sangs shing // rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad ston pa mdzad// de bzhin ma 'ongs dus
73b8(phal chen): rnams kyi// rje su gang byon de'i bskal pa ci 'dra dang // de la mi yi seng gi gang // skye bar 'gyur ba de dag kun kyang shes// smon lam spyod pa ci 'dra dang // spyod yul gang rnams bsgom pa gang gis grub gyur cing // bsgrub pa
74a1(phal chen): rnam pa ci 'dra bas// bskal pa gang la byang chub 'tshang rgya dang // de dag 'khor kyang khong du chud// sku tshe'i tshad dang sems can 'dul ba ci 'dra dang // chos kyi sgo mo gang zhig gis/ 'gro bar chos
74a2(phal chen): kyi 'khor lo bskor ba shes// de ltar kun tu bzang po yi// ye shes mchog gis bsgrubs pa'i spyod pa'i sa gnas shing // de dag thams cad rab tu shes// de ni 'gro gtso kun gyi 'byung gnas yin// de ltar byung ba gzung
74a3(phal chen): byas shing // 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad 'dab chags ma lus par// 'jig rten khams la rab tu 'jug/ de bzhin chos kyis dbyings rnams rab tu shes// des ni mi yi gtso bo rnams// dgra las rgyal zhing
74a4(phal chen): thams cad gzigs pa ji snyed pa// mi thub rgol ba dpa' bo'i rnam sa// chos kyi mnga' la pha rol phyin brnyes pa// de dag 'khor kyang rab tu shes// sems can 'dul dang zhing rnams rnam par dag pa dang // 
74a5(phal chen): rgyal ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i rnams// sems pas bskal pa yangs pa zad par byed// skyes bu'i mchog rnams 'dul mdzad /  // 'jig rten mchog tu phyin pa'i byin rlabs dam pa la// mi zad
74a6(phal chen): mdzod kyi shes yangs pas// ye shes tshul la mkhas pa rab tu 'jug/ chags med mig gis blta ba dang // chags med rna ba mngon par bsgrub pa sgrub byed cing // chags pa med pa'i lus yangs dang // yangs pa'i lhas kyang
74a7(phal chen): 'jig rten tshim par byed// dam pa'i sems la chags med de// bsam pa kun tu rnam yangs rnam par ngag dang ldan// ye shes 'byung gnas bdag nyid cha// dus gsum sems rnams ma lus des khyab po// sprul pa'i pha rol
74a8(phal chen): phyin thob cing // zhing rnams sprul pa'i bslab par bya ba bslab pa'i rnams// sems can sprul la mkhas pa dag/ sprul pa sprul pas 'jig rten 'dul ba byed// 'du shes rnam pa du ma ste// des ni 'jig rten sna tshogs ma lus
74b1(phal chen): rnam par bris// de dag thams cad rab tu shes// sangs rgyas ye shes tshul la rab tu 'jug/ 'khor rnams brjod du med pa dag/ sangs rgyas sku rnams re re dag la yod pa'i rnams// kun la 'jug cing mthong bar byed/ sem
74b2(phal chen): can rnam par 'dul ba'i mtha' yang med// ye shes zab mo mthong bas na// ye shes nyi ma shin tu gsal ba shar gyur pa'i// phyir mi ldog pa'i spyod pa la// 'jig rten 'byam klas kun tu 'jug par byed// ji lta'i tshul du zhugs
74b3(phal chen): gyur cing // 'jig rten 'di dag thams cad rnam par bkod 'dra bar// sems can tshul bzhin rab tu 'phags// khams gsum thams cad mig yor tshul 'drar shes// 'on kyang rtog dang rnam rtog med// 'jig rten
74b4(phal chen): mtha' dang dbung med kun la rtog mi byed// rtog dang rtog med mkhas ba ste// rtog pa'i shes pas rnam par rtog pa med// bskal pa brjod du med pa'i rnams// sems bskyed gcig la yang dag 'du bar
74b5(phal chen): mdzud byed cing // 'jig rten mi khom 'di mthong nas// skad cig sems kyis thams cad shes par byed// brjod du med pa'i zhing rnams kyang // sems bskyed gcig gis thams cad yongasu 'da'
74b6(phal chen): bar bya cha bskal pa brjod med zad byed kyang // sgra'i rtsa'i cha shas gcig las g.yo ba med// bsgral pa brjod du med pa dag/ nyi ma gcig dang yud tsam gcig tu 'dzud byed kyang // ring dang thung la gzhol ba med// 
74b7(phal chen): skad cig gcig la 'jug pa'i pha rol phyin// sems kyi rnam pa 'jig rten kun// 'jig rten rnam pa sems kun gyi sems yin te// rnam pa gnyis kyi grangs su zhugs// 'on kyang de dag mi gnyis rtog pa med// sgyu ma'i
74b8(phal chen): rnam pa 'jig rten te// sems can zhing dang sangs rgyas chos kyang de bzhin no// 'on kyang 'jig rten mgon po'i rnams// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun la gcig tu snyoms// lus rnams brjod du med pa yis// phyogs
75a1(phal chen): bcu thams cad rgyas par bkang zhing yongs su ston// 'on kyang lus la gzhol ba med/ chos nyid rten pa gnas med rab tu shes/ 'on kyang mi yi seng ge rnams/ gnyis la gnas pa'i shes
75a2(phal chen): pas byung ba ma yin te// mi gnyis pa la'ang gnas pa med// gnyis dang gnyis med chos rnams rab tu shes// ji ltar smig rgyu rab rib dang // mig yor sgra brnyan de bzhin rmi lam 'dra ba dang // rmi lam rnam pa sprul pa ltar
75a3(phal chen): 'gro ba thams cad ma lus rab tu shes// de ltar spyod yul nyams med pas// sangs rgyas kun gyi rigs kyi rje su 'byung ba yin// kun tu bzang po'i ye shes dang // chos kyi dbyings la shin tu bdal ba yin// snying rje chen po/ 
75a4(phal chen): mtha' yas kyang // sems can med dang mnyam par zhing rnams thams cad sgom// sngon nas nyon mongs nyams med pa'i// bas ma pa dag pas 'jig rten kun tu 'gro// mi zad mkha'i ltar rnam dag
75a5(phal chen): pa'i// rgya chen shin tu yangs pa'i sa la rab tu zhugs// gsu/ nga ba'i seng ge thams cad kyi// tshul gyi dkyil 'khor thams ca/ da rjes su dran// 'jig rten rab tu spros pa la// smon lam tshad med yongs
75a6(phal chen): su gdab pa byas pas na// de dag spyod pa yongs su dag/ 'jig rten khams rnams thams cad rgyas par khyab// sangs rgyas rnams dang rgyas sras dang // de bzhin sangs rgyas rnams kyi chos rnams thams cad dang // 'jig
75a7(phal chen): rten rnams dang 'jig rten chos// chags med tha dad med pa'i tshul du shes// chos kyi sku'i snying po can// de'i lus la 'jig rten thams cad gzung byas shing // 'jig rten de yi lus yin yang // 'jig rten kun gyis de la
75a8(phal chen): gos pa med// ji ltar dang pa'i chu gsal la// gzugs brnyan yongs su snang yang der song 'phos pa med// de bzhin 'jig rten thams cad kyi// rjes su lus 'gro der song 'phos pa med// de ltar 'jig rten thams cad kyis/ 
75b1(phal chen): gos pa med cing 'jig rten yongasu dag pas na// lus ni mkha' dang 'dra ba ste/ de'i las rnams gang yang skyes pa med// mi zad pa yi lus shes pas// de ni nam yang skyes shing 'gags pa med pa ste// rtag dang mi rtag ma yin
75b2(phal chen): par// 'jig rten kun la'ang rnam par dmigs pa byed// lta ba'i rnam pa rab tu 'gags// brtan pa de dag yang dag lta ba ston pa byed// bdag gi med cing gnas pa med// len pa med cing chos kyi dbyings dang mnyam// ji ltar
75b3(phal chen): sgyu mkhan mkhas pa zhig/ sna tshogs mtshan nyid rnam pa tha dad gzugs 'phrul byed// 'on kyang de la 'gro ba med// gang du 'gro ba de bzhin mi dmigs so// sgyu ma tshad med ma yin te// sgyu ma tshad kyis dmigs par bya ba'ang
75b4(phal chen): ma yin no// tshad de tsha dang ldan pa yang // tshogs kyi dbus su sto na pa rab tu byed// de bzhin rtogs pa'i blo ldan pa// sangs rgyas kun gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba rnams lnga byung // sems ni tshad yod ma yin te// 
75b5(phal chen): tshad med pa la gnas pa'ang de dag min// 'du shes rnam pa ga cig min te// de dag tshad med pa dang tshad dang ldan pa ston// lam gyi rgyud dang 'brel ba med// tshad med rnams gnas pa'ang de bzhin med// 
75b6(phal chen): sangs rgyas chos rnams zab pa ste// shin tu langs pas zab cing zhi bas de bzhin zab/ zab mo sna tshogs rgyud rnams dang // mtha' yas zab pa rnams kyang rab tu shes// ye shes bzang po rmongs pa med// rgyud la dri ma med
75b7(phal chen): pas bsam pa rnam par dag/ byin gyis rlob la mkhas pas na// srog chags bye ba shin tu dag par byed// dge bar byed pa'i dkyil 'khor rnams// rab tu brjod cing dag dang mi dag rnam par ston// gnas la mngon par
75b8(phal chen): ma chags pas// chos kyi dbyings rnams kun tu rab tu rgyu// sems can med mthar phyin gyur kyang // 'jig rten thams cad ma lus de dag khong du chud// 'jig rten thams cad ma lus par// rnam par sangs rgyas mya ngan gar
76a1(phal chen): mi 'dar// chos rnams bgrang ba'i tshul la mkhas// sems can bgrang tshul shes kyang grangs la skyes pa med// chos kyi sprin chen char 'bebs shing // 'jig rten khams rnam
76a2(phal chen): thams cad snang bar byed// sangs rgyas byang chub ma lus la// sems bskyed gcig gis de dag rab tu 'jug/ de dag phyir ldog med pa ste// sems can kun gyi khams las phyir mi ldog/ sangs rgyas sku ni thob
76a3(phal chen): gyur kyang // chos rnams 'di dag lus yod ma yin rab tu shes// lus rnams kun gyi tshul la mkhas// lus kyis rnam phye 'jig rten rab tu shes// sems can kun tu rgyu ba dang // bskal pa rnams dang zhing la pha rol
76a4(phal chen): phyin pa thob// phyogs rnams rgya mtsho gangs chen mtshor// ye shes rgya mtsho'i tshul la mkhas pas zhugs// lus rnams thams cad re/ re las// sems can kun gyi lus rnams sna tshogs ji snyed
76a5(phal chen): dang / sangs rgyas sku ni mtha' yas pa// ye shes shin tu yangs pa de/ ston to// skad gcig gcig gi dus tshul la/ mi'i gtso bomang po 'byung ba rab tu shes// bskal pa mang po brjod med
76a6(phal chen): du/ mi yi seng ge bgrang bas zad mi 'gyur// de dag mya ngan 'da' ba yang // skad cig gcig la tshad med shin tu yangs pa 'byung // ring bsrel rnam dbye mang po yang // ye shes dri med phra bas ston pa byed// de bzhin
76a7(phal chen): ma 'ongs dus kyi yang // mi'i sang gi mtha' yas smon lam 'debs pa'i rnams// byang chub dri med sems bskyed pa// ye shes yangs shing shin tu phra bas shes// bzang po spyod la gnas bcas shing // de bzhin
76a8(phal chen): dus gsum gshegs pa'i sems can gtso bo rnams// ji snyed skyes par gyur pa dag/ de dag thams cad ma lus rab tu shes// de ltar rab tu shes pas na// mtha' dang dpung med spyod pa'i sa dang de bzhin du// 
76b1(phal chen): ye shes 'byung gnas blo gros la// ye shes 'khor lo'i spyod pas phyir mi ldog/ ye shes phra mo rab yangs pa// stobs bcu rnams kyi spyod yul mchog la dang gzhugs// bzang po rtogs pa'i blo can rnams// phyir
76b2(phal chen): mi ldog la 'jug pa brjod bya na// sangs rgyas rgyal ba thams cad kyi/ yang dag gzhol bar bya la de dag zhugs pas na// spyod las phyir ldog med pa ste// byang chub dam pa zhi bar 'tshang yang rgya// de 'dra'i sems
76b3(phal chen): rgyud gcig la yang // mtha' dang dpung med sems rnams yang dag 'dzud pa byed// shin tu yangs pa'i tshad med las// 'du shes de dang de la yang dag bsgrubs// nyon mongs med dang nyon mongs dang // slob dang mi
76b4(phal chen): slob sems kyang de bzhin rab tu shes// sems rgyud de dag re re la ya nga // sems rnams brjod du med pa mngon 'tshang rgya// gcig dang gnyis su shes pa med// de dag yongs su 'dres par
76b5(phal chen): 'gyur ba'ang med pa ste// so so'i 'du shes rnam pa la// sems can de/ ngag skyes par gyur pa yin// 'di na 'dug par mthong gyur tu // sems can brjod med gzhan dang gzhan sems ldan
76b6(phal chen): pa'i rnams// gzhan gyi zhing phyin 'du shes kyang // 'jig rten sna tshogs rnams la rab tu skye// 'di 'dra'i tshul la 'jug pa la// spyod pa'i mchog gis rjes su zhugs par gyur pa'i rnams// kun tu bzang po'i
76b7(phal chen): mang thob ste// 'jig rten mgon po kun gyi rjes su skyes// sems can bye ba la la ni// ngan song 'grangs pa'i ming thogs mtho ris 'du shes 'gyur// la la mtho ris sa rnams kyi// rnam pa kun la ngan song
76b8(phal chen): 'du shes 'gyur// 'jig rten mi mtshungs skal la ltos// rnam pa tha dad las kyi sa las rab tu skyes// 'du shes rnam pa mtha' yas ste// gcig min yangs la 'jig rten rab tu 'jug/ 'jig rten
77a1(phal chen): rten khams rnams thams cad kyi// 'du shes dra ba skal pa mi mnyam rab tu shes// mig 'phrul sgyu ma'i tshul gyis na// skad cig gcig gis sems kyis rab tu gzhol/ 
77a2(phal chen): de bzhin dbang po rnams la ste// mig gi skye mched rna ba sna'i skye mched dang // lce dang lus dang yid la yang // 'jig rten rnam pa tha dad 'du shes 'jug/ mig rnams re re'i yul la yang // mtha' dang dpung med mig
77a3(phal chen): rnams rab tu 'dzud pa byed// rnam pa tha dad du ma ste// tshad med kun la'ang zhen par 'gyur ba med// 'on kyang phan tshun gcig gis gcig bdo zhing gnod par 'gyur ba de dag kun na med// bdag bdag so so'i las kyi rnams// 
77a4(phal chen): ji ltar bsags pa'i tshul bzhin nyam su myong // bzang zhes bya ba de dag ku na/ tshad med stobs dang ye shes sa'i shes rab kyis// 'byam klas mig rnams thams cad la// rab tu zhugs pas shin tu rtogs pa yin/ 
77a5(phal chen): de bzhin 'jig rten thams cad kyang // thams cad ma lus rnam pa tham/ sa cad 'jig tshul du// thams cad shin tu shes gyur kyang / chen spyod pas mya ngan mi 'da'o// sangs rgyas shin tu bstan pa dang / 
77a6(phal chen): sems can bstan dang de bzhin zhing rnams bstan pa dang // dus rnams shin tu bstan pa dang / bstan pa sna tshogs rnam pa kun kyang shes// la la 'di la 'ongs gyur kyang // gzhan dang gzhan rnams ma 'ongs dus la gnas pa
77a7(phal chen): yin// 'on kyang ma 'ongs dus kyi rnams// la las da ltar byung bar rab tu shes// de 'dra'i tshul can gcig min pa'i// 'jig rten mtshan nyid tha dad thams cad rab tu shes// thams cad mkhyen pa nyid tshul gyis// sangs rgyas ye
77a8(phal chen): shes kun tu mtha' yang yas// / shin tu rgyas pa chen po'i mdo// sangs rgyas phal po che zhes bya ba las kun tu bzang po'i spyod pa bstan pa'i le'u ste bzhi bcu gnyis pa'o// 
77b1(phal chen): bam po bdun cu tham pa// bcom ldan 'das ye shes chen pos/ rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i thugs mnga' ba/ 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas thams cad dang / sku gcig pas mnyam pa nyid
77b2(phal chen): brnyes pa/ sang+yas thams cad kyi spyod pa mnyam pa nyid dang ldan pa chags pa med pa'i spyod yul mngon par mkhyen pa ye shes kyi rang bzhin chos kyi sku mnga' ba/ mtshan nyid yod nas med pa'i chos la rten pa chos kyi dbyings mi
77b3(phal chen): gnyis pa'i spyod yul gyis yang dag par spyod pa mtha' dang dpung med cing mtshungs pa'i mngon par 'tshang rgya ba brnyas pa/ rnam par thar pa bsgribs pa med pa'i spyod yul la shin tu dgyes pa/ chos kyi sku na mkha'i dbyings kyi
77b4(phal chen): kyi mthas klas pa mnga' ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i byin gyis brlab sa kyi pho brang khang pa brtsegs pa'i gzhal med khang de bzhin gshegs pa bzhugs pa/ chos kyi dbyings kyi snying po can 'ad kun
77b5(phal chen): nas 'byung ba/ rgyan chen po dang ldan pa 'od dang / zhing gsal ba rnam pa ra snang ba'i snying po can/ sangs rgyas skye ba chos kyi mtha' dang dbus med pa'i gnas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus las byung
77b6(phal chen): ba gzhi 'od zer gyis rnam par brgyan pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus rang bzhin du gnas pas/ rab tu bsgrubs pa'i chos chen po'i gzhir gyur pa/ chos kyi dbyings kun tu rgyas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'od
77b7(phal chen): dang ldan pa/ na mkha'i dbyings kyi mthas btugs pa/ ye shes kyi yul yang dag pa'i mtha' spyod yul chags pa med par rnam par gsal ba na/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po rin po che bzang po'i pad+mo chen
77b8(phal chen): po rang rang gi smon lam byung ba'i dbus kyi snying po la 'khod pa kun kyang tshe gcig gis thogs pa 'jig rten gyi khams gzhan dang gzhan nas phyin pa ye shes chen po rnam par phye ba'i spyod yul la gzhol ba/ chos
78a1(phal chen): kyi dbyings tha mi dad pa'i gzhi mnyam pa nyid la zhugs pa/ nam mkha' dbyings gzhi med cing mtha' dang dbus med pa la rnam par spyod pa/ chos thams cad 'byung ba med cing mngon par grub
78a2(phal chen): pa med pa mngon du byas pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus las ma g.yos su thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes rab tu thob pa 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad du kun gyis brjod pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes las
78a3(phal chen): mngon du byung ba sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon sum du gyur pa'i ye shes snab thob pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod yul rgyun ma chad pa ye shes kyi rang bzhin chos kyi lus gcig cing tha mi dad pas/ gzugs kyi
78a4(phal chen): lus mtha' yas pa'i sgo kun tu ston pa chos kyi dbyings mtha' dang dbus med pa la 'jug pa shin tu shes pa sems can gyi khams su rnam par spyad pa las phyir mi ldog pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos kyi
78a5(phal chen): dbyings dang yang dag pa'i mtha' mnyam pa nyid thob pas sprul pa mngon/ par sgrub pa de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par snang mdzad dang / sngon/ lhan cig tu skyes shing dge ba'i rtsa ba bsags pa sha stag 'di lta
78a6(phal chen): sde/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po dang / kun tu grags pa'i dbang phyug rgyal po dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal dang / rdo rje dpal gyi rgyal mtshal dang / rnam par grol ba
78a7(phal chen): bsgribs pa med pa'i zla ba dang / nyi ma'i 'od zer dri ma med pa'i snying po dang / mngon par shes pa chen pos rnam par 'phrul pa'i blo dang / 'od dri ma med pa'i dpal gyi gzi brjid 'od zer gyi rgyal po dang / blo gros rgya mtsho'i mchog
78a8(phal chen): 'dzin cing blo la rnam par rtse ba bsal bas mngon par shes pa'i dpal dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po// stobs bcu mi 'jigs pa'i seng ge'i nga ro chen pos rnam par rtse bas mngon par shes pa dang / 
78b1(phal chen): de dag la sogs pa/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po sangs rgyas kyi zhing bya ba khrag khrig brgya spong brjod du med pa phrag bcu'i rdul shin tu phra ba snyed dang thabs gcig tu bzhugs so// de nas de'i tshe bcom
78b2(phal chen): ldan 'das kyis dzod spu nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i 'od zer/ 'od zer gyi 'khor bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa mang po'i 'od zer dang ldan pa byung ste/ des 'jig rngan gyi khams 'byam
78b3(phal chen): klas pa thams cad ma lus par snang bar byas/ 'jig rngan g.yas phya yu lan bcur bskor te/ de bzhin gshegs pa rnam par 'phrul pa bstan nas/ byang chub sems dpa' bya ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po bskul ba
78b4(phal chen): byas te/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa thams cad rab tu bskyod nas/ ngan song gi rgyud thams cad kyi skye ba dang / shi 'pho rab tu zhi bar byas te/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ de
78b5(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas/ rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i gdan bstan par byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi 'a/ khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par bkod pa 'byam klas pa rab tu
78b6(phal chen): bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ na mkha'i mthas gtugs pa 'byam klas pa thams cad ma lus par rgyas par khyab par byas nas phyir 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa' 'khor
78b7(phal chen): gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la g.yas phyogs nas bskor nas/ de byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshes pa'i rig su byung ba'i dpal gyi spyi bor nub po// de nas byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor thams cad ngo mtshar
78b8(phal chen): cher 'dzin cing dga' ba thob par gyur te// 'od zer gyi dra ba snang ba 'di lta bu byung bas na/ chos chen po brjod par ni 'gyur du nges so snyam nas rtogs pa'i blo yang thob par gyur to// 'od zer de dag gis
79a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyi lus la phog par gyur ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po// de bzhin ga
79a2(phal chen): pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal pad+mo'i stan las langs te/ bla gos phrag pa gcig la gzar nas/ pad+mo'i snying po de la pus mo g.yas pa'i lha nga sa la btsugs nas/ bcom ldan 'das ga la ba der thal mo sbyar ba
79a3(phal chen): btud de/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'du shes dang ldan pa'i yid la byed pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa la tshig su bcad de gsol pa// rnam dag blo mnga' yon tan mkhyen pas 'phags pa// spyod yul chags pa med
79a4(phal chen): pa'i pha rol phyin brnyas/ dus gsum mnyam pa'i chos nyid mnyam pa ston pa// khyod la bdag ni sti stang rim gro bgyid do// mtshan nyid med pa'i spyod yul pha rol phyin brnyas// mtshan gyis shin tu brgyan
79a5(phal chen): pa'i sku yang ston mdzad// dri med 'od can 'od zer stong dang ldan 'gyed// bdud kyi sde rnams ma lus rab tu mjoms mdzad// phyogs bcu kun na gang rnams ji snyed mchis pa'i// zhing rnams thams cad
79a6(phal chen): ma lus rab tu bskyod kyang // thugs rje ldan pas su la'ang 'jigs par mi mdzad// khyod kyi rdzu 'phrul mthu ni de 'dra de tshul// nam mkha'i dbyings la mnyam pa nyid du rab zhugs// de bzhin chos dbyings mnyam pa nyid kyang brnyes gyur/ 
79a7(phal chen): sems can stong phrag bye ba grol bar mdzad cing // sems can kun gyi sdig chen rab tu zhi mdzad/ bskal pa snong du brtul zhugs dam po spyad de// byang chub mchog gi lam ni yang dag bsgrubs nas// chags pa med pa'i ye shes
79a8(phal chen): spyod yul 'di brnyas// sangs rgyas kun dang rang bzhin gcig tu rab gyur// rnam par 'dren pa khyod kyis 'di nas 'od bkye// 'jig rten thams cad ma lus kun bskyod nas// chu 'phrul mtha' yas yang dag bstan pa bgyi ste// 
79b1(phal chen): bdag gi lus 'dir de dag ma lus zhugs gyur// de la bdag gi blo gros 'di ltar skyes te// chos rje khyod la bdag gis zhu ba'i dus bab// shin tu nges pa'i chos la rab tu brlabs pa'i// byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyang
79b2(phal chen): 'dus par gyur snyam// tshogs 'di dag pa 'dus pas rnam par dag pa// 'jig rten slob dpon mgon pos rab tu bsngags pa// ye shes mtha' pas ldan pa yul la chags med// de 'dra'i mthu chen dpa' bo 'di dag 'dir
79b3(phal chen): phyin/ de don 'jig rten slob dpon drang srong chen po// ye shes stobs dang brtson 'grus mtha' yas byung gyur// byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag snang bar mdzad gsol// chos rab bdag gis gang zhus de yang bshad gsol
79b4(phal chen): drang srong chen po'i spyod yul 'di dag bstan cing // yang dag ma nor brjod par nus pa gang lags// skyes bu khyu mchog rnams kyi sras ni gang lags// 'jig rten mgon gyis gtso bo khyod kyis bshad gsol/ 
79b5(phal chen): tshigs su bcad pa de dag gsol ma thag tu// de'i tshe bcom ldan 'das kyi zhal gyi sgo nas// mi bsnyengs pa'i mthar phyin pa zhes bya ba'i 'od zer 'khor gyi 'od zer khrag khrig brgya stong grangs med pa
79b6(phal chen): dang ldan pa byung ste// des 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa// thams cad ma lus par snang bar byas nas// 'jig rten gsas phyogasu lan bcur bskor te// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa bstan nas// 
79b7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po bskul ba byas ste/ 'jig rten gyi khams 'byam klas pa/ thams cad rab tu bskyod nas/ ngan song gi rgyud thams cad kyi skye ba dang / shi 'pho ba rab tu zhi bar byas
79b8(phal chen): te/ bdud kyi khyim thams cad zil gyis mnan nas/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad mngon par 'tshang rgya bas/ rnam par sangs rgyas pa'i gdan bstan pa byas te/ sangs rgyas kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor rnam par
80a1(phal chen): bkod pa 'byam klas pa rab tu bstan nas/ 'jig rten gyi khams chos kyi dbyings kyis klas pa/ namakha'i mthas gtugs par 'byam klas pa/ thams cad ma lus par rgyas par khyab
80a2(phal chen): par byas nas phyir 'ongs te/ byang chub sems dpa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor thams cad la g.yas phyogs nas bskor nas/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i kha'i sgor nub bo// de bzhin gshegs pa'i
80a3(phal chen): 'od zer des byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la reg par gyur ma thag tu/ de nas de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri/ sngon ci 'dra/ 
80a4(phal chen): bde las byang chub sems dpa'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri/ brgya phrag stong gyur du bzang zhing khyad par du 'phags par 'dug ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i seng ge'i gdan ma gtogs par byang chub sems
80a5(phal chen): dpa' gzhan gyi lus kyi seng ge'i khri las/ byang chub sems dpa' kun tu bzang po'i lus kyi seng ge'i khri brgya phrag spong gyur du/ bzang zhing khyad par du 'phags par snang ngo // de nas byang
80a6(phal chen): chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin
80a7(phal chen): gshegs pa'i cho 'phrul chen po// 'jig rten thams cad kyis khong du chud par dka' ba/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams rab tu dga' bar 'gyur ba/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'di lta bu bstan na/ kye rgyal ba'i
80a8(phal chen): sras de gang gi sngon gyi mtshan mar 'gyur/ de skad ces smras pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang pos/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs
80b1(phal chen): su byung ba'i dpal la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal sras de ni bdag 'di snyam du sems te/ sngon gyi yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi cho 'phrul chen po 'di dra ba dag kyang mthong ste/ de bzhin gshegs pa
80b2(phal chen): rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs bstan par dgongs pa dang / cho 'phrul chen po'i rnam pa 'di lta bu dag ston pa mdzad do// de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa'
80b3(phal chen): chen po// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su byung ba'i dpal gyis/ de bzhin gshegs pa 'byung ba bstan pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs kyi ming thos par gyur ma thag tu de'i tshe sa chen po g.yos par gyur to// de nas byang chub
80b4(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su 'byung ba'i dpal gyis/ byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' tsha na po kun tu bzang po la 'di skad ces smras so// kye rgyal ba
80b5(phal chen): sras legs par spobs par mdzod cig/ ji ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen pos/ de bzhin gshegs pa dgra ba com pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye
80b6(phal chen): bar byung ba bstan pa khong du chud par bya/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'khor 'dus pa 'di ni shin tu dag pa ste/ byang chub sems dpa' bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong kun nas 'dus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di ni byang chub
80b7(phal chen): sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po// sngon spyad pa shin tu spad pa las kyi mtha' shin tu sbyangs pa/ dran pa dang / blo gros dang / rigs pas shin tu 'phags pa/ rgya chen po'i pha rol tu phyin pa mchog thob pa/ de bzhin
80b8(phal chen): bshegs pa thams cad kyi spyod yul dang / spyod pa dang / tshul la rab tu gnas pa/ sangs rgyas kyi rjes su song ba'i 'du shes yid la byed pa ma nyams pa/ snying rje chen pos 'gro ba thams cad la rnam par lta ba/ 
81a1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i mngon par shes pa chen pos/ rnam par rol pa'i spyod yul can/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin rang gis rgyud du len pa/ sangs rgyas thams chosadapal gyi byin
81a2(phal chen): gyis brlabs pa ste/ de dag la sogs pa yon tan dang / legs pa tshad meng pa mang po dang ldan pa sha stag 'ongs shing 'dus pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras khyod kyang sangs rgyas bye ba khrag khrig brgya stong mang po bsnyen bkur ba/ 
81a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi spyod pa'i mchog tu phyin pa ting nge 'dzin dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i sgo thams cad kyi rnam par rol par mngon par mkhas pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsang ba'i gnas
81a4(phal chen): su chud pa/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la the tshom yongasu chad pa// de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis byin tu brlabs pa// sems can thams cad kyi dbang po la mkhas pa dang ldan pa/ sems
81a5(phal chen): can thams cad kyi mos pa dang rnam par grol ba'i lam yang dag par ston pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi rigs dang rgyud yang dag par 'byung ba'i ye shes dang ldan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi
81a6(phal chen): chos thams cad bstan pa la pha rol tu phyin pa'i mchog thob pa de dag la sogs pa yon tan mang po tshad med pa'i khyad par gyi mthar thug pa yin gyis/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang
81a7(phal chen): dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi skye ba 'byung ba bstan pa dang / sku yang dag par bstan pa dang / dbyangs rab tu brjod pa dang / thugs kyi mthu dang / yul gyi gnas dang / spyod yul bstan pa dang / mngon par
81a8(phal chen): byang chub pa'i gnas dang / chos kyi 'khor lo bskor bar mngon par bsgrubs pa dang / yongs su mya ngan las 'das pa chen po bstan pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa rnams mthong zhing thos pa dang / de bzhin gshegs
81b1(phal chen): pa dang 'grogs pas dge ba'i rtsa ba 'byung ba bstan pa la legs par spobs pa mdzod cig/ de nas byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po// de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigasu byung ba'i dpal gyis
81b2(phal chen): don 'di nyid yang bzlas te brjod pa'i phyir/ de'i tshe byang chub sems dpa' sems dpa' chen po kun tu bzang po la tshigs su bcad de smras pa/ chags med blo glos shin tu rnam par sangs rgyas blo ldan// ye shes mtha'
81b3(phal chen): yas yul la mnyam pa nyid gyur// rgyal ba'i spyod yul tshad med legs par yang dag shod cig/ de thos sangs rgyas sras rnams thams cad rab tu dga' 'gyur// rgyal ba mchog rnams 'byung ba ji ltar byang chub sems
81b4(phal chen): dpas// khong du chud bya ji ltar de dag yang dag balnga bya// de bzhin gshegs thugs ci 'drar sku dang dbyangs kyang ci 'dra// skyes bu khyu mchog rnams kyi yul dang spyod yul ci 'dra// de bzhin gshegs pa
81b5(phal chen): byang chub ji ltar rnam par 'tshang rgya// chos kyi 'khor lo dam pa rgyal ba ji ltar bskor mdzad// bde gshegs mya ngan 'das pa'i yang dag nyid kyang gsung ste// sangs rgyas sras po mtha' yas 'di dag
81b6(phal chen): dga' bar mdzod cig/ gang gis bde gshegs chos rgyal chen po mthong bar gyur cing // gang rnams 'grogs shing dge ba yang dag skyed par byed pa// de dag bsod nams 'phel ba'ang ma nor brjod par mdzod cig/ bde
81b7(phal chen): gshegs mthong na cir 'gyur de dang 'grogs na ci 'gyur// bde gshegs mya ngan 'das dang 'on tam bzhugs kyang rung ste// de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan rnams gang gis thos par gyur cing // yon tan 'byung gnas
81b8(phal chen): rnams la gang rnams dang pa skyed pa// de dag don kyang cir 'gyur 'khor 'dir bstan par mdzod cig/ byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad thal mo sbyar cing // bde bar gshegs dang khyod dang bdag la kun kyang
82a1(phal chen): lnga sdong// dris pa 'di dag sems can dag pa khyod kyis lung ston// yon tan rgya mtsho che mnga' rnams kyi spyod yul bstan mdzod// de dag don du chos rab ldan pa'i gsung mchog brjod cing // mang
82a2(phal chen): 'dra khyod kyi skye bo rnams kyi the tsom gcad mdzod// dpe dang rgyur ldan tshig gis de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs sngon// thos nas sems can khrag khrig byang chub mchog tu sems skyed// ji ltar zhing rnams thams cad ma
82a3(phal chen): lus rgyas par bkang zhing // rgyal ba sku'i yan lag sna tshogs yang dag ston mdzod// ji ltar khrag khrig chos dang ldan pa'i gsung rab brjod pa// sangs rgyas byang chub dpe dang rgyu yis bstan par mdzod cig/ gang zhig
82a4(phal chen): phyogs bcu'i zhing rnams khrag khrig thams cad kun tu// bskal pa mang po bye ba mtha' yas 'grangs par song yang // de rang rgyal sras 'dir tshogs 'di 'dra'i 'khor dang 'dra ba// byang chub sems
82a5(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi shin tu dka'o// de bas rgyal sras rang bzhin dag/ pa khyod kyi bshad mdzod// de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi rigs yangs yongs su ston cig/ byang chub sems dpa' 'di dag thams cad
