170b6(phal chen): 'jug pa thams cad gzung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas rnams skye ba nas bzung ste/ yongasu mya ngan las 'da' ba chen po'i bar du gzung ba rgyun 'chad pa med pa/ 
170b7(phal chen): chos kyi dbyings thams cad sangs rgyas kyi yongasu gang bar 'jug cing sangs rgyas skye ba thams cad kyang shin tu rnam par bye bar mthong ba 'di ni dgongs te bshad pa la mkhas pa brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
170b8(phal chen): gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba thams cad mi 'gyur ba'i tshul gyis mya ngan las 'das par shes kyang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i smon lam yongasu rdzogs par bya ba yongasu ma rdzogs kyi bar du smon/ 
171a1(phal chen): lam byir zlog par mi byed pa 'di ni dgongs te bshad pa la mkhas pa dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad gzhan gyi dring mi 'jogs

176b5(phal chen): pa yongasu zad par mi 'gyur bas rtogs pa'i dga' ba dang / phyog/ sa bcu tshad med par khyab pas/ blo'i dga' ba dang / sems can gyi lus sgo mtha' yas pa yongasu ston pas/ byang chub sems
176b6(phal chen): dpa'i rnam par 'phrul pa'i dga' ba dang / ting 'dzin gyi sgo gcig gis/ ting 'dzin gyi sgo thams cad la 'jug pas/ ting nge 'dzin gyi dga' ba dang / thos pa thams cad 'dzin pa nyams pa med par kun tu/ 
176b7(phal chen): 'dzin cing / sems can gzhan gyi rgyud kyis 'thob par byed pas/ gzungs kyi dga' ba dang / tshig gcig dang / yi ge gcig gis bskal pa brjod med par gzhan dang gzhan du smra zhing / nges pa'i tshig
176b8(phal chen): rgyun mi 'chad par rab tu ston pas spobs pa'i dga' ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus mtha' yas pa'i sgo'i rgyud du// mngon par byang chub pa ston pas/ mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i dga'
177a1(phal chen): dang / bdud dang phyir rgol ba thams cad chos dang / 'thun par tshar gcod pas chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i dga' ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems/ 
177a2(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi dga' ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi dgyes pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ 
177a3(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar thub pa med pas/ stobs kyi rgyan dang / zil gyis mi non pas/ mi 'jigs pa'i rgyun dang / don brjod myed cing yangs pa brjod pa'i sgo rgyun mi 'cha
177a4(phal chen): pas/ don gyi brgyan dang / chos kyi phung po stong phrag brgyad bcu rtsab zhi shin tu brtags pa'i chos rab tu ston pa mgo rmongs pa med pas/ chos kyi rgyan dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis bya ba'i smon/ 
177a5(phal chen): lam las phyir mi ldog pas/ smon lam gyi rgyan dang / kun tu bzla/ ngo bo'i theg pas 'byung bas spyod pa'i rgyan dang / zhing thams cang zhing gcig tu byin gyis rlobs pas/ zhing gi rgyan dang / 
177a6(phal chen): shing thams cad chos kyi sprin chen po'i char rgyas pa rab tu 'bebs pas/ dbyangs kyi dkyil 'khor gyi rgyan dang / bskal pa grangs med pa thams cadadu spyod pa'i rgyun mi gcod pas byin gyi brlabs kyi rgyan dang / 
177a7(phal chen): sems can gcig gi lus sems can snyed kyi lus su ston cing / sems can gyis khong du chud par byed pa'i thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi 'jigs pa'i mthu los phyir mi ldog pas/ 'phrul/ 
177a8(phal chen): ba'i rgyan to// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rgyan te/ de dag lo gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thams kyi rgyan bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur
177b1(phal chen): ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa mi sgul ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar btang ba thams cad yongasu gtong zhing / sbyin pa thams cad sbyin par
177b2(phal chen): byed pas/ sems bskyed pa mi sgul ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad nges par rtogs par gzhog pa la sems bskyed pa mi skul ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la mchod cing rim gro bya ba'i yid la bya
177b3(phal chen): ba mang bas sems bskyed pa mi sgul ba dang / sems can thams cad kyis mi 'khrugs pas/ sems bskyed pa mi skul ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu mi gtong bas sems bskyed pa mi sgul ba dang / 
177b4(phal chen): sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yong su btsal ba rgyun mi gcod byas pa/ sems bskyed pa mi sgul pa dang / bskal pa 'gro ba thams cad mnyam pa brjod meng ba'i yang brjod med por byang chub sems dang/ 
177b5(phal chen): spyad pa spyod pas/ zhum par mi 'gyur/ sgyid lug par mi 'gyurazhing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa las phyir mi ldog pas sems bskyed pa mi sprul pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang
177b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' dad pa ting tshugs pa dang / rnyog pa med cing dag pa dang / rnam par dag pa dri ma med pa dang / 'od dang ba/ sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkur ba la brtson pa phyir mi ldog pa mi zad pa/ 
177b7(phal chen): 'phrogs pa dga' ba dang / spro ba dang / mos pa chen pos byung ba dang ldan pas sems bskyed pa mi sgul ba dang / thams cad mkhyen par sbyor zhing 'byung ba'i lam la shin tu grub pas/ sems bskyed pa mi
177b8(phal chen): skul ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / gdams ngag dang / man ngag dang / bslab pa thams cad gzung zhing mnyan par yongasu mi spong zhing mos par bya ba la sems bskyed pa mi sgul po'o// 
178a1(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa mi skul ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye
178a2(phal chen): mi sgul cing / bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa yongasu mi gtong ba la gnas pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di
178a3(phal chen): ltar sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya ba yongasu mi gtong ba dang / sems can thams cad yong su smin par bya ba dang / rnam par 'dul ba yongasu mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas
178a4(phal chen): thams cad kyi gdung bsapa pa yongasu mi gtong ba dang / dge ba'i banyes gakhyen thams cad la bsnyen pa yongasu mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi gong thams 'du/ de bzhin gshegs pa bsnyen bkur bya ba yo su
178a5(phal chen): gtong ba dang / yon tan thams cad yongasu btsal ba'i phyir/ theg/ pa chen po yongasu mi gtong ba dang / sangs rgyas 'byung ba tham/ sarbadu tshangs par spyad pa spyod cing / tshul khrims bsrung ba yod/ 
178a6(phal chen): su mi gtong ba dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad yongasu mi gtong ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung yongasu btsal zhing yang dag par gzung ba la mkhas pa yongasu mi gtong
178a7(phal chen): ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / smon lam thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa yongasu mi gtong ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po da
178a8(phal chen): ngag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lhag pa'i bsam pa yongasu mi gtong ba la gnas pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongasu mi gtong ba blam
178b1(phal chen): med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyi rnam par lta ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos thams cad kyi tshig rab tu dbye ba bstan par
178b2(phal chen): mkhas pa la ye shes kyi rnam par lta ba dang / dus gsum gyi dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad la ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa dang / rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad lo ye shes kyis
178b3(phal chen): rnam par lta ba dang / chos thams cad kyi tshul gyi sgo la ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi 'arlabs la/ ye shes kyi rnam par lta ba dang / gzungs kyi sgo thams cad
178b4(phal chen): ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad chos bstan pa la ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'jug pa la ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba dang / 
178b5(phal chen): phyogs bcu thams cad bsam gyis mi khyab pa la ye shes kyis na/ ma par lta ba dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyis ye shes snang ba chags pa med pa la ye shes kyis rnam par lta
178b6(phal chen): ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes kyis rnam par lta ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen pos rnam par
178b7(phal chen): gzigs pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos shin tu bstan pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos thams cad rten cing 'brel bar
178b8(phal chen): 'byung bar bstan pa dang / chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur bstan pa dang / chos thams cad nyon mongs pa med par bstan pa dang / chos thams cad mtha' dang dbus med par bstan pa dang / chos thams cad
179a1(phal chen): gnas med par bstan pa dang / chos thams cad rdo rje lta bur bstan pa dang / chos thams cad de bzhin gshegs par bstan pa dang / chos thams cad rab tu zhi bar bstan pa dang / chos
179a2(phal chen): thams cad 'byung ba'i lam du bstan pa dang / chos thams cad don gcig pa'i rang bzhin yongasu ma grub par bstan pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos shin tu
179a3(phal chen): bstan pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams chos thams cad shin tu bstan pa la mkhas pa thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
179a4(phal chen): yongasu dag pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar lhag pa'i bsam pa yongasu dag pa dang / the tsom dang yid gnyis rnam par 'thor ba yongs dag pa dang / lta ba yongasu dag po dang / spyod yul yongasu dag
179a5(phal chen): dang / thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la mos pa yongasasu dag pa dang / tha dad / yang dag par shes pa yongasu dag pa dang / mi 'jigs pa 'o// ngasu dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyi ye
179a6(phal chen): shes kyis rnam par spyod pa yong su dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i yang dag par dam bcas pa thams cad yang dag par bsgrub pa yong su dag pa dang / bsod nams brgya pa'i mtshan gyi mi chen po'i mtshan sum/ 
179a7(phal chen): cu rtsa gnyis dang ldan zhing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub kyi mthar thug pa'i dge ba'i chos dang ldan pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad yongasu dag pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni
179a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yongasu dag pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad yongasu dag pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sra
179b1(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi phyag rgya ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' 'du byed kyi sdug bsngal dang / 'gyur ba'i sdug bsngal shes kyang / sangs rgyas kyi chos
179b2(phal chen): yongasu btsal bas/ sgying lug par byed par 'gyur ba med cing / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la zhum par 'gyur ba med la/ mi 'jigs mi sgeg skrag par mi byed de/ smon lam las mi ldog cing // thams cad
179b3(phal chen): mkhyen pa nyid du sems bskyed pa rgyun mi gcod cing / sangs rgyas chos yongasu btsal ba lo mthar thug pa med pa 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya dang po'o// kye rgyal
179b4(phal chen): ba'i sras gzhan yang byis pa so so'i skye bo rang gi kun nas nyon mongs pras shin tu 'khrugs par gyur pa de dag byang chub sems dpa' la mi snyan par brjod cing / ngan du zer la mi tshul ba dang / rtsub pa'i
179b5(phal chen): ngag 'byin cing / sdigs ri byed pa dang / rdo dang / dbyig pa dang / ma/ tshan chas rdeg cing 'debs kyang / de'i rgyus byang chub sems/ dpa'i spyod pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos yong su btsal ba las/ 
179b6(phal chen): skyo bar mi 'gyur la/ bzod pa dang / mos pa mang bar spyod cing / chos skyon med pa yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du rtogs po'i bzod pa dang ldan pa 'di ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur
179b7(phal chen): ba'i phyag rgya gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi chos zab mo thams cad mkhyen pa nyid dang ldan pa bstan pa'i tshe/ khong nas shes pas 'jug cing / mos pa dang / 
179b8(phal chen): yid ches pa dang / dga' ba dang / mngon par dad par 'gyur ba 'di ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub du 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya gsum po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'
180a1(phal chen): gi shes pas bdag shes par byed cing / thams cad mkhyen pa yi du sems bskyed pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pas byung bas sangs rgyasu 'gyur bar bya'o// bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs/ 
180a2(phal chen): bya'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o// ga pa dang yos pa dang / spro ba chen pos byung ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / mos pa chen po'i rgyus rnam par 'phel ba'i brtson 'grus chen pos/ 'gro ba lnga'i rgyu du 'khor zhing
180a3(phal chen): nyon mongs pa'i sems can rnams rab tu dgrol bar bya'o snyam pa 'di ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa
180a4(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes mu med pa la 'jug kyang de bzhi na gshegs pa'i ye shes las mtshams kyis dpog pa mi byed cing / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das tshang med pa rnams las de bzhin/ 
180a5(phal chen): gshegs pa'i ye shes kun tu mtha' yas pa thos shing / da 'dzin par mi byed cing / yi ge rnam par dgod pa thams/ cad kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes la sa mtshams du
180a6(phal chen): dpog par mi byed pa 'di ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
180a7(phal chen): byang chub tu shin tu mos pa yin te/ mos pa gzhan gyis mi thub pa dang / mos pa zab pa dang / mos pa yangs pa dang / mos pa che ba dang / mos pa sna tshogs dang / mos pa zil gyis mi non pa dang / 
180a8(phal chen): mos pa bla na med pa dang / mos pa brtan pa dang / mos pa las mi mtshungs pa'i mos pa dang ldan zhing / de la bdud thams cad dang / bdud kyi ris kyi lha thams cad dang / mu stegs/ 
180b1(phal chen): can gzhan dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad kyi mos pa de las bzlog par mi nus shing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyi du sems bskyed pa las phyir bzlog par mi nus te/ de lta bu'i mos pa chen po la gnas pa'i byang
180b2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi ldog pa'i mos pa dang ldan pa yin te/ 'di ni phyag rgya drug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa'i mi
180b3(phal chen): zlogs shing / lus dang srog la mi lta bar thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la mngon par phyogs shing / thams cad mkhyen pa nyi du sems bskyed pa sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub snang bas byung bas byang chub sem
180b4(phal chen): dpa'i spyod pa la spyod cing / sangs rgyas kyi byang chub yongasu mi gtong la/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsnyen pa las phyir mi ldog pa 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i
180b5(phal chen): phyag rgya bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub/ sems dpa' theg pa chen po la gnas pa'i rigs kyi bu 'am/ rigs kyi bu mo rnams la sangs rgyas kyi chos yongasu btsal
180b6(phal chen): bas nye bar ston pa byed de/ dge ba'i rtsa ba la yang rab tu gzhog go/ ji ltar na byang chub las phyir mi ldog par 'gyur zhes te/ thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sems kyis kyang rab tu 'dzin to// 'di ni bla
180b7(phal chen): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad la snyoms pa'i sems la gnas shing / 
180b8(phal chen): thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes yang dag par bsgrub pa la brtson pa yin te/ sems can thams cad la yang snying rje chen po bskyed cing / bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub las phyir mi
181a1(phal chen): ldog par chos ston te/ 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'das pa dang / 
181a2(phal chen): ma byod pa dang / nga ltar byung ba'i sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams dang / dge ba'i rtsab thams cad kyi rgyud kyi tshul gcig tu gyur cing // sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rigs rgyun mi gcod pa la shin tu brtson pa dang / thang
181a3(phal chen): mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi lam gyis 'byung ba la gnas pa yin te/ 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzos kyi pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba'i phyag rgya bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po dedag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams
181a4(phal chen): kyi phyag rgya ste/ phyag rgya de dag dang ldan na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams myur du blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing / chos kyi ye shes kyi phyag rgya bla na med pa
181a5(phal chen): 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes snang ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' bla na med pa yang dag
181a6(phal chen): par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu nges te/ sangs rgyas kyi byang chub kyis snang bar gyur pa'i ye shes snang ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad blta ba la ye shes snang ba dang / sems can thams cad kyi shi 'pho dang / skye
181a7(phal chen): ba'i skye mched la ye shes snang ba dang / mdo sde'i chos kyi rnam grangs thams cad la ye shes snang ba dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad kyi rgyu 'thun pas/ byang chub tu sems bskyed cing / dge ba'i rtsa ba
181a8(phal chen): thams cad bsogs pa la ye shes snang ba dang / sems can rnam par gdul ba la ye shes snang ba dang / sems can thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdulta bas de bzhin gshegs pa'i sa la
181b1(phal chen): dgod pa la ye shes snang ba dang / chos kyi tshul 'byam klas shing bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan pa la ye shes snang ba dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byin gyi brlabs la mkhas pa la ye shes snang ba dang / 
181b2(phal chen): rol tu phyin pa thams cad yong su rdzogs par bya ba la ye shes snang ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni ye shes snang ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thang
181b3(phal chen): la bla na med pa'i ye shes snang ba 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi byang chub sems dpa'i gnas sems can thaMd dang / nyan thos thang
181b4(phal chen): dang / rang sangs rgyas thams cad dang / mtshungs pa med pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' yang dag pa'i mtha'i gnas kyis gnas kyang / smon lam thams cad
181b5(phal chen): yongasu rdzogs kyi bar du mngon du mi byed pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa dang po'o// kye rgyal/ ba'i skyes gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' dge ba'i rtsa ba thams cad
181b6(phal chen): bskyed par bya ba yang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad kyis klas par sems bskyed pas bskyed par byed la chos gang la yang mngon par chags pa med pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa
181b7(phal chen): gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sprul pa lta bu'i byang chub sos dpa'i spyod pa la chos thams cad rab tu zhi bas spyod kyang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mgo
181b8(phal chen): rmongs pa yang med pa 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa meng pa gsum pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i spos gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'gro ba thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa'i yid la
182a1(phal chen): bya bas bskal pa brjod med par smon lam chen po yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod kyang yongasu skye ba mi skyed de/ 'di ni byang chub sems
182a2(phal chen): dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad rang bzhin gyis dben pas/ chos thams cad la mi gnas par spyod kyang / thams cad mkhyen
182a3(phal chen): par 'byung ba'i chos yongasu ma rdzogs kyi bar du yongasu mya ngan las 'da' bor mi byed pa 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems
182a4(phal chen): dpa' bskal pa thams cad bskal pa ma yin pa yang shes la rna bskal pa'i grangs kyang rab tu ston te/ de yang yang dag par de/  kho na bzhin du 'gyur ba 'di ni byang chub sems dpa' gnas
182a5(phal chen): mtshungs pa med pa drug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad mngon par 'du bya ba med par yang shes la sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad
182a6(phal chen): yongasu btsal ba'i phyir/ mngon par 'du bya ba'i spros pa yang rgyun mi gcod pa 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems
182a7(phal chen): dpa' khams gsum thams cad sems tsam du 'jug ste/ dus gsum yang sems tsam pu shes la/ sems de yang mtha' dang dbud med par khong du chud ba 'di ni/ byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs/ 
182a8(phal chen): ba med pa brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems can cig gi don du yang // thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la rab tu bzhag pa'i phyir bskal pa brjod med par/ byang chub
182b1(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyad nga spyod la/ sems can gcig gi don du ji lta ba bzhin du// sems can thams cad kyi don du yang thams cad mkhyen pa'i sa la dgod pa'i phyir/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod kyang / dus su spyod
182b2(phal chen): pas yang yongasu mi skyo ba yin te/ 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa yang yongasu rdzogs la/ 
182b3(phal chen): sems can thams cad kyi don du 'gyur pos/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya zhing / ji srid ji srid du 'khor ba/ ngo srod de srid sems can gyi don du phyi phyir zhing tshad med
182b4(phal chen): par bya bar 'gyur ro// sangs rgyas kyi bya yul tu dgod par 'gyu ro snyam pa 'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems
182b5(phal chen): dpa'i gnas mtshungs pa med pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing bang / ba sems dpa'i rnams sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la/ ye shes chen po mtshungs pa med pas gnas pa bla na med pa 'tho
182b6(phal chen): par 'gyur ba dag go// / bam po bdun cu rtsa brgyad pa// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sangs rgyas kyi byang chub tu zhum pa med pa'i
182b7(phal chen): sems bskyed pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa'as 'di ltar bdud dang / bdud kyi ris kyi lha thams cad rab tu pham par bya'o snyam s+ho/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed
182b8(phal chen): pa dang / mu stegs can gzhan dang / phas kyi rgol ba thams cad chos dang 'thun par tshar gcod snyam ste/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang legs par bshad pas/ sems can gyi khams thams cad
183a1(phal chen): rim par bya'o snyam ste/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang chos kyi dbyings song su rdzogs par bya bas/ pha rol tu phyin pa yong su rdzogs par bya ba thams cad yong su rdzogs pa/ 
183a2(phal chen): bya'o snyam ste/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi bsod nams kyi phung po yongasu rdzogs par bya ba yongasu rdzogs par bya'o// yang dag par bsdu bar bya'o snyam ste/ zhum pa med/ 
183a3(phal chen): ba'i sems bskyed pa dang / gter chen po bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu brtsam pa chen po dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa rdzogs par dka' ba yongasu rdzogs par bya'o// snyam ste
183a4(phal chen): zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad bla na med pa'i yongasu smin par bya ba dang / bla na med pa'i gdul bas yongasu smin par bya'o// gdul bar bya'o snyam ste/ zhum pa med
183a5(phal chen): sems bskyed pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad kha do/ gdum dang / kha dog sna tshogs dang / brgya stong du ma la sa 'das pa'i kha dog du mos pas/ bsgyur ba la byang chub
183a6(phal chen): tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o snyam te/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'di ltar sems bskyed pa dang / bdag byang chub
183a7(phal chen): sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa'i tshe/ gang la la zhig gis bdag gi lus la dmigs te/ lag pa dang / rkang pa dang / rna ba dang / sna dang / sha dang / khrag dang / rus pa dang / rkang dang / bu dang /

183b1(phal chen): skyo ba dang ldan pa'i sems gcig kyang mi bskyedado// sems can thams cad la phan pa dang / bde ba'i phyir/ rnam par smin pa la re ba med cing // snying rje chen po sngon du 'gro ba dang / byams pa chen po'i mthas
183b2(phal chen): gtugs pa'i sems bskyed pas/ lus thams cad kyang yongasu gtong snyam ste/ zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' 'di snyam du sems te/ dus
183b3(phal chen): gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad dang / sems can thams cad dang / zhing thams cad dang / 'gro ba thams cad dang / dus thams cad dang / namakha'i khams thams cad
183b4(phal chen): dang / spyod par brtags pa'i khams thams cad dang / mya ngan la sa 'das pa'i khams zhi ba gang ji snyed pa thams cad dang / chos tha dad pa de dag thams cad sems skad cig gcig dang ldan pa'i
183b5(phal chen): shes rab kyis shes pa bya/ rtogs par bya// mngon par rdzogs/ bar 'tshang rgya bar bya/ blta bar bya/ khong du chud par bya/ bsgom par bya/ rnam par bsgom par bya/ mngon par shes
183b6(phal chen): par bya/ yongasu shes par bya// rag tu spang bar bya/ mngon du bya ste/ de dag thams cad la ma brtags/ rnam par ma rtags/ sna tshogasu ma byas/ rnam pa tha dad du ma byas/ tshe du bskyod par ma byas/ 
183b7(phal chen): dmigs par ma byas/ bsgom par ma byas/ rnam par bsgom par ma byas/ gcig tu ma byas/ gnyisu ma byas pa'i ye shes mi gnyis pa gnyis po thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / mtshan nyid med
183b8(phal chen): pa'i ye shes mtshan nyid thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / tog pa med pa'i ye shes rtog pa thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / sna tshogasu gyur pa med pa'i ye shes sna tshogs thams cad rab tu shes pa dang
184a1(phal chen): dang / rnam pa tha dad par gyur pa med pa'i ye shes rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / 'jig rten du gyur pa med pa'i se shes 'jig rten thams cad rab tu shes pa na/ 
184a2(phal chen): 'jig rten gyi khamasu phyin pa med pa'i ye shes 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / dus su gyur pa med pa'i ye shes dus thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / sems can gyi sar gyur pa
184a3(phal chen): med pa'i ye shes sems can gyi khams thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / mngon par shes pa thams cad las gyen du 'phags pa'i ye shes mngon par chags pa'i spyod yul gyi mthar thug pa dang / gnas
184a4(phal chen): med pa la gzhol ba'i ye shes gnas thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / kun nas nyon mongs pa med pa'i ye shes kun nas nyon mongs pa thams cad rab tu shes pa dang / mi zad pa'i mthar phyin pa'i ye
184a5(phal chen): shes zad pa thams cad rab tu zhes pa dang / chos kyi dbyings la/ gzhol ba'i ye shes 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad// lus yongasu ston pa dang / brjod pa dang / tshig dang / sgra dang / 
184a6(phal chen): dbyangs dang / bral ba'i ye shes sgra dbyangs brjod med pa rab tu brjod pa dang / rang bzhin gcig pa'i ye shes rang bzhin med pa rab tu rtogs pa dang / spyod yul gcig la zhugs pa'i ye shes spyod
184a7(phal chen): yul tha dad pa yongasu ston pas brjod pa chen po'i byin gyi brlabs yang dag par bstan pa'i phyir/ brjod med pa'i chos thams cad mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o// sems can thams cad
184a8(phal chen): yongasu smin par bya ba dang / gdul ba'i phyir thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi sa chen po mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar bya'o// cho 'phrul chen po dang / rnam par 'phrul pa'i cho 'phrul yang 'gro ba ste
184b1(phal chen): du bstan par bya'o snyam pa 'di ni zhum ba med pa'i sems bskyed pa bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhum pa med pa'i sems bskyed pa ste/ de dag la gnas/

184b3(phal chen): lhag pa'i bsam pa ri bo lta bu ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras 'di la byang chub sems dpa' thams cad mkhyen pa'i chos yid la bya bas rtag tu rgyun mi 'chad par brtson pa yin te/ 'di ni bla
184b4(phal chen): na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lhag pa'i bsam bra ri bo lta bu dang po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhon yang byang chub sems dpa' chos thams cad mi dmigs pas/ chos
184b5(phal chen): thams cad la rang bzhin gyis stong par rnam par lta ba 'di/ ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu/ lhag pa'i bsam pa ri bo lta bu gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal
184b6(phal chen): ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' bskal pa mtha' dong dpung med par chos dkar po thams cad kyi spyod pa dang ldan po'i sems bskyed pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod
184b7(phal chen): cing / chos dkar po yang dag par blangs pa thams cad la nan tan du byed pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes tshad med pa yang khong du chud par byed pa 'di ni bla na mod pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lhag ze'i
184b8(phal chen): bsam pa ri bo lta bu gsum pa'o// kyi rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad kyis dge ba'i bshes gnyen la tshul dang 'dra ba'i rim gro byed cing / re ba med pa'i sems
185a1(phal chen): / bskyed pa chos rku ba dang bral ba nan tan du byed de/ gzhan du na 'di la/ bdag gis de bas kyang rim gro dang / bkur bsti rgya chen po bskyed par bya'o// 'di lnga yongasu gtang ba thams cad
185a2(phal chen): kyang dbul bar bya'o snyam pa 'di ni/ bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lhag pa'i bsam pa ri bo lta bu bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gnan yang byang chub sems dpa' sems can thams cad las sdug
185a3(phal chen): bsngal gyi rnam pa bzod par byed de/ lus la gnod pa dang / srog la 'bab pa yang nyam su len cing / gshe ba dang / mi snyan du zer ba dang / sdigs pa dang / smod pa dang / khyad gsod pa thams cad la bzod par
185a4(phal chen): byed de/ de'i rgyus nyams par mi 'gyur/ 'khrug par mi 'gyur/ nga 'khrug pa dang / rnam par 'khrug par mi byed/ de'i rgyus sems can rnams la snying rje chen po'i go bgos pa yang yongs
185a5(phal chen): mi 'dor / rgyun mi gcod cing de bas kyang shas cher snying rje chen po/ rnam par 'phel bar byed// rgyun mi gcod do// kye rgyal za sras de ci'i phyir zhe na de ni byang chub sems dpa' de chos thams cad
185a6(phal chen): yang dag par ji lta ba bzhin du 'byung ba'i btang snyoms dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i chos thams cad rab tu rtogs pa'i bzod pa dang / dang nges pa'i dbang dang ldan pa'i phyir te/ 'dini bla na med pa yang

185a8(phal chen): ba dang / mi la dbang sgyur ba dang / gzugs la dbang sgyur ba dang / stobs la dbang sgyur ba dang / 'khor lo dbang sgyur ba dang / 'dod pa la dbang sgyur ba dang / rgyal srid la dbang sgyur ba dang / dbang phyug la dbang

185b3(phal chen): dpung gnyen tshol ba dang / chos la gnas pa chos la don du gnyer ga chos la mngon par dga' ba/ chos la tshol ba yin te/ chos nyid la bsam gtan 'cha' zhing gnas pa yin// de rnam pa de lta bu'i 'de
185b4(phal chen): ba'i bye brag dang / 'grogs pas/ bdud kyi yul la gnas pam yi na/ kye rgyal ba'i sras de yang ci'i phyir zhe na/ de ni byang chub sems dpas sngon sems can thams cad bdag gis bdud kyi yul
185b5(phal chen): las rnam par bzlog par bya'o// sangs rgyas kyi yul la dgod bar bya'o zhes sems bskyed pa'i phyir te/ 'di ni bla na ma/ da ba yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lhag pa'i bsam pa

185b8(phal chen): mi 'jigs po 'di lta bu dang ldan pa yin te/ de ring kho na bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu 'gyur ba snyam du 'dzin pas de phyin ched kyang / 'di ltar sems can thams cad yongasu smin/ 
186a1(phal chen): par smin par bya ba'i phyir/ bskal pa tshad med par/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyad pa spyod pa 'di ni bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu lhag pa'i bsam pa ri bo lta bu

187b1(phal chen): yong su shes pa'i tshul gyis/ shin tu zhugs pa yin te/ 'di ni blan med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu ye shes kyis 'jug pa rgya mtsho lta bu bzhi pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems

198b8(phal chen): gcig tu rnam par spyod pa phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhe na/ rnam pa gzhan du ma 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i
199a1(phal chen): rtsab 'dis dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang gcig cing mnyam par 'jug pa yongasu rdzogs pa phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs par 'gyur ram 'gyur zhen
199a2(phal chen): rnam pa gzhan du ma 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ bdag gi dge ba'i rtsa ba 'dis dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams dang tha mi dad pa phun sum tshogs par gyur cig/ phun sum tshogs
199a3(phal chen): par 'gyur ram 'gyur na na/ rnam pa gzhan du ma 'gyur bar de ltar phun sum tshogs par gyur cig ces bya ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba
199a4(phal chen): yongasu bsngo ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams dge ba'i rtsa ba yongasu bsngo ba bla na med pa 'thob pa ra 'gyur ba dag go/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang
199a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes khong du chud pa ste/ bcun/ nga zhe na/ 'di ltar gtong ba'i sems kyis rnam par 'phrul/ ba'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos zang
199a6(phal chen): la mos pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes mtha' dang dpung med pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / dris pa thams cad kyi the tsom gcod pa'i
199a7(phal chen): ye shes khong du chud pa dang / don shes pa la 'jug pa'i ye shes khong du chud ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung la mkhas pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la yid ches
199a8(phal chen): par 'jug pa'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas la bskyed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba chung yang rung ste/ thams cad de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes tshad med par 'gyur bar yid ches par byas shing / 
199b1(phal chen): chos dkar po thams cad yongasu rdzogs par byed pa'i ye shes khong du chud ba dang / byang chub sems dpa'i rnam par spyod pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i ye shes khong du chud pa dang / 
199b2(phal chen): sems kyi skad cig gcig gis sangs rgyas kyi zhing brjod med par 'gro zhing gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ sems kyi skad cig cig gi ye shes khong du chud pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub mngon
199b3(phal chen): bar 'tshang rgya ba dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad la 'jug pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bstan pa dang / gzung ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gsung sna tshogs la 'jug pa'i
199b4(phal chen): rgyan gyi ye shes khong du chud pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po da dgra ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes khong du chud pa rnams te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs
199b5(phal chen): rgyas thams cad kyi ye shes khong du chung ba bla na med pa 'thob/ bar 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa mtha'
199b6(phal chen): dang dpung med pa rnams te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas thams cad la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / chos kyi dbyings thams cad 'jug pa la sems bskyed pa rgya
199b7(phal chen): chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi zhing dang / dus dang / chos kyi dbyingasu 'jug pa la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbung med pa dang / chos thams cad na mkha' dang
199b8(phal chen): mnyam par lta ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad la rgya cher brtag pa la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / 
200a1(phal chen): dus gsum gyi sangs rgyas thams cad yid la bya ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbung med pa dang / las dang rnam par smin pa bsam gyis mi khyab par 'jug
200a2(phal chen): ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad yongasu dag par bya ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbang med pa dang / 'khor gyi dkyil
200a3(phal chen): 'khor thang du 'jug pa la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi dbyings rnam par blta ba la sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dpung med/ 
200a4(phal chen): pa'o/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems bskyed pa rgya chen po mtha' dang dbung med pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas
200a5(phal chen): kyi chos mtha' dang dpung med pa thams cad kyi ye shes chen po rgya mtsho lta bu bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa'
200a6(phal chen): rnams kyi gter te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos thams cad la 'grang bas sbyar ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la nges par rtogs pa'i gter dang / chos thams cad la gzung snang ba'i
200a7(phal chen): gter dang / chos thams cad la tha dad pa yang dag par shes pas rab tu snang ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la brjod med pa'i tshul la mkhas par khong du chud pa'i gter dang / sangs rgyas
200a8(phal chen): kyi rnam par 'phrul pa dang / cho 'phrul thams cad la so sor rtog cing lta ba'i gter dang / chos thams cad la mnyam pa nyid mngon par bsgrub par mkhas pa'i gter dang / sangs rgyas thar
200b1(phal chen): mthong ba dang mi 'bral ba'i gter dang / sgyu ma lta bu'i bskal pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa yongasu grub par 'jug pa la mkhas pa'i gter dang / sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la dga' ba
200b2(phal chen): dang / rab tu dga' ba dang / mos pa chen po rab tu rnyed pa'i gter ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi gter te/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa'
200b3(phal chen): rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi chos kyi ye shes kyi gter bla na med pa 'thob pas sems can thams cad 'dul ba la brtson par byed pa dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa/ 
200b4(phal chen): rnams kyi sdom pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad la mi 'jug mi 'khrul pa'i sdom pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad la bsam pa'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems
200b5(phal chen): dpa' thams cad la bsam pa rlabs po che'i sdom pa dang / dge ba'i bshes gnyen thams cad la bsam pa mi 'od ra ba'i sdom pa dang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas yid la bya ba
200b6(phal chen): thams cad la yongasu mi rgyu ba'i sdom pa dang / byang chub sems dpa' chung za ba'i lam thams cad rnam par bzlog pa'i sdom pa dang / sems can thams cad la khong khro ba med pa'i sdom pa dang / 
200b7(phal chen): dge ba'i rtsa ba brtsam pa thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba'i sdom pa dang / bdud thams cad rab tu pham par bya ba'i sdom pa dang / pha rol tu phyin pa thams cad yong su rdzogs par bya ba'i sdom pa'o// 
200b8(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sdom pa ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams ye shes chen po'i sdom pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba
201a1(phal chen): dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar bskal pa brjod med par tshe'i tshad byin gyis rlob pas tshe
201a2(phal chen): la dbang ba dang / ting 'dzin grangs med pa la nges par rtogs par gzhog cing / ye shes kyis 'jug pa'i tshul gyis sems la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad rgyan rnam par dab ba du
201a3(phal chen): mas rab tu brgyan par byin gyis brlab par ston pa'i tshul gyis yo byad la dbang ba dang / dus ji lta ba bzhin du las kyi rnam par smin pa byin gyis brlob pas las la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi
201a4(phal chen): khams thams cad skye ba ston pas skye ba la dbang ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad sangs rgyas kyi yongasu grang bar lta bas mos pa la dbang ba dang / dus dang shing gang du 'dod
201a5(phal chen): par mngon par 'tshang rgya bas/ smon lam la dbang ba dang / rdzu 'phrul gyi rnam par 'phrul pa thams cad yongasu ston pa/ sa/ rdzu 'phrul la dbang ba dang / chos kyi sgo dang / snang ba mtha' dang
201a6(phal chen): dbus med pa yang dag par ston pas chos la dbang ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / mi bsnyengs pa skad cig skad cig tu go bar yongasu ston pas/ ye shes la dbang ba'o// kye rgyal
201a7(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po dadag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi dbang ste/ de dag la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams sangs rgyas thams cad kyi byang chub kyi mnga'i pha rol tu phyin pa ye shes kyi rnam

201b1(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / lus la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / spyod yul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang /

201b4(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu grang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad sems can med pas sprul ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi 'du shes
201b5(phal chen): kyi rnam par byin gyis brlab pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad la dus la bab na chos ston pa rgyu na mi gcod pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams cad
201b6(phal chen): du sprul pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad skra'i sbubs gcig tu btsud kyang gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad 'jig rten
201b7(phal chen): gyi khams byin gyis brlabs te/ pha rol shes par byed pa dang / yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon cha
201b8(phal chen): dbang yongs ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad ldan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi gzugs dang / kha dog dang mtshan dang / cho ga dang / spyod lam yongasu ston par

202a5(phal chen): zad pa la 'jug pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad du/ kyil mo krung gcig gis rgyas par 'gengs pa'i lus gcig yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing
202a6(phal chen): thams cad rang gi lus su chud par yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad rab tu bskyod kyang / sems can 'jigs par mi 'gyur ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams
202a7(phal chen): cad kyi rgyan rnam par phye ba zhing gcig tu yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing gcig gis rnam par phye zhing thams cad kyi rgyan rnam par phye bar yongasu ston pa dang / zhing thams cad kyi de bzhin
202a8(phal chen): gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gcig gis yongasu khyab par sems can thams cad la ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul ba dang / zhing phra ba dang / che ba dang / 
202b1(phal chen): yangs pa dang / rgya che ba dang / zab pa dang snrel zhi dang / spyi'i tshugasu rgyu ba dang / gzhi mnyam pa la 'jug par yong su gzhol bas phyogs kyi drab rnam par phye ba la 'jug par sems can ma lus pa thams cad

202b3(phal chen): rnams kyi chos la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos thams cad chos gcig tu yang dag par gzhol bar bya ba dang / chos gcig po chos thams cad yang dag par gzhol bar byed kyang
202b4(phal chen): sems can gyi bsam pa dang / mi 'gal bar rnam par dmigs pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pas sgrub par khong du chud bar bya ba pha rol gyi go bar bya ba'i rnam
202b5(phal chen): par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad 'du shes dang bral bar sems ca na mang pos khong du chud par bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad la tshul gcig tu 'jug cing tshul mtha'
202b6(phal chen): yas par ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad la brjod myed par 'jug cing sgo brgya stong gi pha rol gyi rgyud du bstan pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad sgo kun nas rgyu ba'i yi ge'i

203a1(phal chen): la chags pa med pa'i mthar phyin cing mtha' dang dbus med pa'i sgyu ma'i dra ba rnam pa tha dad pa la 'jug pa med pas bskal pa mu med par mi zad par sems can la ston pa'i rnam

203a4(phal chen): kyi lus kyi 'dus su byin gyi rlob pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi sku sangs rgyas gcig gi skur mos shing / 'jug pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas gcig gi sku

203a7(phal chen): rnam par ldang ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / lus gcig gis mngon par sangs rgyas shing sems can snyed kyi lus su yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad kyi lus sem/

203b4(phal chen): ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bskal pa 'grangs pa mu med pa thams cad smon lam gyi rgyun mi gcod pa'i rnam par 'phrul shra dang / rnam par shes pa'i lus las gyen du bskyod de/ ye shes kyi
203b5(phal chen): lus la'ang mi gnas pa'i smon lam la dbang bsgyur bas/ lus thams cad yongasu ston pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang rang gi lus tshang gyur pas pha rol gyi tshogs kyi smon lam thams cad
203b6(phal chen): yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad yongasu smin par bya ba'i smon lam las phyir mi ldog pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / bskal pa 'grangs pa thams cad byang chub
203b7(phal chen): kyi spyod pas rgyas par dgang ba'i smon lam rgyun mi 'chad ba'i rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sgra'i sbubs gcig tu mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i smon lam gyi stobs kyis sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad du
203b8(phal chen): rgyas par dgang zhing / 'jig rten gyi khams brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa/ sems can gcig tu ston pa'i smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos kyi tshig gcig brjod pas chos kyi dbyings
204a1(phal chen): ma lus pa thams cad rgyas par bkang ste/ chos kyi sprin chen po byung ba las chos bdud rtsi'i na rab tu 'bab cing / rig pa dang rnam par grol ba'i grog spang ba dang / yang / 
204a2(phal chen): bA kho na nyid kyi chos kyi 'brug smra mngon par 'thubyung bas sems can gyi khams thams cad yong su mas par bya ba'i sngon lam chen po yongasu rdzogs par bya bas rnam par bya ba'i rnam par 'phrul ba ste/ 
204a3(phal chen): ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi smon lam la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal po'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi spyod yul la rnam par 'phrul pa
204a4(phal chen): ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni chos kyi dbyings kyi spyod yul dang yang ldan la sems can gyi khams kyi spyod yul du'ang sna // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub

204a6(phal chen): ngan las 'das pa'i spyod yul dang yang ldan la 'khor ba'i spyod yul las kyang mi g.yo'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa'/ mas ni thams cad mkhyen pa nyid kyi spyod yul dang ldan la
204a7(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i spyod yul gyi rgyud kyang rgyun mi gtsang // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni zhi ba dang / rab tu zhi ba dang / phye bar zhi ba'i spyad yul dang yang ljon la/ sems can ma
204a8(phal chen): go b.rab tu ma ni ba nye bar ma zhi ba'i phyid yul ci rnams kyang rnam par mi spong ngo // kyi rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni blang ba med pa dang / dong baming ba dang / spro bameng ba dang / ma ma
204b1(phal chen): ba dang / mtshan ma med pa dang / dngos po meng ba dang / rnam par mi dmigs pa dang / bar snang dang mnyam pa'i spyod yul dang yang ldan la/ sems can smos pa dang / mtshan ma thams cad dmigs pa'i srung
204b2(phal chen): yul can rnams kyi gnas na yang snango // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni stobs dang rgya sa rgya sa kyi chu po sus maman tshad spyod pa das jug no sa rgya
204b3(phal chen): rnam par mi spong ngo // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni bsam gtan dang / rnam par thar pa dang / rtogs pa dang / ye shes dben pa'i spyod yul dang yang ldan la/ 'jig rten gyi kham
204b4(phal chen): thams cad skye bar yang sna // kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni de bzhin gshegs pa'i spyod pa dang / mngon par 'tshang rgya bo dang / sangs rgyas kyi rgyan dang / spyod yul
204b5(phal chen): thams cad kyang thob la/ nyan thos dang rang sangs rgyas thams cadaspyod lam dang / cho ga yang yongasu ston to// kye rgyal ba sras bcu po de dag ni// byang chub sems dpa'i rnams
204b6(phal chen): spyod yul la rnam par 'phrul ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar tha dad pa yang dag par
204b7(phal chen): shes pa'i ye shes mi zad pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rmongs pa med pa'i gzungs thams cad thob pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / smon lam shin tu rnam par gdon mi za ba bstan pa dang
204b8(phal chen): sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi dbang po yong su 'dzin pa dang / khong du chud pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / rang gi sems kyi ye shes pha rol gyi sems kyi ye shes dang sems gcig
205a1(phal chen): las sems can thams cad kyi spyod pa dang / rnam par g.yo bar byed pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / bag la
205a2(phal chen): nyal ba dang / bag chags dang / nyon mongs pa'i nad la gang dang 'byor pa'i sman yang dag par gtong ba'i ye shes rnam par 'phrul pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu la skad cig gcig gis
205a3(phal chen): 'jug pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / dus gsum gyi bskal pa'i grangs thams cad la chags pa med pa'i ye shes yangs pa sems can gzhan gyis thob par byed pa'i ye shes la rnam par
205a4(phal chen): 'phrul pa dang / thogs pa med pa'i sems kyi skad cig tu mngon par 'tshang rgya bar 'gro ba thams cad yongasu ston pa'i ye she sa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gcig gi 'du shes kyis/ 
205a5(phal chen): sems can ma lus pa thams cad kyi las dang bya ba la/ mngon sum du ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems/ can gcig gi sgra dbyangs kyis sgra thams cad la 'jug pa/ yongasu ston
205a6(phal chen): pa'i ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ye shes la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems
205a7(phal chen): dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad lus yongasu ston kyang / lus gcig tu dmigs pa'i mngon par shes pa la rnam/ 
205a8(phal chen): bar 'phrul pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor dang / chos bstan pa yongasu 'dzin pa'i mngon par shes
205b1(phal chen): ba la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gcig gi sems la dmigs pas byang chub kyi rgyud 'arjod med gang tshang rgya zhing sems can thams cad kyi sems kyis go bar byung ba'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 
205b2(phal chen): dbyangs gcig gis 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad go bar byed cing / sgra rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad shes par byed pas/ sems can gzhan gyi sems kyi rlung phyin par byed pa'i mngon par shes pa la/ rnam par
205b3(phal chen): 'phrul ba dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sngon gyi mtha'i chung drug pa'i bskal pa/ sems kyi skad cig gcig gos rje su drad shing shes pas/ las kyi 'bras bu rnam par smi pa ji lta ba bzhin du mngan sum du
205b4(phal chen): ston cing / sems can gyi go bar byed pa'i mngon par shes ba la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams tham/ sa cad brgyan par bya ba'i mngon par shes pa la/ rnam par 'phrul
205b5(phal chen): dang / dus thams cad mnyam pa lta du 'jug pa'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sangs rgyas thams ca/ da kyi byang chub tu spyod pa'i smon lam yang dag par bskyed pa dang / chos
205b6(phal chen): snang ba rab tu dgye ba'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / lha dang / klu dang / gnod sbyin dang / dri za dang / lha ma yin dang / na mkha' lding dang / mi 'am ci dang / lto 'phye chen po dang / brgya
205b7(phal chen): byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po thams cad kyis mngon par shes pa nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i stobs bcu dang / 
205b8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa'i dge pa'i rtsab thams cad kyis yongasu bsrung ba'i mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / kye rgyal ba'i sras mdor na/ byang chub sems dpa' ni mngon par
206a1(phal chen): shes pas chos thams cad la yang dag par gzhol ba yin te/ bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mngon par shes pa la rnam par 'phrul ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'ang
206a2(phal chen): ngag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa/ rdul shin tu phra ba gcig tu 'dzud pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam
206a3(phal chen): bar 'phrul pa dang / rdul shin tu phra ba gcig la chos kyi dbyings thams cad dang / mnyam pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing gcig yongasu ston pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / rgya mtsho thams cad kyi chu'i phung po chen po ba
206a4(phal chen): spu'i khung bu gcig tu blugs te/ chos kyi dbyings dang / mnyam pa'i 'jig rten gyi kham su 'gro yang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams brjod med pa
206a5(phal chen): yang brjod med pa rang gi lus su btsud/ bya ba thams cad yo/ ngasu ston pa la mkhas pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa da/ khor yug dang rdo rje'i ri bsam gyis mi khyab pa thams cad ba spu'i khung bu
206a6(phal chen): gcig tu bres te/ 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'gro yang / sems can rnams sdang bar mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / bskal pa brjod du med pa'i yang brjod med pa bskal pa gcig tu byin gyi
206a7(phal chen): rlab te/ bskal pa gcig la brjod med pa yang brjod med pa'i bskal pa 'du ba dang / 'jig pa ston kyang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thang du
206a8(phal chen): chus 'jig pa yongasu bstan pa dang / me dang rlung gi 'jig pa yongasu bstan kyang sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'tshig cing
206b1(phal chen): chu dang / me dang rlung gis 'jig kyang longs spyod dang / nye bar spyod pa thams cad kyis yongasu gang bar byas shing / sems can la kun tu ston pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul ba dang / 'jig rten gyi khams bsam gyis mi
206b2(phal chen): khyab pa lag pa'i mthil gyis blangs te/ 'jig rten gyi khams brjod med pa'i yang brjod med par bkod kyang / sems can la gnod par mi 'gyur ba'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / zhing thams cad namakha'i
206b3(phal chen): rang bzhin du yongasu bstan pas/ sems can go bar byed pa'i rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rdzu 'phrul la rnam par 'phrul pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i
206b4(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sto/ sa la rnam par 'phrul ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar yongs sngon bar bya ba dang / 'dul ba ma gtong bas sems can gyi stobs la rnam par
206b5(phal chen): 'phrul pa dang / namakha' brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa/ thams cad rgyan rnam par phye bas brgyan par yongasu ston pa sa zhing gi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / lus thams cad lus med
206b6(phal chen): par 'jug pas chos kyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / spyod pa rgyun mi gcod pas bskal pa'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / gnyid kyis log pa sangs par byed pas sangs rgyas kyi stobs la
206b7(phal chen): rnam par 'phrul pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa thams cad skyed cing rab tu 'dzin pa'i phyir spyod pa'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yang dag par sgrol bas sangs
206b8(phal chen): rgyas kyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / chos thams cad bdag po med par mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir/ rang zung gi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes ma lus par
207a1(phal chen): mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i phyir/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa dang / sems can thams cad yongasu mi gtong bas/ snying rje chen po'i stobs la rnam par 'phrul
207a2(phal chen): ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras sems can la rnam par 'phrul pa bzung ba man chad/ stobs la rnam par 'phrul pa
207a3(phal chen): yan chad kyi bar du/ bcu po de dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par 'phrul pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras byang chub sems dpa' gang gis rnam par 'phrul pa bcu po de dag thob par gyur pa de ni 'dod na/ bla na med
207a4(phal chen): pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par 'tshang rgya'o// / mi 'dod na mngon par 'tshang mi rgya'o// 'dod na mngon par 'tshang yang rgyal spyod pa yang rgyun mi gcong // kye rgyal ba'i sras/ de ci'i phyir/ 
207a5(phal chen): na/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni smon lam chen pos byung / ba ste/ sgo mtha' yas pa'i rnam par 'phrul pa yongasu bstan pa la mkhas pa'i phyir ro// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub
207a6(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par rtse ba ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar byang chub sems dpa' sems can gyi lus la zhing gi lus byin gyis rlob pa byed kyang / sems can gyi lus 'byed par mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse
207a7(phal chen): bdang po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' zhing gi lus la sems can gyi lus byin gyis rlob pa byed kyang / zhing gi lus 'dres par yang mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal
207a8(phal chen): ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas kyi sku la sems can gyi lus byin gyis rlob kyang / sangs rgyas kyi sku dpa' bar mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtsib gsum pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang
207b1(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus la de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku yongasu ston kyang / nyan thos dang / rang sangs rgyas kyi lus rgya chen por yang mi byed pa 'di ni/ rnam par rtse ba bzhi pa'o// 
207b2(phal chen): kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang chub sems dpa' spyod pa'i lus la mngon par 'tshang rgya ba'i lus yongasu ston kyang / spyod pa'i rgyun mi gcod pa de ni rnam par rtse ba lnga pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub
207b3(phal chen): sems dpa' mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa'i lus la spyod pa yongasu ston kyang / mngon par rdzogs par byang chub pa nye bar len par yang mi byed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba drug pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / 
207b4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' mya ngan las 'das pa'i dbyings 'khor ba'i rgyun yongasu ston kyang / mya ngan las 'das pa la mngon par chags pa mi skyed pa de ni rnam par rtse ba bdun pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang byang
207b5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' 'khor ba la mya ngan las 'das pa yong/ ston kyang / yongs mya ngan las 'da' bas shin tu mya ngan las 'da' bar mi byed pa 'di ni rnam par rtseb brgyad pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sra
207b6(phal chen): gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' mnyam par bzhag bzhin du 'di lta ste/ 'ong ba dang / 'gro ba dang / 'greng ba dang / 'dug pa'i bya ba thams cad yongasu ston kyang / ting 'dzin gyi mnyam pa nyid 'khrug par mi
207b7(phal chen): byed pa 'di ni rnam par rtse ba dgu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras gzhan yang / byang chub sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs pa gcig gi zhabs kyi drung nas chos thos nas/ lus kyang mi snang bar mi byed la ting 'dzin gyi stom
207b8(phal chen): kyis de bzhin gshegs pa'i 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor brjod med pa'i yang brjo med pa gzhan dang gzhan du lus rnam par dgod pas ldang yang lus tha dad par yang mi byed/ ting 'dzin tha dad par yang mi byed la
208a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa de dag las kyang chos nyan cing thos nas kyang 'dzin cing kun chub par byed la/ ting 'dzin la snyoms par 'jug cing / chos dri'i gzung ba'i rgyun kyang mi gcod nga// de de/ 
208a2(phal chen): ltar mnyam par bzhag bzhin du lus mi snang bar yang mi byed la/ ting 'dzin gyi lus dang sgo mngon par sgrub pa re re las kyang brjod med pa'i yang brjod med pa'i ting 'dzin gyi lus dang / sgo mngon par sgrub cing / de lta
208a3(phal chen): bu'i tshul gyis bskal pa thams cad zad par gyur kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i ting 'dzin gyi sgo mngon par sgrub pa'i mtha' gang yang med pa de ni rnam par rtse ba bcu pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ 
208a4(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi rnam par rtse ba ste/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen pos rnam par rol pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i
208a5(phal chen): sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yu/ la ti/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar chos kyi dbyings mtha' yas pa'i sgo la 'jug par sems can la/ yongasu ston pa'i yul dang / 'jig
208a6(phal chen): rten gyi khams thams cad rgyan rnam pa sna tshogs/ du ma dang mngon par sgrub pa 'gro ba thams cad kyis rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i yul dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad/ sprul pa mngon par sgrub pa/ 
208a7(phal chen): rnam par dmigs par bya ba'i yul dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku byang chub sems dpa'i lus su mngon par sgrub pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i lus de bzhin gshegs pa'i skur mngon par sgrub pa'i yul
208a8(phal chen): dang / nam mkha'i khams 'jig rten gyi khamasu mngon par sgrub pa dang / 'jig rten gyi khams na mkha'i khamasu mngon par sgrub pa'i yul dang / mya ngan las 'das pa 'khor bar mngon par sgrub pa dang / 
208b1(phal chen): 'khor ba mya ngan las 'das pa mngon par sgrub pa'i yul dang / sems can gcig gi skad brjod pas/ sangs rgyas kyi chos thams cad bstan par mngon par sgrub pa'i yul dang / mtha' yas pa'i sgo nas lus kun
208b2(phal chen): tu ston cing / lus gcig tu byin gyis brlab pa dang / lus rnam pa tha dad pa thams cad mngon par sgrub pa'i yul dang / lus gcig gis chos kyi dbyings thams cad rgyas par dgang ba'i yul dang // sems can
208b3(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems bskyed pa'i skad cig re re la/ mtha' yas pa'i sgo mngon par sgrub cing / rnam par 'tshang rgya ba'i yulo// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi yul te/ de dag
208b4(phal chen): la gnas shing / byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gagus pa'i ye shes chen po'i yul/ bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyurasha dag go// / bam po brgyad cung / 
208b5(phal chen): kye rtul ba'i bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa'/ rnams kyi stobs te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten thams cad dang 'du 'dzi med pa'i phyir bsam pa'i stobs dang / sangs
208b6(phal chen): rgyas kyi chos thams cad la sgyid lug pa meng par bya ba'i phyir/ lhag pa'i bsam pa'i stobs dang / byang chub sems dpa'i brtsams pa thams cad mthar phyin par bya ba yong su bstan pa'i phyir sbyor ba'i stobs
208b7(phal chen): dang / 'gro ba thams cad kyi sems dang spyod pa rab tu shes par bya ba'i phyir ye shes kyi stobs dang / bsam pa thams cad yongasu rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir sman lam gyi stobs dang / phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug
208b8(phal chen): par rgyun chad pa med par bya ba'i phyir spyod pa'i stobs dang / theg pa thams cad kyi 'byung bar kun tu bstan pa dang / theg pa chen po las phyir mi ldog par bya ba'i phyir theg pa'i stobs dang / skra'i sbubs gcig tu
209a1(phal chen): sangs rgyas 'byung ba thams cad dang / 'jig rten gyi khams yong su dag pa thams cad kun tu bstan pa'i phyir/ rnam par 'phrul pa'i stobs dang / sems bskyed pa thams cad la byang chub
209a2(phal chen): tu rnam par 'tshang rgya ba dang / mi 'bral ba'i phyir byang chub kyi stobs dang / chos kyi tshig gcig brjod pas sems can thams cad kyi bsam pa dang / dbang po ma lus pa lhag ma med pa mtha' dag rtogs par bya ba'i phyir/ 
209a3(phal chen): chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i stobs te/ kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi stobs te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes dang / 
209a4(phal chen): stobs bcu dang ldan pa'i mchog tu 'gyur ba 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mi 'jigs pa ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang
209a5(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams ni sgra thams cad 'dzin pa'i gzungs rab tu thob pa yin te/ de 'di snyam du/ shar phyogs dang // byang phyogs dang / lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs nas/ ston pa la la shig
209a6(phal chen): bdag gi gan du byon te/ 'gro ba chen po brgya stong rab tu bshad par gyur na/ bdag gis de gzung bar mi nus snyam du mi sems te/ byang chub sems dpas rgyu yang rje su mi mthong ngo // rgyu yang rje su mi mthong
209a7(phal chen): bas/ mi 'jigs pa chen po'i dam pa thob cing / brtan la zhum pa med pa'i yid kyis 'gro ba thams cad la ci 'dod pa de dris shig ces skabs 'byed pa 'di ni/ mi 'jigs pa dang po'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras
209a8(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni yi ge dang / don brjod pa dang / sgra dang skad thams cad kyi mtshams sbyar ba rab tu rtogs par bya ba dang / de bzhin gshegs pas dbang bskur ba'i stobs pa thogs pa med
209b1(phal chen): bdam pa'i pha rol tu phyin pa thob pa yin te/ de dag 'di snyam du shar phyogs dang / byang phyogs dang / lho phyogs dang / nub phyogs nas la la zhig 'ongs te/ bdag la chos kyi the tshom chen po zhig dris par gyur na// bdag
209b2(phal chen): gis lan mi lon pa snyam du mi sems te/ byang chub sems dpas rgyu yang rjesu mi mthong ngo // rgyu yang rjesu mi mthong bas mi 'jigs pa chen po'i dam pa thob cing / 'gro ba thams cad kyi dri ba yongasu dri ba ci yod pa
209b3(phal chen): bstan pa dang / 'jigs shing spu ldang ba med par byos la gang 'dod pa de dag dris shig ces skabs 'byed pa 'di ni mi 'jigs pa gnyis pa'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams ni stong pa'i chos
209b4(phal chen): khong du chud bar rtogs pa yin te// bdag dang bdag gi dang / byed pa dro dang / byed 'jug pa dang / tshor ba po dang / srog dang / gso ba dang / gang zag dang / phung po dang / khams dang / skye mche du lta ba dang bral te/ 
209b5(phal chen): sems na mkha' dang mtshungs pa'i rjesu song ba de dag 'di ste ma du bdag la la la zhig gis lus dang / ngag dang / yid kyis gnod par bya ba 'am/ cig tu mi 'gyur ba 'am sum du sems pa med
209b6(phal chen): byang chub sems dpa' sa mtshan ma yang rje su mi mthong // de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'di ltar skyes bu dam pa ni bdag tu 'dzin pa dang / bdag gir 'dzin pa dang bral ba'i phyir te/ mtshan ma yang rje su mi mthong bas/ mi 'jig

215a2(phal chen): sum tshogs pa dang / 'gro ba thams cad dge ba'i bshes gnyen brten pa las phyir mi ldog cing / de bzhin gshegs pa la rim gror bya ba rgyun mi gcod pa de ni byang chub sems dpa'i chos ma 'dres pa ste/ 'di ni

215a4(phal chen): chos ma 'dres pa bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi las te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad yongasu spyad
215a5(phal chen): las dang / sangs rgyas thams cad bsnyen bkur ba'i las dang // byang chub sems dpa'i grogs thams cad dang dge ba'i rtsa ba/ gcig tu bya ba'i las dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad yongasu
215a6(phal chen): smin par bya ba'i las dang / ma 'ongs pa'i dus thams cad kyi phyi ma'i mtha'i mur thug par yongasu gzung ba'i las dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'gro yang 'jig rten gyi khams gcig nas mi g.yo ba'i
215a7(phal chen): rdzu 'phrul gyi las dang / kha dog mtha' yas pa'i 'od zer dgye ba'i 'od kyi las dang / pad+mo'i snying po la byang chub sems dpa'i gzugs 'khod pa yongasu bstan pa'i 'od zer gyi las dang / mya ngan las 'das pa'i
215a8(phal chen): sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams kyi bstan pa bzung bas/ dkon mchog gsum gyi rigs rgyun mi gcad pa'i las dang / 'jig rten thams cad rgyu ning chos bstan pa dang / sems can gdul ba yang dag par
215b1(phal chen): sgrub pa'i sprul pa'i las dang / nam 'dod pa dang / nam sems bskyed pa na smon lam yongasu rdzogs par sems can la yang dag par ston pa'i byin gyi rlabs kyi laso// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa'

215b3(phal chen): rnams kyi lus te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'odi ltar 'gro ba thams cad byung ba med pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni 'ongs pa medo// 'gro ba thams cad mi dmigs pa med pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni 'ongs
215b4(phal chen): ba'o// 'jig rten thams cad kyis dmigs pa ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni bden pa ma yin pa'o// 'jig ste/ na gyi bden pa rnam par dmigs pa ji lta ba bzhin du byang chub sems
215b5(phal chen): lus ni brdzun pa ma yin pa'o// phyi ma'i mtha'i mur rgyun mi 'a chang pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni rgyun mi zang ba'o// ba dung thams cad kyis mi shigs pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi
215b6(phal chen): lus ni brtan pa'o// bdud kyi rgol ba thams cad kyis mi sgul bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni sra ba'o// bsod nams brgya pa'i mtshan gyis shin tu rnam par dag par snang bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni
215b7(phal chen): mtshan bzang po dang ldan pa'o// chos kyi mtshan nyid med pa'i mthar thug pas/ byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni mtshan nyid med pa'o// 'das pa dang / ma byon pa dang / da ltar byung ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thang
215b8(phal chen): kyi sku dang mnyam pa nyid thob pas byang chub sems dpa'i lus ni kun tu song ba'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnas
216a1(phal chen): de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku mi zad pa/ bla na meng ba 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus kyi las te/ bcu gang zhe na/

216a3(phal chen): las dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad 'gro ba'i lus kyi las dang / sangs rgyas thams cad kyi 'khor gyi dkyil 'khor du 'gro ba'i lus kyi las dang / 'jig rten gyi khams thams cad lag pa gcig
216a4(phal chen): gis kun tu khebs par byed pa'i lus kyi las dang / khor yug dang / rdo rje'i ri thams cad lag pa gcig gis nyug pa'i lus kyi las dang / sangs rgyas kyi zhing thams cad rang gi lus 'jig pa dang / 'byung
216a5(phal chen): ba yongasu ston pa'i lus kyi las dang / sems can gyi kham sa thams cad lus gcig gis yongasu 'dzin pa'i lus kyi las dang / sems can gyi khams thams cad lus med par khong du chung
216a6(phal chen): bas/ zhing yongasu dag pa dang / yongasu rdzogs pa kun tu ston pa'i lus kyi laso// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po de dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi lus kyi las te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems

216a8(phal chen): 'ji ltar nan tan dang ldan pas/ pha rol tu phyin pa'i rang bzhin dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongasu mi gtong bas/ bsdu ba'i dngos po'i rang bzhin dang / sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal gyi phung po rang gi lus kyi
216b1(phal chen): len kyang yongasu mi skyobs/ snying rje chen po'i rang bzhin dang / 'gro ba thams cad yongs skyo pas/ byams pa chen po'i rang bzhin dang / 'gro ba thams cad lte bar 'tsho bas bsod rnams kyi rang bzhin dang / sangs rgyas tha
216b2(phal chen): sku dang gcig tu 'dres pas ye shes kyi rang bzhin dang / skye ba'i skye mched thams cad las 'das pas/ chos kyi rang bzhin dang / thams cad sgo yongasu ston pas/ thams cad kyi rang bzhin dang / rdzu 'phrul dang /

216b4(phal chen): sems dpa' rnams kyi rang bzhin te/ de dag la gnas shing byang chub sems dpa' rnams de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes chen po'i rang bzhin bla na med pa 'thob par 'gyur ba dag go// kye rgyal ba'i sras
216b5(phal chen): bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can thams cad bde bar byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'jam pa'o// sems can
216b6(phal chen): thams cad kyi sems sim par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni sman pa'o// yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du go bar byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni mi rdzun pa'o// rmi lam na yang
216b7(phal chen): log par mi smra bas/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni bden pa'i rjesu 'brang ba'o// brgya byin dang / tshangs pa dang / 'jig rten gyi mgon po thams cad zil gyis gnon pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi pha/ 
216b8(phal chen): ni rgya che ba'o// chos kyi rang bzhin ston pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni zab mo'i dbyangasu sgrog pa'o// chos bstan pa thams cad mi zad pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni snying po dang ldan pa'o// 
217a1(phal chen): sgra ji lta ba bzhin du khong du chud par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni shin tu gsal ba'o// dus dang las dang rnam par smin pa ji lta ba bzhin du yongasu ston pas/ dang
217a2(phal chen): chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni rnam pa tha dad pa'o// bsam pa ji lta ba bzhin du rnam par spyod pa la 'jug par byed pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag ni 'gro ba thams cad la 'gro ba'o// kye rgyal po

217a4(phal chen): chub sems dpa'i ngag de yang las rnam par dag pa bcus yongasasu sbyangs pa yin to// bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i gsung la mos pa yong su dag pa dang / byang chub sems dpa'i tshig sngon
217a5(phal chen): ma thos pa la mngon par mos pa yongasu dag pa dang / 'gro ba tha/ mas cad kyi yid myi 'ong ba'i tshig yongasu spangs pa/ yongasu dag pa dang / sngon gyi mthar dag gi nyes pa bzhi dang bral bas yongasu pa/ 
217a6(phal chen): pa dang / dga' ba dang mos pa chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa mngon du bstod pas yong su dag pa dang / sgra chen pos de bzhin gshegs pa mchod par 'os pa/ yang dag pa ji lta ba bzhin du sangs rgyas kyi yon tan pa

217a8(phal chen): bzhin gshegs pa la mngon par bstod pas yongasu dag pa dang / sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das rnams las mngon sum du chos thos nas// rang gi lus 'bul bas yongasasu dag pa dang // byang chub sem/ 
217b1(phal chen): dba'i chos smra ba thams cad las chos thos nas/ rim gro bya ba'i phyir/ bdag 'bul zhing snying thag pa nas yongasu gtong bas yongasu dag pa ste/ kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag ni las rnam par dag pa
217b2(phal chen): bcu po nga dag gis shin tu sbyangs par 'byung // kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi ngag de ltar yongasu sbyangs pa de yang yong su 'dzin pa bcus yongasu bzung bar 'byung ste/ bcu gang zhe na/ 
217b3(phal chen): 'di ltar lha'i dbang po la sogs pa lha thams cad kyis yongasu bzung bar 'byung ba yin/ klu'i dbang po dang / gnod sbyin gyi dbang po dang / dri za'i dbang po dang / lha ma yin gyi dbang po dang / na mkha' lding gi
217b4(phal chen): dbang po dang / mi 'am ci'i dbang po dang / lto 'phye chen po'i dab nga po dang / tshangs pa'i dbang po la sogs pa tshangs po'i ri su gtogs pa'i lha thams cad kyis yongasu bzung bar 'byung ba yin/ de bzhin gabye

217b6(phal chen): bzung bar 'byung // kye rgyal ba'i sras/ byang chub sems dpa'i ngag de ltar shin tu bzung bar 'byung ba de yang dgos pa bcu yongs grub par byed de/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'di ltar sems can gyi khams mngon pa/

217b8(phal chen): spong bar byeng // bsam pa'i khams spyod par byed // lhag pa'i bsam pa'i khams rnam par 'phel bar bye// chos kyi khams rgyas par byed// mya ngan las 'das pa'i khams yang dag par rtogs par byed/ 
218a1(phal chen): dgos pa bcu po nga dag yongs sgyu'o// kye rgyal ba'i sras bcu po 'di dag ni/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems te/ bcu gang zhe na/ 'gro ba thams cad kyi dge ba'i rtsa ba yang

218a4(phal chen): mongs pa med cing bsam pa dag pa dang ldan pas/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi sems ni nor bu rin po che lta bu'o// chos thams cad la rab tu rno bas/ byang chub sems dpa'
